oṃ mahan me voco bhargo me voco yaśo me vocaḥ stomaṃ me voco bhuktiṃ me vocaḥ sarvaṃ me vocas tan māvatu tan māviśatu tena bhukṣiṣīya
devo devam etu somaḥ somam etv ṛtasya pathā
vihāya dauṣkṛtyam
badvā nāmāsi sṛtiḥ somasaraṇī somaṃ gameyam
pitaro bhūḥ pitaro bhūḥ pitaro bhūḥ
nṛmaṇa ūrdhvabharasaṃ tvordhvabharā dṛśeyam
mṛdā śithirā devānāṃ tīrthaṃ vedir asi mā mā hiṃsīḥ
viṣṇoḥ śiro 'si yaśodhā yaśo mayi dhehi
iṣa ūrja āyuṣe varcase ca
yunajmi te pṛthivīm agninā saha yunajmi vācaṃ saha sūryeṇa yukto vāto 'ntarikṣeṇa te saha yuktās tisro vimṛjaḥ sūryasya
ṛtasya sadane sīdāmi
ṛtapātram asi
vānaspatyo 'si bārhaspatyo 'si prājāpatyo 'si prajāpater mūrdhāsy atyāyupātram asīdam ahaṃ māṃ prāñcaṃ prohāmi tejase brahmavarcasāya
maruto napāto 'pāṃ kṣayāḥ parvatānāṃ kakubhaḥ śyenā ajirā endraṃ vagnunā vahata ghoṣeṇāmīvāṃ cātayadhvaṃ yuktā stha vahata
idam aham amuṃ yajamānaṃ paśuṣv adhyūhāmi paśuṣu ca māṃ brahmavarcase ca
vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa chandasā saṃmṛjantu rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena chandasā saṃmṛjantv ādityās tvā jāgatena chandasā saṃmṛjantu
pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspate prabhur gātrāṇi paryeṣi viśvato 'taptatanūr na tad āmo aśnute śṛtāsa id vahantaḥ saṃ tad āśata
pra śukraitu devī manīṣāsmad rathaḥ sutaṣṭo na vājy āyuṣe me pavasva varcase me pavasva viduḥ pṛthivyā divo janitrācchṛṇvantv āpo 'dhaḥ kṣarantīḥ somehodgāya mām āyuṣe mama brahmavarcasāya yajamānasyarddhyā amuṣya rājyāya
bekurānāmāsi juṣṭā devebhyo namo vāce namo vācaspataye devi vāg yat te vāco madhumat tasmin mā dhāḥ sarasvatyai svāhā
sūryo mā divyābhyo nāṣṭrābhyaḥ pātu vāyur antarikṣābhyo 'gniḥ pārthivābhyaḥ svāhā
yo 'dya saumyo vadho 'ghāyūnām udīrate viṣūkuhasya dhanvanāpa tān varuṇo 'padhamatu
yo ma ātmā yā me prajā ye me paśavas tair ahaṃ mano vācaṃ prasīdāmi
agnes tejasendrasyendriyeṇa sūryasya varcasā bṛhaspatis tvā yunaktu devebhyaḥ prāṇāyāgnir yunaktu tapasā somaṃ yajñāya voḍhave dadhātv indra indriyaṃ satyāḥ kāmā yajamānasya santu
annaṃ kariṣyāmy annaṃ praviṣyāmy annaṃ janayiṣyāmi
annam akaram annam abhūd annam ajījanam

saṃ varcasā payasā saṃ tapobhir aganmahi manasā saṃ śivena saṃ vijñānena manasaś ca satyair yathā vo 'haṃ cārutamaṃ vadānīndro vo dṛśe bhūyāsaṃ sūryaś cakṣuṣe vātaḥ prāṇāya somo gandhāya brahma kṣatrāya
namo gandharvāya viṣvagvādine varcodhā asi varco mayi dhehi
adhvanām adhvapate svasti me 'dyāsmin devayāne pathi bhūyāt
samrāḍ asi kṛśānuḥ
tutho 'si janadhāyo nabho 'si pratakvāsaṃmṛṣṭo 'si havyasūdanaḥ

samudro 'si viśvavyacāḥ
ahir asi budhnyaḥ

pāta māgnayo raudreṇānīkena piṣṭata mā namo vo 'stu mā mā hiṃsiṣṭa
ṛtasya dvārau stho mā mā saṃtāptam
namaḥ sakhibhyaḥ pūrvasadbhyo namo 'parasadbhyaḥ
śyeno nṛcakṣā agneṣṭvā cakṣuṣāvapaśyāmi
indavindrapītasya ta indriyāvato gāyatracchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
ūrdhvaḥ sapta ṛṣīn upatiṣṭhasvendrapīto vācaspate saptartvijo 'bhyucchrayasva juṣasva lokam mārvāg avagāḥ
soma rārandhi no hṛdi pitā no 'si mama tan mā mā hiṃsīḥ
soma gīrbhiṣṭvā vayaṃ vardhayāmo vācovidaḥ sumṛḍīko na āviśa
āpyāyasva sametu te viśvataḥ soma vṛṣṇyaṃ bhavā vājasya saṃgathe
avamais ta ūrvais te kāvyais te pitṛbhir bhakṣitasya madhumato nārāśaṃsasya sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
dīkṣāyai varṇena tapaso rūpeṇa manaso mahimnā vāco vibhūtyā prajāpatis tvā yunaktu prajābhyo 'pānāya

sūryo yunaktu vācā stomaṃ yajñāya voḍhave dadhātv indra indriyaṃ satyāḥ kāmā yajamānasya santu
svaro 'si gayo 'si jagacchandā anu tvā rabhe svasti mā saṃpārayā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam
indavindrapītasya ta indriyāvatastriṣṭupchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
āyur me prāṇe manasi me prāṇa āyupatnyām ṛci yan me mano yamaṃ gataṃ yad vā me aparāgataṃ rājñā somena tad vayaṃ punar asmāsu dadhmasi
yan me yamaṃ vaivasvataṃ mano jagāma dūragās tan ma āvartayā punar jīvātave na martave 'tho ariṣṭatātaye
yenā hyājim ajayad vicakṣya yena śyenaṃ śakunaṃ suparṇaṃ yad āhuś cakṣur aditāv anantaṃ somo nṛcakṣā mayi tad dadhātu
aindraṃ saho 'sarji tasya ta indavindrapītasyendriyāvato 'nuṣṭupchandaso harivataḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
indavindrapītasya ta indriyāvato 'nuṣṭupchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
stutasya stutam asy ūrjasvat payasvad ā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam
iṣṭayajuṣas te deva soma stutastomasya śastokthasya tirohnyasya yo 'śvasanir gosanir bhakṣas tasyopahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
ṛtasya tvā deva stomapade viṣṇor dhāmani vimuñcāmy etat tvaṃ deva stomān avakaram agann aśīmahi vayaṃ pratiṣṭhām
somehānu mehi soma saha sadasa indriyeṇa
subhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmir devānāṃ saṃsad devānāṃ yātur yayā tanvā brahma jinvasi tayā mā jinva tayā mā janaya prakāśaṃ mā kuru
apāṃ puṣpam asy oṣadhīnāṃ rasa indrasya priyatamaṃ haviḥ svāhā
hāriyojanasya te deva someṣṭayajuṣaḥ stutastomasya śastokthasya yo 'śvasanir gosanir bhakṣas tasyopahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
devakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi pitṛkṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi manuṣyakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asy asmatkṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi yad divā ca naktaṃ cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asi yat svapantaś ca jāgrataś cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asi yad vidvāṃsaś cāvidvāṃsaś cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asy enasa enaso 'vayajanam asi

ūrg asy ūrjam mayi dhehi
prāṇa somapīthe me jāgṛhi
dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣaṃ jiṣṇor aśvasya vājinaḥ surabhi no mukhā karat pra na āyūṃṣi tāriṣat

ādityānāṃ patmānvihi namas te 'stu mā mā hiṃsīḥ
vāyoṣṭvā tejasā pratigṛhṇāmi nakṣatrāṇāṃ tvāṃ rūpeṇa pratigṛhṇāmi sūryasya tvā varcasā pratigṛhṇāmi
rathantaram asi vāmadevyam asi bṛhad asi
aṅkā nyaṅkū abhito rathaṃ yau dhvāntaṃ vātāgram abhisaṃcaratau dūre hetir indriyavān patatrī te no 'gnayaḥ paprayaḥ pārayantu
vaiśvānaraḥ pratnathā nākam āruhad divaḥ pṛṣṭhe mandamānaḥ sumanmabhiḥ sa pūrvavaj jantave dhanaṃ samānam ayman paryeti jāgṛviḥ
gidaiṣa te ratha eṣa vām aśvinā ratho 'riṣṭo viśvabheṣajaḥ
kṛśāno savyān āyaccha
dāsano dakṣiṇān avagṛhāṇa
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ pratigṛhṇāmi
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe varuṇāyāśvaṃ tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe rudrāya gāṃ tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe 'gnaye 'jam
agnaye hiraṇyam
agnīṣomābhyām ajāṃ tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
annasyānnapatiḥ prādād anamīvasya śuṣmiṇo namo viśvajanasya kṣāmāya bhuñjati mā mā hiṃsīḥ
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe tvaṣṭre 'viṃ tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
gnās tvā 'kṛntann apaso 'tanvata vayitryo 'vayan
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe bṛhaspataye vāsas tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe uttānāyāṅgirasāyāprāṇat tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe pūṣṇa uṣṭram
vāyave mṛgaṃ tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre

varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe savitre 'śvataraṃ vāśvatarīṃ vā tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
ka idaṃ kasmā adāt kāmaḥ kāmāyādāt kāmo dātā kāmaḥ pratigrahītā kāmaḥ samudram āviśat kāmena tvā pratigṛhṇāmi kāmaitat te
raśmir asi kṣayāya tvā kṣayaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
pretir asi dharmaṇe tvā dharmaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
anvitir asi dive tvā divaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
saṃdhir asy antarikṣāya tvāntarikṣaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
pratidhir asi pṛthivyai tvā pṛthivīṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
viṣṭambho 'si vṛṣṭyai tvā vṛṣṭiṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
prāco 'sy ahne tvāhar jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
anvāsi rātryai tvā rātriṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
uśig asi vasubhyas tvā vasūn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
praketo 'si rudrebhyas tvā rudrān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
sudītir asy ādityebhyas tvādityān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
ojo 'si pitṛbhyas tvā pitṝn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
tantur asi prajābhyas tvā prajā jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
revad asy oṣadhībhyas tvauṣadhīr jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
pṛtanāṣāḍ asi paśubhyas tvā paśūn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
abhijid asi yuktagrāvendrāya tvendraṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
adhipatir asi prāṇāya tvā prāṇān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
dharuṇo 'sy apānāya tvāpānān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
saṃsarpo 'si cakṣuṣe tvā cakṣur jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
vayodhā asi śrotrāya tvā śrotraṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
trivṛd asi trivṛte tvā savṛd asi savṛte tvā pravṛd asi pravṛte tvānuvṛd asy anuvṛte tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
niroho 'si nirohāya tvā saṃroho 'si saṃrohāya tvā praroho 'si prarohāya tvānuroho 'sy anurohāya tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
vasuko 'si vasyaṣṭir asi veṣaśrīr asi savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
ākramo 'sy ākramāya tvā saṃkramo 'si saṃkramāya tvotkramo 'sy utkramāya tvotkrāntir asy utkrāntyai tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa prathamayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa madhyamayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa uttamayodyatī trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ
jyeṣṭho jyaiṣṭhineya stuvīta
agrād agraṃ rohaty abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtir vipāpmanā vartate ya etayā stute nāvagato 'parudhyate nāparuddho 'vagacchati
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhiḥ parivartinī triviṣṭutiḥ
praparīvartam āpnoti ya etayā stute saṃtatā viṣṭutiḥ prāṇo 'pāno vyānas ta ṛcas tān hiṅkāreṇa saṃtanoti
ślakṣṇeva tu vā īśvarā paśūn nirmṛjaḥ saiṣā ca parācota śreyān bhavaty uta yādṛg eva tādṛṅ net tu pāpīyān
tām etāṃ bhāllavaya upāsate tasmāt te pratigṛhṇantaḥ parīvartān na cyavante
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti yā madhyamā sā prathamā yottamā sā madhyamā yā prathamā sottamā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti yottamā sā prathamā yā prathamā sā madhyamā yā madhyamā sottamā kulāyinī trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ
prajākāmo vā paśukāmo vā stuvīta prajā vai kulāyaṃ paśavaḥ kulāyaṃ kulāyam eva bhavati
etām evānujāvarāya kuryād etāsām evāgraṃ pariyatīnāṃ prajānām agraṃ paryeti
etām eva bahubhyo yajamānebhyaḥ kuryāt yat sarvā agriyā bhavanti sarvā madhye sarvā uttamāḥ sarvān evainān samāvadbhājaḥ karoti nānyonyam apaghnate sarve samāvadindriyā bhavanti
varṣukaḥ parjanyo bhavatīme hi lokās tṛcas tān hiṅkāreṇa vyatiṣajati
pāpavasīyasaṃ tu bhavati
adharottaram apāvagato rudhyateva gacchaty aparuddhaḥ pāpīyān śreyāṃsam abhyārohati janatā janatām abhyety anyonyasya prajā ādadate na yathākṣetraṃ kalpante
pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ pañcapañcinī pañcapañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ
pāṅktaḥ puruṣaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavas tayā puruṣaṃ ca paśūṃś cāpnoti vajro vai pañcadaśo yat pañca pañca vyūhati vajram eva tad vyūhati śāntyā eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā pañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhiḥ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ
trīn stomān prativihitā brahmavarcasakāmaḥ stuvīta
pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ tisṛbhis trivṛtaṃ saptabhiḥ saptadaśam
vīryaṃ vai stomā vīryam eva tad ekadhā samūhate brahmavarcasasyāvaruddhyai tejasvī brahmavarcasī bhavati ya etayā stute
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhiḥ pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir udyatī pañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ
etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃllokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir daśasaptā saptadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ
etayā vai devā asurān atyakrāmann ati pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ krāmati ya etayā stute
abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
garbhiṇī viṣṭutiḥ pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya etayā stute
viḍ vai saptadaśas tasyā rājā garbho viśa eva tad rājānaṃ garbhaṃ karoti
nāvagato 'parudhyate nāparuddho 'vagacchati
annaṃ vai saptadaśo yat sapta madhye bhavanti pañca pañcābhito 'nnam eva tan madhyato dhīyate 'naśanāyuko yajamāno bhavaty anaśanāyukāḥ prajāḥ
vairājo vai puruṣaḥ sapta grāmyāḥ paśavo yad daśa pūrvā bhavanti saptottamā yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā saptadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
eṣa eva vyūhaḥ saptaikamadhyā
brahmaṇo vā āyatanaṃ prathamā kṣatrasya madhyamā viśa uttamā yat prathamā bhūyiṣṭhā bhājayati brahmaṇy eva tad ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti brahmaṇa eva tat kṣatraṃ ca viśaṃ cānuge karoti kṣatrasyāsya prakāśo bhavati ya etayā stute
tām etāṃ trikharvā upāsate tasmāt te spardhamānā na vlīyante
saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti parācībhiḥ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ saptāsthitā
bhrātṛvyavāṁ stuvīta yathā saptāsthitena matyena samīkaroty evaṃ pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ prarujati
etām eva bahubhyo yajamānebhyaḥ kuryād yaḥ prathamo hiṅkāraḥ sa prathamāyā yat tāṃ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti tena sā sapta bhajate yat saptaiva madhye sampadyante tena sā sapta bhajate ya uttamo hiṅkāraḥ sa uttamayā yat tāṃ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti tena sā sapta bhajate sarvān evainān samāvadbhājaḥ karoti nānyonyam apaghnate samāvadindriyā bhavanti
tām etām abhipratāriṇa upāsate tasmāt ta ojiṣṭhā svānām
eṣa eva vyūha ubhayaḥ saptaikamadhyā nirmadhyā
ānujāvara stuvītāloko vā eṣa yad ānujāvaro yat sapta prathamāḥ saptottamās tisro madhye tryakṣaraḥ puruṣo lokam evāsmai tan madhyataḥ karoti tasmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhati
etām eva prajākāmāya kuryān madhyato vā eṣa saṃrūḍho yaḥ prajāṃ na vindate lokam evāsmai taṃ madhyataḥ karoti taṃ lokaṃ prajayā ca paśubhiś cānuprajāyate
etām evāparuddharājanyāya kuryād viḍ vai saptadaśas tasyā rājā garbho viśa eva tad rājānaṃ nirhantyapāvagato 'parudhyate 'vagacchaty aparuddhaḥ
etām evābhicaryamāṇāya kuryāt prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim eva madhyataḥ praviśanty astṛtyai
pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhir navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ
catura stomān prativihitā brahmavarcasakāmaḥ stuvīta pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ tisṛbhis trivṛtaṃ navabhis triṇavaṃ svayaṃ saptadaśaḥ sampanno vīryaṃ vai stomā vīryam eva tad ekadhā samūhate brahmavarcasasyāvaruddhyai tejasvī brahmavarcasī bhavati ya etayā stute
tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhiḥ pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir udyatī saptadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ
etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai svargāllokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'bhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa ekayā sa tisṛbhir bhastrāvācīnabilā
yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya kuryād yathāvācīnabilayā bhastrayā pradhūnuyād evaṃ yajamānasya paśūn pradhūnoty apakrāmantī viṣṭutis tayā yajamānasya paśavo 'pakrāmanti pāpīyān bhavati ya etayā stute
saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ saptasaptiny ekaviṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ
sapta grāmyāḥ paśavas tān etayā spṛṇoti sapta śirasi prāṇāḥ prāṇā indriyāṇīndriyāṇy evaitayāpnoti
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitaikaviṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir udyaty ekaviṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ
etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'bhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
saiṣā trivṛtprāyaṇā trivṛdudayanā yat trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati navaitā ekaviṃśasyottamā bhavanti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān eva tad ubhayato dadhāti tasmād ayam ardhabhāg avākprāṇa uttareṣāṃ prāṇānāṃ sarvam āyur eti na purāyuṣaḥ pramīyate ya etayā stute
tām etāṃ karadviṣa upāsate tasmāt te sarvam āyur yanti
navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ pañcabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ pratiṣṭutiḥ
navabhis trivṛtaṃ pratiṣṭauti pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ saptabhiḥ saptadaśaṃ svayam ekaviṃśaḥ sampannaḥ
ya eva stomā yajñaṃ vahanti tān uttame stotre saṃtarpayati yathānaḍuho vāśvān vāśvatarān voḍhuṣaḥ saṃtarpayed evam etad uttame stotre stomān saṃtarpayati tṛpyati prajayā paśubhir ya etayā stute
etām eva purodhākāmāya kuryād brahma vai trivṛt kṣatram ekaviṃśo yat trivṛtaikaviṃśaṃ pratipadyate brahma tat kṣatrasya purastān nidadhāti gacchati purodhāṃ na purodhāyāś cyavate ya etayā stute
tām etāṃ prāvāhaṇya upāsate tasmāt te purodhāyā na cyavanta
navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhis tisṛbhyo hiṃkaroti sa parācībhir navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sūrmy ubhayata ādīptā
brahmavarcasakāmaḥ stuvīta tejo vai trivṛt tryakṣaraḥ puruṣo yat trivṛtāv abhito bhavatas tisro madhye yathā hi hiraṇyaṃ niṣṭaped evam enaṃ trivṛtau niṣṭapatas tejase brahmavarcasāya
apaśavyeva tu vā īśvarā paśūn nirdahaḥ kilāsatvān nūbhayamati hi niṣṭapataḥ
etām evābhiśasyamānāya kuryācchamalaṃ vā etam ṛcchati yam aślīlā vāg ṛcchati yaivainam asāv aślīlaṃ vāg vadati tām asya trivṛtau niṣṭapatas tejasvī bhavati ya etayā stute
navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhiḥ sa ekayā navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhir navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa pañcabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
vajro vai triṇavo vajram eva tad vyūhati śāntyai
pañcabhir vihitaikā paricarā pāṅktāḥ paśavo yajamānaḥ paricarā yat pañcabhir vidadhāty ekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā triṇavasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir udyatī triṇavasya viṣṭutiḥ
etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai svargāllokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'bhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
ekādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa saptabhiḥ sa ekayaikādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa saptabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa saptabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
anto vai trayastriṃśaḥ paramo vai trayastriṃśa stomānāṃ saptabhir vihitaikā paricarā sapta grāmyāḥ paśavo yajamānaḥ paricarā yat saptabhir vidadhāty ekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tad antataḥ paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā trayastriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
ekādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhir ekādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir nedīyaḥsaṃkramā
anto vai trayastriṃśo yathā mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ sṛptvā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmaty evam etan nedīyaḥsaṃkramayā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmati
pañcabhir vihitās tisraḥ paricarāḥ pāṅktāḥ paśava etāvān puruṣo yadātmā prajā jāyā yat pañcabhir vidadhāti tisraḥ paricarā bhavanti yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati paśumān bhavati ya etayā stute
navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhiḥ sa ekayaikādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa saptabhis trayodaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa saptabhiḥ sa tisṛbhir udyatī trayastriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ
etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai svargāllokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'grād agraṃ rohaty abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmādetayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
trayodaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhiḥ sa pañcabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir navabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ pratyavarohiṇī trayastriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ
yathā mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ sṛptvā śākhāyāḥ śākhām ālambham upāvarohed evam etayemaṃ lokam upāvarohati pratiṣṭhityai
trivṛtā praiti trivṛtodeti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇenaiva praiti prāṇam abhyudeti sarvam āyur eti na purāyuṣaḥ pramīyate ya etayā stute
tām etāṃ karadviṣa upāsate tasmāt te sarvam āyur yanti
pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ saptabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
yo vai trayastriṃśam ekaviṃśe pratiṣṭhitaṃ veda pratitiṣṭhati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśaḥ stomānāṃ yad etāḥ sapta trayastriṃśasyottamā bhavanti saptavidhaikaviṃśasya viṣṭutir ekaviṃśa eva tat trayastriṃśaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
aṣṭābhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa catasṛbhiḥ sa ekayāṣṭābhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa catasṛbhir aṣṭābhyo hiṃkaroti sa catasṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
paśavo vai chandomā yad aṣṭābhyo 'ṣṭābhyo hiṃkaroti aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśas tat paśūn āpnoti
catasṛbhir vihitaikā paricarā catuṣpādāḥ paśavo yajamānaḥ paricarā yaccatasṛbhir vidadhātyekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā caturviṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā caturdaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
brahmaṇo vā āyatanaṃ prathamā kṣatrasya madhyamā viśa uttamā yat pañcadaśinyau pūrve bhavataś caturdaśottamā brahmaṇi caiva tat kṣatre caujo vīryaṃ dadhāti brahmaṇe caiva tat kṣatrāya ca viśam anugāṃ karoti kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati ya etayā stute
astomā vā ete yacchandomā ayujo hi stomā yugmanti chandāṃsi yad eṣā yujinī catuścatvāriṃśasya viṣṭutis tenāstomāḥ
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā catuścatvāriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
caturdaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ sa ekayā pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhir nirmadhyā
astīva vā ayaṃ loko 'stīvāsau chidram ivedam antarikṣaṃ yad eṣā nirmadhyā bhavatīmān eva lokān anuprajāyate pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya etayā stute
pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā pañcadaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ caturdaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa daśabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
ājyānāṃ prathamā pṛṣṭhānāṃ dvitīyokthānāṃ tṛtīyā
yājyānāṃ sā hotur yā pṛṣṭhānāṃ sā maitrāvaruṇasya yokthānāṃ sā brāhmaṇācchaṃsino yaiva hotuḥ sācchāvākasya yā pṛṣṭhānāṃ sā hotur yokthānāṃ sā maitrāvaruṇasya yājyānāṃ sā brāhmaṇācchaṃsino yaiva hotuḥ sācchāvākasya yokthānāṃ sā hotur yājyānāṃ sā maitrāvaruṇasya yā pṛṣṭhānāṃ sā brāhmaṇācchaṃsino yaiva hotuḥ sācchāvākasya sarvā ājyeṣu sarvāḥ pṛṣṭheṣu sarvā uktheṣu
paśavo vai samīṣantī yad eṣā sarvāṇi savanāny anusaṃcaraty anusavanam evainaṃ paśubhiḥ samardhayati paśumān bhavati ya etayā stute
ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa dvādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa dvādaśabhiḥ ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa dvādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
anto vā aṣṭācatvāriṃśaḥ paśavaś chandomā yat ṣoḍaśabhyaḥ ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti ṣoḍaśakalāḥ paśavaḥ kalāśas tat paśūn āpnoti
dvādaśabhir vihitaikā paricarā dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaro yajamānaḥ paricarā yad dvādaśabhir vidadhāty ekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tad antatas saṃvatsare paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitāṣṭācatvāriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṃkaroti sa daśabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir nedīyaḥsaṃkramā
anto vā aṣṭācatvāriṃśo yathā mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ sṛptvā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmaty evam etan nedīyaḥsaṃkramayā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmati
daśabhir vihitā tisraḥ paricarā daśākṣarā virāḍ etāvān puruṣo yad ātmā prajā jāyā yad daśabhir vidadhāti tisraḥ paricarā bhavanti yajamānam eva tad virājy annādye 'ntataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayatyannādo bhavati ya etayā stute
gāvaḥ vai etat sattram āsata
tāsām daśasu _ śṛṅgāṇi ajāyanta
tāḥ abruvan arāsma uttiṣṭhāma upaśāḥ naḥ ajñata iti
tāḥ udatiṣṭhan
tāsām tu eva bruvan āsāmahai eva imau dvādaśau māsau saṃ saṃvatsaram āpayāma iti
tāsām dvādaśasu _ śṛṅgāṇi prāvartanta
tāḥ sarvam annādyam āpnuvan
tāḥ etāḥ tūparāḥ
tasmāt tāḥ sarvān dvādaśa māsaḥ prerate
sarvam hi tāḥ annādyam āpnuvan
sarvam annādyam āpnoti yaḥ evam veda
prajāpatiḥ vai idam ekaḥ āsīt
saḥ akāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti
saḥ etam atirātram apaśyat
tam āharat
tena ahorātre prājanayat
yat eṣa atirātraḥ bhavati ahorātre eva prajanayanti
ahorātrayoḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
etāvān vāva saṃvatsaraḥ yat ahaḥ ca rātriḥ ca
ahorātrābhyām eva tat saṃvatsaram āpnuvanti
yat jyotiṣṭomaḥ bhavati yajña mukham tat ṛdhnuvanti yat ukthaḥ yajña kratoḥ anantarayāya yat rātriḥ sarvasya āptaye
saḥ etān stomān apaśyat jyotiḥ gauḥ āyuḥ iti
ime vai lokāḥ ete stomāḥ
ayam eva jyotiḥ
ayam madhyamaḥ gauḥ
asau uttamaḥ āyuḥ
yat ete stomāḥ bhavanti imān eva lokān prajanayanti eṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
saḥ etam tri aham punar prāyuṅkta
tena ṣaṣ ahena ṣaṣ kratūn prājanayat
yat eṣa ṣaṣ ahaḥ bhavati ṛtūn eva prajanayanti ṛtuṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
saḥ etam ṣaṣ aham punar prāyuṅkta
tābhyām dvābhyām ṣaṣ ahābhyām dvādaśa māsaḥ prājanayat
yat etau ṣaṣ ahau bhavataḥ māsān eva prajanayanti māseṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
saḥ etau dvau ṣaṣ ahau punar prāyuṅkta
taiḥ caturbhiḥ ṣaṣ ahaiḥ caturviṃśatim ardha māsān prājanayat
yat ete catvāraḥ ṣaṣ ahāḥ bhavanti ardha māsān eva prajanayanti ardha māseṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
saḥ idam bhuvanam prajanayitvā pṛṣṭhyena ṣaṣ ahena vīryam ātmani adhatta
yat eṣa pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaṣ ahaḥ bhavati vīrye eva antatas pratitiṣṭhanti
tena māsān saṃvatsaram prājanayat
yat eṣa māsaḥ bhavati saṃvatsaram eva prajanayanti saṃvatsare pratitiṣṭhanti
prāyaṇīyam etat ahar bhavati
prāyaṇīyena vai ahnā devāḥ svargam lokam prāyan
yat prāyan tat prāyaṇīyasya prāyaṇīya tvam
tasmāt prāyaṇīyasya ahnaḥ _ bhavitavyam
etat hi svargasya lokasya nediṣṭham
yaḥ etasya ṛtvijaḥ na bhavati hīyate svargāt lokāt
caturviṃśam bhavati
caturviṃśati akṣarā gāyatrī
tejaḥ brahmavarcasam gāyatrī
tejaḥ eva brahmavarcasam ārabhya prayanti
caturviṃśam bhavati
caturviṃśaḥ vai saṃvatsaraḥ
sākṣāt eva saṃvatsaram ārabhante
yāvatyaḥ caturviṃśasya ukthasya stotrīyāḥ tāvatyaḥ saṃvatsarasya rātrayaḥ
stotrīyābhiḥ eva tat saṃvatsaram āpnuvanti
pañcadaśa stotrāṇi bhavanti
pañcadaśa ardha māsasya rātrayaḥ
ardha māsaśas eva tat saṃvatsaram āpnuvanti
pañcadaśa stotrāṇi
pañcadaśa śastrāṇi samāsaḥ
māsaśas eva tat saṃvatsaram āpnuvanti
tat āhuḥ īrmaḥ iva vai eṣā hotrā yat acchāvākyā yat acchāvākam anusaṃtiṣṭhate īśvarā īrmāḥ bhavitoḥ iti
_ uktham sma traikakubham ca udvaṃśīyam ca antatas pratiṣṭhāpye

dvādaśa stotrāṇi agniṣṭomaḥ

tena saṃvatsara saṃmitaḥ

mithunam iva vai eṣā vyāhṛtiḥ
pavasva iti puṃsaḥ rūpam vācaḥ iti striyāḥ

atha u khalu āhuḥ yajñāyajñīyam eva kāryam

abhīvartaḥ brahma sāma bhavati

yat ṛcā punar āyanti asmin loke pratitiṣṭhanti

yat ṛcam anusṛjeyuḥ naśyeyuḥ asmāt lokāt
samānam sāma bhavati anyonyaḥ pragāthaḥ
anyat anyat hi citram adhvānam avagacchan eti
vṛṣā vai eṣa retaḥ dhāḥ yat abhīvartaḥ
pragātheṣu retaḥ dadhat eti

yat parastāt samānaḥ pragāthaḥ bhavati anyat anyat sāma retaḥ eva tat hitam prajanayanti
sāmnā itas pragāthān dugdhe

ye vai adhvānam punar nivartayanti na enam te gacchanti

tad v āhur yat samau bhavata ekavīryau tarhi bhavata iti pañcadaśasaptadaśāv eva kāryau sācīva vai vayaḥ pakṣau kṛtvā patīyaḥ patati
dakṣiṇato bṛhat kāryaṃ dakṣiṇo vā ardha ātmano vīryavattaraḥ
atho khalv āhur uttarata eva kāryaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsino 'rdhāt traiṣṭubhaṃ vai bṛhat traiṣṭubho vai brāhmaṇācchaṃsī traiṣṭubhaḥ pañcadaśastomaḥ
dakṣiṇato rathantaraṃ kāryaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyārdhād gāyatraṃ vai rathantaraṃ gāyatro maitrāvaruṇo gāyatraḥ saptadaśastomaḥ
ekaviṃśaṃ pucchaṃ bhavati
ekaviṃśo vai stomānāṃ pratiṣṭhā tasmād vayaḥ pucchena pratiṣṭhāyotpatati pucchena pratiṣṭhāya niṣīdati
yajñāyajñīyaṃ pucchaṃ kāryaṃ yajñāyajñīyaṃ hy eva mahāvratasya puccham
atho khalv āhur atiśayaṃ vai dvipadāṃ yajñāyajñīyaṃ bhadram kāryaṃ samṛddhyai
vāmadevyaṃ mahāvrataṃ kāryaṃ tasya gāyatraṃ śiro bṛhadrathantare pakṣau yajñāyajñīyaṃ puccham
yo vai mahāvrate sahasraṃ protaṃ veda pra sahasraṃ paśūn āpnoti
tasya prācī dik śiras tac chandobhiḥ sahasram asāv anyataraḥ pakṣaḥ sa nakṣatraiḥ sāhasro 'yam anyataraḥ pakṣaḥ sa oṣadhibhiś ca vanaspatibhiś ca sāhasro 'ntarikṣam ātmā tad vayobhiḥ sāhasraṃ pratīcī dik pucchaṃ tad agnibhiś ca raśmibhiś ca sāhasraṃ pra sahasraṃ paśūn āpnoti ya evaṃ veda
tad āhur apṛṣṭhaṃ vai vāmadevyam anidhanaṃ hīti
anāyatanaṃ vā etat sāma yad anidhanam
rājanaṃ mahāvrataṃ kāryam
etad vai sākṣād annaṃ yad rājanaṃ pañcavidhaṃ bhavati pāṅktaṃ hy annam
hiṅkāravad bhavati tena vāmadevyasya rūpam
nidhanavad bhavati tena pṛṣṭhasya rūpam
aticchandaḥsu pañcanidhanaṃ vāmadevyaṃ brahmasāma kāryam
ati vā eṣānyāni chandāṃsi yad aticchandā aty etad anyāny ahāny ahar yan mahāvratam
brahmasāmnaiva tad anyāny ahāny atimedayati
pañcanidhanaṃ bhavati pāṅktaṃ hy annam
ilāndam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam
etad vai sākṣād annaṃ yad ilāndam irānnaṃ etad irāyām evānnādye 'ntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
samudro vā etac chandaḥ salilaṃ lomaśaṃ samudra iva khalu vai sa bhavati salila iva lomaśa iva yo bhavati
tasmād etāsu kāryaṃ samṛddhyai
vratam iti nidhanaṃ bhavati mahāvratasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate svar iti bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai śakuna iti bhavati śakuna iva vai yajamāno vayo bhūtvā svargaṃ lokam eti
yajñāyajñīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam
yad vā anyā vāṅ nātivadet tad agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ na vai vāg vācam ativadati vāg yajñāyajñīyaṃ vācy evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam
agnir vā idaṃ vaiśvānaro dahannait tasmād devā abibhayus taṃ varaṇaśākhayāvārayanta yad avārayanta tasmād vāravantīyam
tasmād varaṇo bhiṣajya etena hi devā ātmānam atrāyanta
tasmād brāhmaṇo vāraṇena na pibed vaiśvānaraṃ necchamayā iti
paśavo vai vāravantīyaṃ śāntiḥ paśavaḥ śāntād eva tat saṃvvatsarād uttiṣṭhanti
prāṇena purastād āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhante prāṇam eva taj jayanti
apānena paścāt puccham upatiṣṭhante apānam eva taj jayanti
vratapakṣābhyāṃ pakṣāv upatiṣṭhante diśa eva taj jayanti
prajāpater hṛdayenāpikakṣam upatiṣṭhante jyaiṣṭhyam eva taj jayanti
vasiṣṭhasya nihavena cātvālam upatiṣṭhante svargam eva tallokam āptvā śriyaṃ vadante
vaiśvadevyām ṛci bhavati viśvarūpaṃ vai paśūnāṃ rūpaṃ paśūn eva taj jayanti
sattrasyarddhyāgnīdhram upatiṣṭhanta ṛddhāv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
caturakṣaraṇidhanaṃ bhavati catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
ā tamitor nidhanam upayanty āyur eva sarvam āpnuvanti
ślokānuślokābhyāṃ havirdhāne upatiṣṭhante kīrtim eva taj jayanti
yāmena mārjālīyam upatiṣṭhante pitṛlokam eva taj jayanti
āyurṇavastobhābhyāṃ sada upatiṣṭhante brahma caiva tat kṣatraṃ ca jayanti
ṛśyasya sāmnā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhante
indraṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny astuvaṃs tasyarśya ekam aṅgam astutam acāyat tad asyaitenāstaut tenāsya priyaṃ dhāmopāgacchat priyam evāsyaitena dhāmopagacchanti
yat parokṣaṃ nidhanam upeyur hrītamukhaṃ pratimuñceran pratyakṣam upayanti hrītamukham evāpajayanti
āsandīm āruhyodgāyati devasākṣya eva tad upariṣadyaṃ jayati
audumbarī bhavaty ūrg udumbara ūrjam evāvarunddhe
prādeśamātrī bhavaty asya lokasyānuddhānāya
chandobhir ārohati svargam eva tal lokam ārohati
chandobhir upāvarohaty asmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhati
sarveṇātmanā samuddhṛtyodgeyam eṣu lokeṣu ned vyāhito 'sānīti
ekasyāṃ stotrīyāyām astutāyāṃ pādāv upāharati
saha nidhanena pratiṣṭhām upayanty eṣveva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhante
preṅkhām āruhya hotā śaṃsati mahasa eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
yadā vai prajā maha āviśati preṅkhās tarhy ārohanti
phalakam āruhyādhvaryuḥ pratigṛṇāti
kūrcān itare 'dhyāsata ūrdhvā eva tad utkrāmanto yanti
abhigarāpagarau bhavato nindaty enān anyaḥ prānyaḥ śaṃsati ya enān nindati pāpmānam eṣāṃ so 'pahanti yaḥ praśaṃsati yad evaiṣāṃ suṣṭutaṃ suśastaṃ tat so 'bhigṛṇāti
śūdrāryau carmaṇi vyāyacchete tayor āryaṃ varṇam ujjāpayanti
devāś ca vā asurāś cāditye vyāyacchanta taṃ devā abhyajayaṃs tato devā abhavan parāsurā abhavann ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
yadāryaṃ varṇam ujjāpayanty ātmānam eva tad ujjāpayanti
parimaṇḍalaṃ carma bhavaty ādityasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
sarvāsu sraktiṣu dundubhayo vadanti yā vanaspatiṣu vāk tām eva taj jayanti
bhūmidundubhir bhavati yā pṛthivyāṃ vāk tām eva taj jayanti
sarvā vāco vadanti yeṣu lokeṣu vāk tām eva taj jayanti
saṃnaddhāḥ kavacinaḥ pariyantīndriyasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate 'tho mahāvratam eva mahayanti
sarve sahartvijo mahāvratena stuvīran
adhvaryuḥ śirasodgāyan maitrāvaruṇo dakṣiṇena pakṣeṇa brāhmaṇācchaṃsy uttareṇa gṛhapatiḥ pucchenodgātātmanā
tad yady evaṃ kuryur ekaikayā stotrīyayāstutayodgātāram abhisameyuḥ
tisṛbhir udgātātmana udgīyātha yā śirasaḥ stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyād aparābhis tisṛbhir udgīyātha yā dakṣiṇasya pakṣasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyād aparābhis tisṛbhir udgīyātha yottarasya pakṣasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyāt tisṛbhir vaikayā vā stutaṃ syād atha yā pucchasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyāt
ātmany eva tad aṅgāni pratidadhati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
atho khalv āhuḥ katham adhvaryur bahvṛcaḥ sāma gāyed ity udgātaiva sarveṇodgāyet tad eva samṛddhaṃ samṛddhāv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
havirdhāne śirasā stutvā saṃrabdhāḥ pratyañca eyus te dakṣiṇena dhiṣṇyān parītya paścān maitrāvaruṇasya dhiṣṇyasyopaviśya rathantareṇa pañcadaśena stuvīraṃs ta udañcaḥ saṃsarpeyur jaghanena hotur dhiṣṇyaṃ paścād brāhmaṇācchaṃsino dhiṣṇyasyopaviśya bṛhatā saptadaśena stuvīraṃs te yenaiva prasarpeyus tena punar niḥsṛpyottareṇāgnīdhraṃ parītya paścād gārhapatyasyopaviśya pucchenaikaviṃśena stuvīraṃs te yenaiva niḥsarpeyus tena punaḥ prasṛpya yathāyatanam upaviśyāsandīm āruhyodgātātmanodgāyati
taṃ patnyo 'paghāṭilābhir upagāyanty ārtvijyam eva tat patnyaḥ kurvanti saha svargaṃ lokam ayāmeti
kule kule 'nnaṃ kriyate tad yat pṛccheyuḥ kim idaṃ kurvantītīme yajamānā annam atsyantīti brūyuḥ
yo vai dīkṣitānāṃ pāpaṃ kīrtayati tṛtīyam evāṃśaṃ pāpmano haraty annādas tṛtīyaṃ pipīlikās tṛtīyam
parimādbhiś caranti tvak ca vā etal loma ca mahāvratasya yat parimādas tvacaṃ caiva tal loma ca mahāvratasyāptvāvarundhate
vāṇaṃ vitanvanty anto vai vāṇo 'nto mahāvratam antenaiva tad antam abhivādayanti
śatatantrīko bhavati śatāyur vai puruṣaḥ śatavīryaḥ
tam ullikhet prāṇāya tvāpānāya tvā vyānāya tveti prāṇāpānavyānān eva tad āptvāvarundhate
pari kumbhinyo mārjālīyaṃ yantīdaṃ madhv idaṃ madhv iti saghoṣā eva tad vayo bhūtvā saha svargaṃ lokaṃ yanti
devā vai vācaṃ vyabhajanta tasyā yo raso 'tyaricyata tad gaurīvitam abhavad anuṣṭubham anu pariplavate vāg anuṣṭub vāco raso gaurīvitam
yad gaurīvitenānvahaṃ stuvate vācy eva tad vācā rasaṃ dadhati
rasavad vācā vadati ya evaṃ vedeti
dvyudāsaṃ bhavati svargasya vā etau lokasyāvasānadeśau pūrveṇaiva pūrvam ahaḥ saṃsthāpayanty uttareṇottaram ahar abhyativadanti
etad vai yajñasya śvastanaṃ yad gaurīvitaṃ yad gaurīvitam anusṛjeyur aśvastanā aprajasaḥ syuḥ
saṃ vā anyo yajñas tiṣṭhata ity āhur vāg eva na saṃtiṣṭhata iti yad gaurīvitam anvahaṃ bhavati vācam eva tat punaḥ prayuñjate
svarṇidhanam anvahaṃ bhavati
devakṣetraṃ vā ete 'bhyārohanti ye svarṇidhanam upayanti sa u vai sattriṇaḥ sattram upanayed ity āhur ya enān devakṣetram abhyārohayed iti na vai devakṣetra āsīna ārtim ārchati yat svarṇidhanam anvahaṃ bhavati naiva kāṃcanārtim ārchanti
cyavante vā ete 'smāllokād ity āhur ye svarṇidhanam upayantīti yad ṛcā svarūpaṃ yanty asmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhanti yad ekāro 'ntarikṣe yat sāmnāmuṣmin sarveṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti svarṇidhanena tuṣṭuvānāḥ
sujñānaṃ bhavati
devā vai svargaṃ lokaṃ yanto 'jñānād abibhayus ta etat sujñānam apaśyaṃs tena jñātram agacchan yat sujñānam anvahaṃ bhavati jñātram eva gacchanti
ye vai vācam annam ādayanty annādā bhavanti ye vitarṣayanti rūkṣā bhavanti
gaurīvitaṃ śyāvāśvaṃ nihava etāni vai sāmāni vāco 'nnam eteṣāṃ vāg annaṃ yad etāni na cyavante vācam eva tad annam ādayanti tena sarve 'nnādā bhavanti
abhikrāntāpakrāntāni bhavanty abhikrāntāpakrāntaṃ vai vāco rūpam
plavo 'nvahaṃ bhavati
samudraṃ vā ete prasnānti ye saṃvvatsaram upayanti yo vā aplavaḥ samudraṃ prasnāti na sa tata udeti yat plavo bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
ati viśvāni duritā taremeti yad evaiṣāṃ duṣṭutaṃ duḥśastaṃ tad etena taranti
okonidhanaṃ ṣaḍahamukhe bhavati
parāṃ vā ete parāvataṃ gacchanti ye ṣaḍahasyāntaṃ gacchanti yad okonidhanaṃ ṣaḍahamukhe bhavati prajñātyai
yadā vai puruṣaḥ svam oka āgacchati sarvaṃ tarhi prajānāti sarvam asmai divā bhavati
ekāṣṭakāyāṃ dīkṣeran
eṣā vai saṃvvatsarasya patnī yad ekāṣṭakaitasyāṃ vā etāṃ rātriṃ vasati sākṣād eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhya dīkṣante
tasya sā niryā yad apo 'nabhinandanto 'bhyavayanti
vicchinnaṃ vā ete saṃvvatsarasyābhidīkṣante ya ekāṣṭakāyāṃ dīkṣante 'ntanāmānāv ṛtū bhavete
ārtaṃ vā ete saṃvvatsarasyābhidīkṣante ye 'ntanāmānāv ṛtū abhidīkṣante
tasmād ekāṣṭakāyāṃ na dīkṣyam
phālgune dīkṣeran
mukhaṃ vā etat saṃvvatsarasya yat phālguno mukhata eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhya dīkṣante
tasya sā niryā yat saṃmeghe viṣuvān sampadyate
citrāpūrṇamāse dīkṣeran
cakṣur vā etat saṃvvatsarasya yaccitrāpūrṇamāso mukhato vai cakṣur mukhata eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhya dīkṣante tasya na niryāsti
caturahe purastāt paurṇamāsyā dīkṣeran
teṣām ekāṣṭakāyāṃ krayaḥ sampadyate tenaikāṣṭakāṃ na saṃvaṭkurvanti
teṣāṃ pūrvapakṣe sutyā sampadyate pūrvapakṣe māsāḥ saṃtiṣṭhamānā yanti pūrvapakṣa uttiṣṭhanti tān uttiṣṭhataḥ paśava oṣadhayo 'nūttiṣṭhanti tān kalyāṇī vāg abhivadaty arātsur ime sattriṇa iti te rādhnuvanti
ā vā ete saṃvvatsaraṃ pyāyayanti ya utsṛjanti
yathā vai dṛtir ādhmāta evaṃ saṃvvatsaro 'nutsṛṣṭo yan notsṛjeyur amehena pramāyukāḥ syuḥ
prāṇo vai saṃvvatsara udānā māsā yad utsṛjanti prāṇa evodānān dadhati yo dīkṣitaḥ pramīyate yā saṃvvatsarasyānutsṛṣṭasya śuk sā tam ṛcchati
tad āhur utsṛjyā3ṃ notsṛjyā3m iti
yady utsṛjeyur ukthāny utsṛjeyus tad evotsṛṣṭaṃ tad anutsṛṣṭam
atho khalv āhur ekatrikaṃ kāryaṃ tad eva sākṣād utsṛṣṭam abhyutṣuṇvanti
chidro vā eteṣāṃ saṃvvatsara ity āhur ye stomam utsṛjantīti
paśum ālabhante stomam eva tad ālabhante stomo hi paśuḥ
śva utsṛṣṭāḥ sma iti vatsān apākurvanti prātaḥ paśum ālabhante tasya vapayā pracaranti tatas savanīyenāṣṭākapālena tata āgneyenāṣṭākapālena tato dadhnaindreṇa tataś caruṇā vaiśvadevena tat prātaḥsavanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
tataḥ paśupuroḍāśenaikādaśakapālena tataḥ savanīyenaikādaśakapālena tato marutvatīyenaikādaśakapālena tataś caruṇaindreṇa tan mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
paśunā pracaranti tataḥ savanīyena dvādaśakapālena tato vaiśvadevena dvādaśakapālena tataś caruṇāgnimārutena tat tṛtīyaṃ savanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
pṛṣadājyena pracarya patnīs saṃyājayanti
prajāpatiḥ akāmayata bahu syām prajāyeya iti
saḥ etam agniṣṭomam apaśyat
tam āharat
tena imāḥ prajāḥ asṛjata
ekādaśena ca vai satā stotreṇa agniṣṭomasya asṛjata ekādaśena ca māsā saṃvatsarasya
tasmāt prajāḥ daśa māsaḥ garbham bhṛtvā ekādaśam _ prajāyante
tasmāt dvādaśam na abhyatiharanti
dvādaśena hi parigṛhītāḥ
tat yaḥ evam veda _ jātāḥ prajāḥ gṛhṇāti pra a jātāḥ janayati
tāsām parigṛhītānām aśvatarī atyakrāmat
tasyāḥ anuhāya retaḥ ādatta
tat vaḍabāyām nyamāṭ
_ vaḍabā dvi retāḥ tasmāt aśvatarī aprajā
ātta retāḥ hi
tasmāt u a dakṣiṇīyā
ati hi sā yajñam aricyata
atiriktasya dakṣiṇā syāt saloma tvāya
ṣoḍaśinaḥ stotre deyā
atiriktaḥ vai ṣoḍaśī
atirikte eva atiriktām dadāti
saḥ akāmayata yajñam sṛjeya iti
saḥ mukhāt eva trivṛtam asṛjata
tam gāyatrī chandaḥ anvasṛjyata agniḥ devatā brāhmaṇaḥ manuṣyaḥ vasantaḥ ṛtuḥ
tasmāt trivṛt stomānām mukham gāyatrī chandasām agniḥ devatānām brāhmaṇaḥ manuṣyāṇām vasantaḥ ṛtūnām
tasmāt brāhmaṇaḥ mukhena vīryam karoti
mukhāt hi sṛṣṭaḥ
karoti mukhena vīryam yaḥ evam veda
saḥ urasaḥ eva bāhubhyām pañcadaśam asṛjata
tam triṣṭubh chandaḥ anvasṛjyata indraḥ devatā rājanyaḥ manuṣyaḥ grīṣmaḥ ṛtuḥ
tasmāt rājanyasya pañcadaśaḥ stomaḥ triṣṭubh chandaḥ indraḥ devatā grīṣmaḥ ṛtuḥ
tasmāt u bāhu vīryaḥ
bāhubhyām hi sṛṣṭaḥ
karoti bāhubhyām vīryam yaḥ evam veda
saḥ madhyāt eva prajananāt saptadaśam asṛjata
tam jagatī chandaḥ anvasṛjyata viśvāḥ devāḥ devatāḥ vaiśyaḥ manuṣyaḥ varṣāḥ ṛtuḥ
tasmāt vaiśyaḥ adyamānaḥ na kṣīyate
prajananāt hi sṛṣṭaḥ
tasmāt u bahu paśuḥ
vaiśvadevaḥ hi jāgataḥ
varṣā hi asya ṛtuḥ
tasmāt brāhmaṇasya ca rājanyasya ca adyaḥ
adharaḥ hi sṛṣṭaḥ
saḥ pattas eva pratiṣṭhāyāḥ ekaviṃśam asṛjata
tam anuṣṭubh chandaḥ anvasṛjyata na kācana devatā śūdraḥ manuṣyaḥ
tasmāt śūdraḥ _ bahu paśuḥ ayajñiyaḥ
videvaḥ hi
na hi tam kācana devatā anvasṛjyata
tasmāt pādāvanejyam na ativardhate
pattas hi sṛṣṭaḥ
tasmāt ekaviṃśaḥ stomānām pratiṣṭhā
pratiṣṭhāyāḥ hi sṛṣṭaḥ
tasmāt anuṣṭubham chandāṃsi na anuvyūhanti
pāpavasīyasaḥ vidhṛtaye
vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyasaḥ bhavati yaḥ evam veda
yaḥ vai stomān upadeśanavataḥ veda upadeśanavān bhavati
prāṇaḥ vai trivṛt
ardha māsaḥ pañcadaśaḥ
saṃvatsaraḥ saptadaśaḥ
ādityaḥ ekaviṃśaḥ
ete vai stomāḥ upadeśanavantaḥ
upadeśanavān bhavati yaḥ evam veda
vai
ime vai lokāḥ triṇavaḥ
triṇavasya vai brāhmaṇena ime lokāḥ tris punarnavāḥ bhavanti
eṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati yaḥ evam veda
devatāḥ vāva trayastriṃśaḥ aṣṭa vasavaḥ ekādaśa rudrāḥ dvādaśā ādityāḥ prajāpatiḥ ca vaṣaṭkāraḥ ca trayastriṃśau
sa devena yajñena yajate yaḥ evam veda
yaḥ vai adhipatim veda adhipatiḥ bhavati
trayastriṃśaḥ vai stomānām adhipatiḥ puruṣaḥ paśūnām
tasmāt nyāñcaḥ anye paśavaḥ adanti ūrdhvaḥ puruṣaḥ
adhipatiḥ hi saḥ
adhipatiḥ samānānām bhavati yaḥ evam veda
eṣa vāva yajño yad agniṣṭomaḥ
ekasmā anyo yajñaḥ kāmāyāhriyate sarvebhyo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
dvādaśa stotrāṇy agniṣṭomo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nu prajāyante tena paśavyaḥ samṛddhaḥ
dvādaśa stotrāṇi dvādaśa śastrāṇi taccaturviṃśatiś caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nuprajāyante tena paśavyaḥ samṛddhaḥ
agnau stotram agnau śastraṃ pratitiṣṭhati tena brahmavarcasyaḥ
kiṃ jyotiṣṭomasya jyotiṣṭomatvam ity āhur virājaṃ saṃstutaḥ sampadyate virāḍ vai chandasāṃ jyotiḥ
jyotiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
jyeṣṭhayajño vā eṣa yad agniṣṭomaḥ
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmai śraiṣṭhyāya nātiṣṭhanta sa etam agniṣṭomam apaśyat tam āharat tato 'smai prajāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta
tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya ya evaṃ veda
yat tv ity āhur gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ kva tarhi turīyaṃ chando 'nuṣṭub iti
chandasāṃ vā anvavaluptiṃ yajamāno 'nvavalupyate
aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī hiṅkāro navama ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub dvādaśākṣarā jagatī chandobhirevānuṣṭubham āpnoti yajamānasyānavalopāya
yo vā anuṣṭubhaṃ sarvatrāpiṃ savanāny anvāyattāṃ veda sarvatrāsyāpir bhavaty eṣā vā anuṣṭup sarvatrāpiḥ savanāny anvāyattā tad ya evaṃ veda sarvatrāpir bhavati
yad vai rājāno 'dhvānaṃ dhāvayanti ye 'śvānāṃ vīryavattamās tān yuñjate trivṛt pañcadaśa ekaviṃśa ete vai stomānāṃ vīryavattamās tān eva yuṅkte svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
catuṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vai catuṣṭomaḥ pratiṣṭhityai
prajāpatir devebhya ūrjaṃ vyabhajat tata udumbaraḥ samabhavat prājāpatyo vā udumbaraḥ prājāpatya udgātā yad udgātaudumbarīṃ prathamena karmaṇānvārabhate svayaiva tad devatayātmānam ārtvijyāya vṛṇīte
tām ucchrayati dyutānas tvā māruta ucchrayatūd divaṃ stabhānāntarikṣaṃ pṛṇa dṛṃha pṛthivīm
tām anvārabhata āyoṣ ṭvā sadane sādayāmy avataś chāyāyāṃ samudrasya hṛdaya iti
yajño vā āyus tasya tat sadanaṃ kriyate
yajño vā avati tasya sā chāyā kriyate
madhyato vā ātmano hṛdayaṃ tasmān madhye sadasa audumbarī mīyate
namaḥ samudrāya namaḥ samudrasya cakṣuṣa ity āha vāg vai samudro manaḥ samudrasya cakṣus tābhyām eva tan namas karoti
mā mā yūnarvā hāsīd ity āha sāma vai yūnarvā sāmna eva tan namaskaroty ārtvijyaṃ kariṣyan
yo vā evaṃ sāmne namaskṛtya sāmnārtvijyaṃ karoti na sāmno hīyate nainaṃ sāmāpahate
ya enam anuvyāharati sa ārtim ārchati
ūrg asy ūrjodā ūrjaṃ me dehy ūrjaṃ me dhehy annaṃ me dehy annaṃ me dhehi prajāpater vā etad udaraṃ yat sada ūrg udumbaro yad audumbarī madhye sadaso mīyate madhyata eva tat prajābhyo 'nnam ūrjaṃ dadhāti
tasmād yatraiṣā yātayāmā kriyate tat prajā aśanāyavo bhavanti
sāma devānām annaṃ sāmany eva tad devebhyo 'nna ūrjaṃ dadhāti sa eva tad ūrji śritaḥ prajābhya ūrjaṃ vibhajati
udaṅṅ āsīna udgāyaty udīcīṃ tad diśam ūrjā bhājayati pratyaṅṅ āsīnaḥ prastauti pratīcīṃ tad diśam ūrjā bhājayati dakṣiṇāsīnaḥ pratiharati dakṣiṇāṃ tad diśam ūrjā bhājayati prāñco 'nya ṛtvija ārtvijyaṃ kurvanti tasmād eṣā diśāṃ vīryavattamaitāṃ hi bhūyiṣṭhāḥ prīṇanti
brahmavādino vadanti kasmāt satyāt prāñco 'nya ṛtvija ārtvijyaṃ kurvantīti viparikramyodgātāra iti diśām abhīṣṭyai diśām abhiprītyā iti brūyāt tasmāt sarvāsu dikṣv annaṃ vidyate sarvā hy abhīṣṭāḥ prītāḥ
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti so 'śocat tasya śocata ādityo mūrdhno 'sṛjyata so 'sya mūrdhānam udahan sa droṇakalaśo 'bhavat tasmin devāḥ śukram agṛhṇata tāṃ vai sa āyuṣārtim atyajīvat
āyuṣārtim atijīvati ya evaṃ veda
taṃ prohed vānaspatyo 'si bārhaspatyo 'si prājāpatyo 'si prajāpater mūrdhāsy atyāyupātram asīdam ahaṃ māṃ prāñcaṃ prohāmi tejase brahmavarcasāyeti
yad āha vānaspatya iti satyenaivainaṃ tat prohati
yad āha bārhaspatya iti bṛhaspatir vai devānām udgātā tam eva tad yunakti
yad āha prājāpatya iti prājāpatyo hy eṣa devatāyā yad droṇakalaśo yad āha prajāpater mūrdheti prajāpater hy eṣa mūrdhna udahanyata
yad āhātyāyupātram ity ati hy etad anyāni pātrāṇi yad droṇakalaśo devapātraṃ droṇakalaśaḥ
devapātrī bhavati ya evaṃ veda
brāhmaṇaṃ pātre na mīmāṃseta yaṃ brāhmaṇam iva manyate pra devapātram āpnoti na manuṣyapātrāc chidyate
vāg vai devebhyo 'pakrāmat sāpaḥ prāviśat tāṃ devāḥ punar ayācaṃs tā abruvan yat punar dadyāma kiṃ nas tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayadhva ity abruvaṃs tā abruvan yad evāsmāsu manuṣyā apūtaṃ praveśayāṃs tenāsaṃsṛṣṭā asāmeti
śuddhā asmā āpaḥ pūtā bhavanti ya evaṃ veda
sā punarttātyakrāmat sā vanaspatīn prāviśat tān devāḥ punar ayācaṃs tāṃ na punar adadus tān aśapan svena vaḥ kiṣkuṇā vajreṇa vṛścān iti tasmād vanaspatīn svena kiṣkuṇā vajreṇa vṛścanti devaśaptā hi
tāṃ vanaspatayaś caturdhā vācaṃ vinyadadhur dundubhau vīṇāyām akṣe tūṇave tasmād eṣā vadiṣṭhaiṣā valgutamā vāg yā vanaspatīnāṃ devānāṃ hy eṣā vāg āsīt
adho 'dho 'kṣaṃ droṇakalaśaṃ prohanti tasyā vāco 'varuddhyā uparyupary akṣaṃ pavitraṃ prayacchanty ubhayata eva vācaṃ parigṛhṇanti
yasya kāmayetāsuryam asya yajñaṃ kuryāṃ vācaṃ vṛñjīyeti droṇakalaśaṃ prohan bāhubhyām akṣam upaspṛśed asuryam asya yajñaṃ karoti vācaṃ vṛṅkte yo 'sya priyaḥ syād anupaspṛśann akṣaṃ prohet prāṇā vai droṇakalaśaḥ prāṇān evāsya kalpayati
yan nv ity āhur vācānyān ṛtvijo vṛṇate kasmād udgātāro 'vṛtā ārtvijyaṃ kurvantīti
yad droṇakalaśam upasīdanti tenodgātāro vṛtāḥ
prājāpatyā vā udgātāraḥ prājāpatyo droṇakalaśo droṇakalaśa evainām ārtvijyāya vṛṇīte
prāñca upasīdanti prāñco yajñasyāgre karavāmeti
anabhijitā vā eṣodgātṝṇāṃ dig yat prācī yad droṇakalaśaṃ prāñcaṃ prohanti diśo 'bhijityai
yannvityāhur antarāśvaḥ prāsevau yujyate 'ntarā śamye anaḍvān ka udgātṝṇāṃ yoga iti yad droṇakalaśam upasīdanti sa eṣāṃ yogas tasmād yuktair evopasadyaṃ na hy ayukto vahati
grāvnaḥ saṃsādya droṇakalaśam adhyūhanti viḍ vai grāvāṇo 'nnaṃ somo rāṣṭraṃ droṇakalaśo yad grāvasu droṇakalaśam adhyūhanti viśy eva tad rāṣṭram adhyūhanti
yaṃ dviṣyād vimukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvedam aham amum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram amuṣyā viśo 'muṣmād annādyān nirūhāmīti nirūhed viśa evainam annādyān nirūhati
yo 'sya priyaḥ syāt saṃmukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvedam aham āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram amuṣyāṃ viśy amuṣminn annādye 'dhyūhāmīty adhyūhed viśy evainam annādye 'dhyūhati
atho tad ubhayam anādṛtyedam ahaṃ māṃ tejasi brahmavarcase 'dhyūhāmīty adhyūhet tejasy eva brahmavarcasa ātmānam adhyūhati
yaḥ kāmayeta viśā rāṣṭraṃ hanyām iti vyūhya grāvṇo 'dho droṇakalaśaṃ sādayitvopāṃśusavanam upariṣṭād abhinidadhyād idam aham amuyā viśā 'do rāṣṭraṃ hanmīti viśaiva tad rāṣṭraṃ hanti
yo vai daivāni pavitrāṇi veda pūto yajñiyo bhavati chandāṃsi vai daivāni pavitrāṇi tair droṇakalaśaṃ pāvayanti
vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa chandasā punantu rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena chandasā punantv ādityās tvā jāgatena chandasā punantv etāni vai daivāni pavitrāṇi pūto yajñiyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
svarbhānur vā āsura ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat taṃ devā na vyajānaṃs te 'trim upādhāvaṃs tasyātrir bhāsena tamo 'pāhan yat prathamam apāhan sā kṛṣṇāvir abhavad yad dvitīyaṃ sā rajatā yat tṛtīyaṃ sā lohinī yayā varṇam abhyatṛṇat sā śuklāsīt
tasmācchuklaṃ pavitraṃ śukraḥ somaḥ sa śukratvāya
yaṃ dviṣyāt tasyaiteṣāṃ varṇānām api pavitre kuryāt pāpmanaivainaṃ tamasā vidhyati kṛṣṇam iva hi tamo yo 'sya priyaḥ syād āsaktiśuklaṃ kuryāj jyotir vai hiraṇyaṃ jyotir evāsmin dadhāti
tasmād ātreyaṃ candreṇecchanty atrir hi tasya jyotiḥ
abhyatṛṇat pavitraṃ vigṛhṇanti hastakāryam eva tad yajñasya kriyata etad vā udgātṝṇāṃ hastakāryaṃ yat pavitrasya vigrahaṇam
na hastaveṣyān nirṛcchati ya evaṃ veda
yo 'pi na vigṛhṇāti prāṇād enam antaryanti
taṃ brūyād vepamānaḥ prameṣyasa iti vepamāna eva pramīyate
pra śukraitu devī manīṣāsmad rathaḥ sutaṣṭo na vājīty udgātā dhārām anumantrayate
āyuṣe me pavasva varcase me pavasva viduḥ pṛthivyā divo janitrācchṛṇvantv āpo 'dhaḥ kṣarantīḥ somehodgāyety āha mahyaṃ tejase brahmavarcasāyeti
eṣa vai somasyodgītho yat pavate somodgītham eva sāma gāyati
achinnaṃ pāvayanti yajñaṃ caiva prāṇāṃś ca saṃtanvanti saṃtataṃ pāvayanti yajñasya saṃtatyai
bṛhaspatiḥ vai devānām udagāyat
tam rakṣāṃsi ajighāṃsan
saḥ ye eṣām lokānām adhipatayaḥ tān bhāgadheyena upādhāvat
sūryaḥ mām divyābhyaḥ nāṣṭrābhyaḥ pātu vāyuḥ antarikṣābhyaḥ agniḥ pārthivābhyaḥ _ iti juhoti
ete vai eṣām lokānām adhipatayaḥ
tān bhāgadheyena upāsarat
karoti vācā vīryam na sadasyām ārtim ārchati yaḥ evam veda
vāc vai devebhyaḥ apākrāmat
tām devāḥ anvamantrayanta
sā abravīt a bhāgā asmi bhāgadheyam mama astu iti
kaḥ te bhāgadheyam kuryāt iti
udgātāraḥ iti abravīt
udgātāraḥ vai vāce bhāgadheyam kurvanti
tasyai juhuyāt bekurā nāmā asi juṣṭā devebhyaḥ namaḥ vāce namaḥ vācaspataye devi vāc yat te vācaḥ madhumat tasmin mām dhāḥ sarasvatyai _ iti
vāc vai sarasvatī
tām eva tat bhāgadheyena ārabhate
yam dviṣyāt tasya etām āhutim juhuyāt
vācam manasā dhyāyet
vācam eva asya vṛṅkte
bahiṣpavamānam sarpanti
svargam eva tat lokam sarpanti
prakkāṇāḥ iva sarpanti
pratikūlam iva hi itas svargaḥ lokaḥ
tsarantaḥ iva sarpanti
mṛga dharmaḥ vai yajñaḥ yajñasya śāntaye a pratrāsāya
vācam yacchanti
yajñam eva tat yacchanti
yat vyavavadeyuḥ yajñam nirbrūyuḥ
tasmāt na vyavavadyam
pañca ṛtvijaḥ saṃrabdhāḥ sarpanti
pāṅktaḥ yajñaḥ
yāvān yajñaḥ tam eva saṃtanvanti
_ prastotā avacchidyate yajñasya śiraḥ chidyate
brahmane varam dattvā saḥ eva punar vartavyaḥ
chinnam eva tat pratidadhāti
_ udgātā avacchidyate yajñena yajamānaḥ vyṛdhyate
a dakṣiṇaḥ saḥ yajña kratuḥ saṃsthāpyaḥ
atha anyaḥ āhṛtyaḥ
tasmin deyam _ dāsyan syāt
_ pratihartā avacchidyate paśubhiḥ yajamānaḥ vyṛdhyate
paśavaḥ vai pratihartā
sarvavedasam deyam
_ sarvavedasam na dadāti sarva jyānim jīyate
adhvaryuḥ prastaram harati
yajamānaḥ vai prastaraḥ
yajamānam eva tat svargam lokam harati
yajñaḥ vai devebhyaḥ aśvaḥ bhūtvā apākrāmat
tam devāḥ prastareṇa aramayan
tasmāt aśvaḥ prastareṇa saṃmṛjyamānaḥ upāvaramate
_ adhvaryuḥ prastaram harati yajñasya śāntaye a pratrāsāya
prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata
te asmāt sṛṣṭāḥ aśanāyantaḥ apākrāman
tebhyaḥ prastaram annam prāyacchat
enam upāvartanta
tasmāt adhvaryuṇā prastaraḥ īṣat iva vidhūyaḥ
hi tṛṇam paśavaḥ upāvartante
_ enam paśavaḥ āvartante yaḥ evam veda
prastaram āsadya udgāyet haviṣaḥ a skandāya
yajamānam tu svargāt avagṛhṇāti
aṣṭhīvatā upaspṛśatā udgeyam
tena asya haviḥ a skannam bhavati
na yajamānam svargāt lokāt avagṛhṇāti
cātvālam avekṣya bahiṣpavamānam stuvanti
atra vai asau ādityaḥ āsīt
tam devāḥ bahiṣpavamānena svargam lokam aharan
yat cātvālam avekṣya bahiṣpavamānam stuvanti yajamānam eva tat svargam lokam haranti
saḥ tu vai yajñena yajeta iti āhuḥ yasya virājam yajña mukhe dadhyuḥ iti
navabhiḥ stuvanti
hiṅkāraḥ daśamaḥ
daśa akṣarā virāj
virājam eva asya yajña mukhe dadhāti
navabhiḥ stuvanti
nava prāṇāḥ
prāṇaiḥ eva enam samardhayanti
hiṅkāraḥ daśamaḥ
tasmāt nābhiḥ an avatṛṇṇā daśamā prāṇānām
navabhiḥ stuvanti
nava adhvaryuḥ prātaḥsavane grahān gṛhṇāti
tān eva tat pāvayanti
teṣām prāṇān utsṛjanti
prajāpatiḥ vai hiṅkāraḥ
striyaḥ bahiṣpavamānāḥ
yat hiṃkṛtya prastauti mithunam eva asya yajña mukhe dadhāti prajananāya
eṣa vai stomasya yogaḥ yat hiṅkāraḥ
yat hiṃkṛtya prastauti yuktena eva stomena prastauti
eṣa vai sāmnām rasaḥ yat hiṅkāraḥ
yat hiṃkṛtya prastauti rasena eva etāḥ abhyudya prastauti
āraṇyebhyaḥ vai etat paśubhyaḥ stuvanti yat bahiṣpavamānam
eka rūpābhiḥ stuvanti
tasmāt eka rūpāḥ āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ
parāñgbhiḥ stuvanti
tasmāt parāñcaḥ prajāyante parāñcaḥ vitiṣṭhante
a pariśrite stuvanti
tasmāt a parigṛhītāḥ āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ
bahis stuvanti antar anuśaṃsanti
tasmāt grāmam āhṛtaiḥ bhuñjate
grāmyebhyaḥ vai etat paśubhyaḥ stuvanti yat ājyaiḥ nānā rūpaiḥ stuvanti
tasmāt nānā rūpāḥ grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ
punar abhyāvartam stuvanti
tasmāt pra itvaryaḥ pretya punar āyanti
pariśrite stuvanti
tasmāt parigṛhītāḥ grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ
amuṣmai vā etat lokāya stuvanti yat bahiṣpavamānam
sakṛt hiṃkṛtābhiḥ parāñgbhiḥ stuvanti
sakṛt hi itas asau parāñc lokaḥ
asmai vai etat lokāya stuvanti yat ājyaiḥ punar abhyāvartam stuvanti
tasmāt ayam lokaḥ punar punar prajāyate
parāñcaḥ vai eteṣām prāṇāḥ bhavanti iti āhuḥ ye parāñgbhiḥ bahiṣpavamānābhiḥ stuvate iti
āvatīm uttamām gāyet prāṇānām dhṛtaye
cyavante vai ete asmāt lokāt iti āhuḥ ye parāñgbhiḥ bahiṣpavamānābhiḥ stuvate iti
rathantara varṇām uttamām gāyet
iyam vai rathaṃtaram
asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati
_ asmai gāyata nāraḥ iti grāma kāmāya pratipadam kuryāt
naraḥ vai devānām grāmaḥ
grāmam eva asmai upākaḥ
_ vai annam
annam eva asmai upākaḥ
upa u su jātam apturam iti prajā kāmāya pratipadam kuryāt
_ vai prajā
tām jātam iti eva ajījanat
saḥ naḥ pavasva śam gave iti pratipadam kuryāt yām samām mahādevaḥ paśūn hanyāt
saḥ naḥ pavasva śam gave iti catuṣpadāya bheṣajam karoti
śam janāya iti dvipade śam arvante iti eka śaphāya
viṣeṇa vai tām samām oṣadhayaḥ aktāḥ bhavanti yām samām mahādevaḥ paśūn hanti
yat śam rājñ oṣadhībhyaḥ iti āha
oṣadhīḥ eva asmai svadayati
ubhayāḥ asmai svaditāḥ pacyante a kṛṣṭapacyāḥ ca kṛṣṭapacyāḥ ca
pavasva vācaḥ agriyaḥ iti pratipadam kuryāt yam kāmayeta samānānām śreṣṭhaḥ syāt iti
pavasva vācaḥ agriyaḥ iti agram eva enam pariṇayati
śrīḥ vai vācaḥ agram
śriyam eva asmin dadhāti
ete asṛgram indavaḥ iti bahubhyaḥ pratipadam kuryāt
ete iti sarvān eva enān ṛddhaye bhūtyai abhivadati
ete iti vai prajāpatiḥ devān asṛjata asṛgram iti manuṣyān indavaḥ iti pitṝn tiras pavitre iti grahān āśavaḥ iti stotram viśvāni iti śastram _ saubhaga iti anyāḥ prajāḥ
yat ete iti tasmāt yāvantaḥ eva agre devāḥ tāvantaḥ idānīm
sarvām u vṛddhim ārdhnuvan
sthitā iva hi eṣā vyāhṛtiḥ
yat asṛgram iti tasmāt manuṣyāḥ śvas śvas sṛjyante
yat indavaḥ iti indavaḥ iva hi pitaraḥ
manaḥ iva
yām tāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ ṛddhim ārdhnuvan tām ṛdhnuvanti yeṣām evam vidvān etām pratipadam karoti
chandāṃsi vai somam āharan
tam gandharvaḥ viśvāvasuḥ paryamuṣṇāt
tena apaḥ prāviśat
tam devatāḥ anvaicchan
tam viṣṇuḥ apsu paryapaśyat
saḥ vyakāṅkṣat ayam nu na iti
tam padā prāsphurat
tasmāt pṛthak indavaḥ asṛjyanta
saḥ devatābhyaḥ abhitas tiṣṭhatībhyaḥ ete asṛgram indavaḥ iti prābravīt
bahiṣpavamānena vai yajñaḥ sṛjyate
yat ete asṛgram indavaḥ iti prastauti yajñam eva tat sṛṣṭam devatābhyaḥ prāha
vyṛddham vai etat a paśavyam yat prātaḥsavanam an iḍam hi
yat iḍām naḥ saṃyatam iti āha prātaḥsavanam eva tat iḍāvat paśumat karoti
davidyutatyā rucā iti vrātāya pratipadam kuryāt
davidyutatyā rucā iti vai gāyatryāḥ rūpam pariṣṭobhatyā iti triṣṭubhaḥ kṛpā iti anuṣṭubhaḥ somāḥ śukrāḥ gavāśiraḥ iti jagatyāḥ
sarveṣām vai eṣā chandasām rūpam
svena eva enān tat rūpeṇa samardhayati
vṛddhāḥ vai ete indriyeṇa vīryeṇa yat vrātaḥ
indriyam vīryam chandāṃsi
indriyeṇa eva enān vīryeṇa samardhayati
agne āyūṃṣi pavase iti pratipadam kuryāt yeṣām dīkṣitānām pramīyate
a pūtāḥ iva vai ete yeṣām dīkṣitānām pramīyate
_ eṣā āgnipāvamānī pratipad bhavati agniḥ eva enān niṣṭapati pavamānaḥ punāti
yat āyūṃṣi iti āha ye eva jīvanti teṣu āyuḥ dadhāti
_ naḥ mitrāvaruṇā iti jyok āmayāvine pratipadam kuryāt
apakrāntau vai etasya prāṇa apānau yasya jyok āmayati
prāṇa apānau mitrāvaruṇau
prāṇa apānau eva asmin dadhāti
apaghnan pavate mṛdhaḥ _ somaḥ arāvṇaḥ iti anṛtam abhiśasyamānāya pratipadam kuryāt
arāvāṇaḥ vai ete ye anṛtam abhiśaṃsanti
tān eva asmāt apahanti
gacchan indrasya niṣkṛtam iti pūtam eva enam yajñiyam indrasya niṣkṛtam gamayati
vṛṣā pavasva dhārayā iti rājanyāya pratipadam kuryāt
vṛṣā vai rājanyaḥ
vṛṣāṇam eva enam karoti
marutvate ca matsaraḥ iti
marutaḥ vai devānām viśaḥ
viśam eva asmai _ niyunakti
an apakrāmukā asmāt viś bhavati
viśvāni dadhānaḥ ojasā iti ojasā eva asmai vīryeṇa viśam purastāt parigṛhṇāti
an apakrāmukā asmāt viś bhavati
pavasva indo vṛṣā āsutaḥ iti pratipadam kuryāt yaḥ kāmayeta jane me ṛdhyeta iti
kṛdhi naḥ yaśasaḥ jane iti janatāyām eva asmai ṛdhyate
yuvam hi sthaḥ svar patī iti dvābhyām pratipadam kuryāt
samāvat bhājau eva enau yajñasya karoti
ubhau yajña yaśasena arpayati
pra asya dhārāḥ akṣaran iti vṛṣṭi kāmāya pratipadam kuryāt
pra asya dhārāḥ akṣaran iti divaḥ vṛṣṭim cyāvayati vṛṣṇaḥ sutasya ojasaḥ iti antarikṣāt
devāṁ _ prabhūṣataḥ iti asmin loke pratiṣṭhāpayati
ojasā vai etat vīryeṇa pradīyate yat a prattam bhavati
yat vṛṣṇaḥ sutasya ojasaḥ iti āha ojasā eva asmai vīryeṇa divaḥ vṛṣṭim prayacchati
tayā pavasva dhārayā yayā gāvaḥ iha āgaman janyāsaḥ upa naḥ gṛham iti pratipadam kuryāt yaḥ kāmayeta _ mām janyāḥ gāvaḥ nameyuḥ vindeta mama janyāḥ gāḥ rāṣṭram iti
yat eṣā pratipad bhavati _ enam janyāḥ gāvaḥ namanti vindate asya janyāḥ gāḥ rāṣṭram
ime vai lokā gāyatraṃ tryāvṛd geyaṃ trayo hīme lokā yat tryāvṛd gāyaty ebhir evainaṃ lokaiḥ saṃmimīte
dvir avanardeddhiṃkuryāt tṛtīyam
yat trir avanardaty ati tad gāyatraṃ recayati
yo vai gāyatreṇāpratihṛtenodgāyaty apratiṣṭhāno bhavati hiṅkāro vai gāyatrasya pratihāraḥ
sa manasā dhyeyaḥ pratihṛtena gāyatreṇodgāyati pratitiṣṭhati
yo vā ebhyo lokebhyo gāyatraṃ gāyati naibhyo lokebhya āvṛścyata ima enaṃ lokā ūrjābhisaṃvasate
mandram ivāgra ādadītātha tārataram atha tāratamaṃ tad ebhyo lokebhyo 'gāsīt
aniruktaṃ geyam etad vai gāyatrasya krūraṃ yan niruktaṃ yad aniruktaṃ gāyati krūram evāsya parivṛṇakti
prāṇo gāyatraṃ na vyavānyāt prāṇasyāvicchedāya yadi vyavāniti pramāyuko bhavati yadi na vyavāniti sarvam āyur eti
yadi vyavānyān madhya ṛco vyavānyāt prāṇo vai gāyatraṃ prāṇaḥ svaraḥ prāṇam eva tan madhyata ātman dadhāti sa sarvam āyur eti
iḍāṃ paśukāmāya nidhanaṃ kuryāt svaḥ svargakāmāya yaśo brahmavarcasakāmāyāyur āmayāvine haṃsīty abhicarate
ete vai gāyatrasya dohāḥ
brahmavarcasī paśumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
prajāpatir devebhya ātmānaṃ yajñaṃ kṛtvā prāyacchat te 'nyonyasmā agrāya nātiṣṭhanta tān abravīd ājim asminn iteti ta ājim āyan yad ājim āyaṃs tad ājyānām ājyatvam
sa indro 'ved agnir vā idam agra ujjeṣyatīti so 'bravīd yataro nāv idam agra ujjayāt tan nau saheti so 'gnir agra udajayad atha mitrāvaruṇāv athendro 'thaiṣaikā hotrānujjitāsīt sa indro 'gnim abravīd yat sahāvocāvahīyaṃ nau tad iti saiṣaindrāgny adhyardham agne stotram adhyardham indrasya
catvāri santi ṣaḍdevatyāni
ṣaḍdhā vihito yajño yāvān yajñas tam evārabhate
sarvāṇi svārāṇy ājyāni taj jāmi nānādevatyaiḥ stuvanty ajāmitāyai
grāmyebhyo vā etat paśubhyaḥ stuvanti yad ājyaiḥ punarabhyāvartaṃ stuvanti tasmāt parāñcaḥ prājyante pratyañcaḥ prajāyante tasmād u pretya punar āyanti
etāvatā vāva mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ pupuve
tribhiś ca chandobhiḥ pañcabhiś ca sāmabhiḥ
yan mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvanti mādhyandinam eva tat savanaṃ pāvayanti
etāvanti vāva sarvāṇi sāmāni yāvanti mādhyandine pavamāne
gāyatraṃ nidhanavad anidhanam aiḍam
yan mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvanti sarvair eva tat sāmabhiḥ stuvanti
ātmā vai yajñasya pavamāno mukhaṃ gāyatrī prāṇo gāyatraṃ yad gāyatryāṃ gāyatreṇa stuvanti mukhata eva tat prāṇān dadhati
prāṇāpānā vā etāni chandāṃsi prāṇo gāyatrī vyāno bṛhaty apānas triṣṭub yad etaiś chandobhiḥ stuvanti prāṇāpānānām avicchedāya
ime vai lokā etāni chandāṃsy ayam eva gāyatry ayaṃ madhyamo bṛhaty asāv uttamas triṣṭub yad etaiś chandobhiḥ saṃhitaiḥ stuvanty eṣāṃ lokānām avicchedāya
yad anyac chando 'ntarā vyaveyād imāṃl lokān vicchindyāt
gāyatreṇa stutvā nidhanavatā stuvantīyaṃ vai gāyatry asyām eva tad āyatanaṃ kriyate
yad anidhanenāgre stuyur anāyatano yajamānaḥ syāt
nidhanavatā stuvanti vīryaṃ vai gāyatrī vīryaṃ nidhanaṃ vīryeṇaiva tad vīryaṃ samardhayati
aiḍena bṛhatīm ārabhante
paśavo vā iḍā paśavo bṛhatī paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti
bṛhatyāṃ bhūyiṣṭhāni sāmāni bhavanti
tatrāpi triṇidhanam
abaliṣṭha iva vā ayaṃ madhyamo lokas tasyaiva tad āyatanaṃ kriyate
triṇidhanaṃ bhavati trīṇi savanānāṃ chidrāṇi tāni tenāpidhīyante
triṇidhanaṃ bhavati traya ime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
triṇidhanaṃ bhavaty etena vai mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yat triṇidhanaṃ yat triṇidhanaṃ na syād apratiṣṭhitaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ syāt
dvyakṣarāṇi nidhanāni bhavanti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati
anidhanam antato bhavati svargasya lokasyānatipādāya
yan nidhanavat syād yajamānaṃ svargāl lokān nirhanyāt
svāraṃ bhavati
svareṇa vai devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ prayacchati
gāyatraṃ purastād bhavati svāram antataḥ
prāṇo vai gāyatraṃ prāṇaḥ svaraḥ prāṇān eva tad ubhayato dadhāti tasmād ubhayataḥprāṇāḥ paśavaḥ
yad gāyatraṃ purastād bhavati svāram antataḥ prāṇair eva praity apāne pratitiṣṭhati
etad vai yajñasya svargyaṃ yan mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ mādhyandinasya pavamānaḥ pavamānasya bṛhatī yad bṛhatyāḥ stotre dakṣiṇā dīyante svargasyaiva tal lokasyāyatane dīyante
devā vai chandāṃsyabruvan yuṣmābhiḥ svargyaṃ lokam ayāmeti te gāyatrīṃ prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvaṃs triṣṭubhaṃ prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvañ jagatīṃ prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvann anuṣṭubhaṃ prāyuñjata tayālpakādiva vyāpnuvaṃs ta āsāṃ diśāṃ rasān pravṛhya catvāry akṣarāṇy upādadhuḥ sā bṛhaty abhavat tayemāṃl lokān vyāpnuvan
bṛhatī maryā yayemāṃl lokān vyāpāmeti tad bṛhatyā bṛhattvam
paśūn vā asyāntān upādadhuḥ paśavo vai bṛhatī yad bṛhatyāḥ stotre dakṣiṇā dīyante sva eva tad āyatane dīyante
yannvity āhur anyāni chandāṃsi varṣīyāṃsi kasmād bṛhaty ucyata eṣā hīmāṃl lokān vyāpnon nānyacchandaḥ kiṃcana yāni sapta caturuttarāṇi chandāṃsi tāni bṛhatīm abhisaṃpadyante tasmād bṛhaty ucyate
yannvity āhur gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ kasmād bṛhatyā madhyandine stuvantīti
bahiṣpavamānena vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃ lokam aharan sa nādhriyata taṃ bṛhatyā madhyandine 'stabhnuvaṃs tasmād bṛhatyā madhyandinaṃ stuvanty ādityaṃ hy eṣā madhyandine dādhāra
yair u kaiśca chandobhir madhyandine stuvanti tāni triṣṭubham abhisaṃpadyante tasmāt triṣṭubho na yanti mādhyandināt savanāt
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa śocann amahīyamāno 'tiṣṭhat sa etad āmahīyavam apaśyat tenemāḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā amahīyanta yad amahīyanta tasmād āmahīyavam
tā asmāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tāsāṃ divi sad bhūmy ādada iti prāṇān ādatta tā enaṃ prāṇeṣv ātteṣu punar upāvartanta tābhya ugraṃ śarma mahi śrava iti punaḥ prāṇān prāyacchat tā asmād ud evāyodhaṃs tāsāṃ stauṣa iti manyūn avāśṛṇāt tato vai tasmai tāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta
tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya ya evaṃ veda
prajānāṃ ca vā eṣā sṛṣṭiḥ pāpavasīyasaś ca vidhṛtir yad āmahīyavam
vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃ veda
devā vai yaśaskāmāḥ sattram āsatāgnir indro vāyur makhas te 'bruvan yan no yaśa ṛchāt tan naḥ sahāsad iti teṣāṃ makhaṃ yaśa ārchat tad ādāyāpākrāmat tad asya prāsahāditsanta taṃ paryayatanta svadhanuḥ pratiṣṭabhyātiṣṭhat tasya dhanurārtnir ūrdhvā patitvā śiro 'chinat sa pravargyo 'bhavad yajño vai makho yat pravargyaṃ pravṛñjanti yajñasyaiva tacchiraḥ pratidadhati
tad devā yaśo vyabhajanta tasyāgnī rauravaṃ prābṛhata
tad vai sa paśuvīryaṃ prābṛhata paśavo vai rauravam
paśumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
agnir vai rūras tasyaitad rauravam
asurā vai devān paryayatanta tata etāv agnī rūrau viṣvañcau stobhāv apaśyat tābhyām enān pratyauṣat te pratyuṣyamāṇā aravanta yad aravanta tasmād rauravam
athendro yaudhājayaṃ prābṛhata tad vai sa vajraṃ prābṛhata vajro vai yaudhājayam
vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati ya evaṃ veda
indro vai yudhājit tasyaitad yaudhājayam
yudhā maryā ajaiṣmeti tasmād yaudhājayam
atha vāyur auśanaṃ prābṛhata
tad vai sa prāṇavīryaṃ prābṛhata prāṇā vā auśanam
sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃ veda
vāyur vā uśanās tasyaitad auśanam
uśanā vai kāvyo 'surāṇāṃ purohita āsīt taṃ devāḥ kāmadughābhir upāmantrayanta tasmā etāny auśanāni prāyacchan kāmadughā vā auśanāni
kāmadughā enam upatiṣṭhante ya evaṃ veda
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa tūṣṇīṃ manasādhyāyat tasya yan manasy āsīt tad bṛhat samabhavat
sa ādīdhīta garbho vai me 'yam antarhitas taṃ vācā prajanayā iti
sa vācaṃ vyasṛjata sā vāg rathantaram anvapadyata
rathaṃ maryāḥ kṣepṇātārīd iti tad rathantarasya rathantaratvam
tato bṛhad anuprājāyata bṛhan maryā idaṃ sa jyog antarabhūd iti tad bṛhato bṛhattvam
yathā vai putro jyeṣṭha evaṃ bṛhat prajāpateḥ
jyeṣṭhabrāhmaṇaṃ vā etat
pra jyaiṣṭhyam āpnoti ya evaṃ veda
yan nv ity āhur bṛhat pūrvaṃ prajāpatau samabhavat kasmād rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśa iti
bṛhad eva pūrvaṃ samabhavad rathantaraṃ tu pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭyāsṛjata tasmāt pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśe
tayoḥ samānaṃ nidhanam āsīt tasmin nātiṣṭhetāṃ ta ājim aitāṃ tayor has iti bṛhat prāṇam udajayad as iti rathantaram apānam abhisamaveṣṭata
prāṇāpānau vai bṛhadrathantare jyog āmayāvina ubhe kuryād apakrāntau vā etasya prāṇāpānau yasya jyog āmayati prāṇāpānāv evāsmin dadhāti
yan nv ity āhur ubhe bṛhadrathantare bahirṇidhane kasmād bṛhad bahirṇidhanāni bhajate 'ntarṇidhanāni rathantaram iti
prāṇo bṛhat tasmād bahirṇidhanāni bhajate bahir hi prāṇo 'pāno rathantaraṃ tasmād antarṇidhanāni bhajate 'ntar hy apānaḥ
mahāvṛkṣau vai bṛhadrathantare nidhane na samarpye
yad vai mahāvṛkṣau samṛcchete bahu tatra vibhagnaṃ prabhagnaṃ śete
airaṃ vai bṛhad aiḍaṃ rathantaraṃ mano vai bṛhad vāg rathantaraṃ sāma vai bṛhad ṛg rathantaraṃ prāṇo vai bṛhad apāno rathantaram asau vai loko bṛhad ayaṃ rathantaram etāni manasānvīkṣyodgāyet kﾱptābhyām evābhyām udgāyati
paśavo vai bṛhadrathantare aṣṭākṣareṇa prathamāyā ṛcaḥ prastauty aṣṭāśaphāṃs tat paśūn avarunddhe
dvyakṣareṇottarayor ṛcoḥ prastauti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati
pañcākṣareṇa rathantarasya pratiharati pāṅktāṃs tat paśūn avarunddhe
caturakṣareṇa bṛhataḥ pratiharati catuṣpadas tat paśūn avarunddhe
na vai bṛhan na rathantaram ekaṃ chando 'yacchat tataḥ kakubhāv uttare upādadhus tasmād bṛhatī prathamā kakubhāv uttare tasmād bṛhadrathantare ekarcena kurvanti na hi te ekaṃ chando 'yacchat
nava bṛhato rohān rohati nava prāṇāḥ prāṇān evāvarunddhe
trīn prathamāyāṃ rohati bhūtaṃ bhavad bhaviṣyat tān evāvarunddhe trīn madhyamāyāṃ rohaty ātmānaṃ prajāṃ paśūṃs tān evāvarunddhe trīn uttamāyāṃ rohati traya ime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
sarvān kāmān avarunddhe ya evaṃ vidvān bṛhato rohān rohati
vajreṇa vā etat prastotodgātāram abhipravartayati yad rathantaraṃ prastauti samudram antardhāyodgāyed vāg ity ādeyaṃ vāg vai samudraḥ samudram evāntardadhāty ahiṃsāyai
balavad geyaṃ vajram evaṃ pravṛttaṃ pratyudgṛhṇāti
valvalā kurvatā geyam abhilobhayateva vajram evābhilobhayati
kṣipraṃ geyaṃ svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
devaratho vai rathantaram akṣareṇākṣareṇa pratiṣṭhāpayatodgeyam areṇāreṇa hi rathaḥ pratitiṣṭhati
yo vai devaratham ananvālabhyātiṣṭhaty avāsmāt padyata iyaṃ vai devaratha imām ālabhyodgāyen nāsmād avapadyate
īśvaraṃ vai rathantaram udgātuś cakṣuḥ pramathitoḥ prastūyamāne saṃmīlet svar dṛśaṃ prativīkṣeta nainaṃ cakṣur jahāti
prajananaṃ vai rathantaraṃ yat tasthuṣa ity āhāsthāyukodgātur vāg bhavaty api prajananaṃ hanty asthuṣa iti vaktavyaṃ susthuṣa iti vā sthāyukodgātur vāg bhavati na prajananam api hanti
pṛṣṭhāni vā asṛjyanta tair devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs teṣāṃ rathantaraṃ mahimnā nāśaknod utpatat
tasya vaśiṣṭho mahimno vinidhāya tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam ait tān saṃbhṛtyodgāyet
yas te goṣu mahimā yas te apsu rathe vā te stanayitnau ya u te yas te agnau mahimā tena saṃbhava rathantara draviṇavan na edhi
apo vā ṛtvyam ārchat tāsāṃ vāyuḥ pṛṣṭhe vyavartata tato vasu vāmaṃ samabhavat tasmin mitrāvaruṇau paryapaśyatāṃ tāv abrūtāṃ vāmaṃ maryā idaṃ deveṣv ājanīti tasmād vāmadevyam
tat parigṛhṇantāv abrūtām idam avidāvedaṃ nau mābhyarttiḍhvam iti tat prajāpatir abravīn mad vā etaddhy ajani mama vā etad iti tad agnir abravīn māṃ vā etad anvajani mama vā etad iti tad indro 'bravīcchreṣṭhasthā vā etad ahaṃ vaḥ śreṣṭho 'smi mama vā etad iti tad viśve devā abruvann asmaddevatyaṃ vā etad yad adbhyo 'dhi samabhūd asmākaṃ vā etad iti tat prajāpatir abravīt sarveṣāṃ na idam astu sarva idam upajīvāmeti tat pṛṣṭheṣu nyadadhuḥ sarvadevatyaṃ vai vāmadevyam
yat kavatīṣu tena prājāpatyaṃ ko hi prajāpatir yad aniruktāsu tena prājāpatyam anirukto hi prajāpatiḥ
yad gāyatrīṣu tenāgneyaṃ gāyatracchandā hy agniḥ
yat pṛṣṭheṣu nyadadhus tenaindraṃ sarvāṇi hi pṛṣṭhānīndrasya niṣkevalyāni
yan maitrāvaruṇo 'nuśaṃsati tena maitrāvaruṇam
yad bahudevatyam uttamaṃ padaṃ tena vaiśvadevaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
prajāpatir vā etāṃ gāyatrīṃ yonim apaśyat sa ādīdhītāsmād yoneḥ pṛṣṭhāni sṛjā iti
sa rathantaram asṛjata tad rathasya ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
sa bṛhad asṛjata tat stanayitnor ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata sa vairūpam asṛjata tad vātasya ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
sa vairājam asṛjata tad agner ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
sa śakvarīr asṛjata tad apāṃ ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
sa revatīr asṛjata tad gavāṃ ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
etair vā etāni saha ghoṣair asṛjyanta
sarve 'smin ghoṣāḥ sarvāḥ puṇyā vāco vadanti ya evaṃ veda
pitā vai vāmadevyaṃ putrāḥ pṛṣṭhāni
etasmād vā etāni yoner asṛjyanta
tasmāt pṛṣṭhānāṃ stotraṃ vāmadevyenānuṣṭuvanti śāntyai
yaddhi putro 'śāntaṃ carati pitā tacchamayati
ayaṃ vai loko madhyamo vāmadevyam etasmād vā imau lokau viṣvañcāv asṛjyetāṃ bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ ca
yad rathantareṇa stuvanti ye rathantarāḥ paśavo 'ntarīkṣaṃ ta upaśrayanti yad bṛhatā stuvanti ye bārhatāḥ paśavo 'ntarīkṣaṃ ta upaśrayanti te vāmadevyasya stotreṇāvaruddhāḥ
dhruva āsīno vāmadevyenodgāyet paśūnām upavṛttyai
upainaṃ paśava āvartante ya evaṃ veda
antarikṣaṃ vai vāmadevyam adhūnvatevodgeyam adhūtam ivāntarikṣaṃ paśavo vai vāmadevyam ahiṃsatevodgeyaṃ paśūnām ahiṃsāyai
katham iva vāmadevyaṃ geyam ity āhuḥ
yathāṅkulī putrān saṃdaśyāsaṃbhindantī harati yathā vāto 'psu śanair vāti
svadhūr vāmadevyaṃ geyam
yo vai svadhūr vāmadevyaṃ gāyati svadhūr bhavati
yāty asyānyo niyānena nānyasya niyānena yāti
na bṛhato na rathantarasyānurūpaṃ geyaṃ svenaivāyatanena geyam āyatanavān bhavati
devā vai paśūn vyabhajanta te rudram antarāyaṃs tān vāmadevyasya stotra upekṣate
aniruktaṃ geyam
yan nirāha rudrāya paśūn apidadhāti rudras tāṃ samāṃ paśūn ghātuko bhavati
revatīṣu vāmadevyena paśukāmaḥ stuvīta
āpo vai revatyaḥ paśavo vāmadevyam adbhya evāsmai paśūn prajanayati
anavarttiḥ paśuto bhavati prajā svasya mīliteva bhavati
kavatībhyo hy eti prajāpateḥ
imau vai lokau sahāstāṃ tau viyantāv abrūtāṃ vivāhaṃ vivahāvahai saha nāv astv iti
tayor ayam amuṣmai śyaitaṃ prāyacchan naudhasam asāv asmai
tata enayor nidhane viparyakrāmatāṃ devavivāho vai śyaitanaudhase
pravasīyāṃsaṃ vivāham āpnoti ya evaṃ veda
ito vā ime lokā ūrdhvāḥ kalpamānā yanty amuto 'rvāñcaḥ kalpamānā āyanti
yad rathantareṇa stuvantīmaṃ lokaṃ tena yunakty antarikṣaṃ vāmadevyena naudhasenāmuṃ yad bṛhatā stuvanty amuṃ lokaṃ tena yunakty antarikṣaṃ vāmadevyena śyaitenemam
kﾱptān imāṃllokān upāste ya evaṃ veda
bṛhadrathantare vai śyaitanaudhase yad rathantarāya naudhasaṃ prati prayuñjanti bṛhad evāsmai tat prati prayuñjanti bṛhaddhy etat parokṣaṃ yan naudhasaṃ yad bṛhate śyaitaṃ prati prayuñjanti rathantaram evāsmai tat prati prayuñjanti rathantaraṃ hy etat parokṣaṃ yacchyaitam
ubhābhyāṃ bṛhadrathantarābhyāṃ stute ya evaṃ veda
devā vai brahma vyabhajanta tānnodhāḥ kākṣīvata āgacchat te 'bruvann ṛṣir na āgaṃstasmai brahma dadāmeti tasmā etat sāma prāyacchaṃs tasmān naudhasaṃ brahma vai naudhasam
brahmavarcasakāma etena stuvīta brahmavarcasī bhavati
athaitacchyaitam
prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān etena sāmnābhivyāharat te 'smā atiṣṭhanta te śetyā abhavan yacchetyā abhavaṃs tasmācchyaitaṃ paśavo vai śyaitam
paśukāma etena stuvīta paśumān bhavati
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā aśocaṃs tāḥ śyaitena huṃmā ity abhyajighrat tato vai tāḥ samaidhanta samedhante tāṃ samāṃ prajā yatraivaṃ vidvāñchyaitenodgāyati
eṣa vai yajamānasya prajāpatir yad udgātā yacchyaitena hiṃkaroti prajāpatir eva bhūtvā prajā abhijighrati
vasunidhanaṃ bhavati paśavo vai vasu paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanam abhicaraṇīyasya brahmasāma kuryād abhinidhanaṃ mādhyandine pavamāne
deveṣur vā eṣā yad vaṣaṭkāro 'bhīti vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharad abhītyevāsmai vajraṃ prahṛtya deveṣvā vaṣaṭkāreṇa vidhyati
traikakubhaṃ paśukāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt tvam aṅga praśaṃsiṣa ity etāsu
indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat teṣāṃ traya udaśiṣyanta rāyovājo bṛhadgiriḥ pṛthuraśmis te 'bruvan ko naḥ putrān bhariṣyatīty aham itīndro 'bravīt tāṃs trikakub adhinidhāyācarat sa etat sāmāpaśyad yat trikakub apaśyat tasmāt traikakubham
sa ātmānam eva punar upādhāvat tvam aṅga praśaṃsiṣo devaḥ śaviṣṭha martyaṃ na tvad anyo maghavann asti ca marḍitendra bravīmi te vaca iti sa etena ca pragāthenaitena sāmnā sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata tān ebhyaḥ prāyacchat te pratyatiṣṭhan
yaḥ paśukāmaḥ syād yaḥ pratiṣṭhākāma etasmin pragātha etena sāmnā stuvīta pra sahasraṃ paśūn āpnoti pratitiṣṭhati
trivīryaṃ vā etat sāma trīndriyam aindrya ṛca aindraṃ sāmaindreti nidhanam indriya eva vīrye pratitiṣṭhati
traiśokaṃ jyogāmayāvine brahmasāma kuryāt
ime vai lokāḥ sahāsaṃs te 'śocaṃs teṣām indra etena sāmnā śucam apāhan yat trayāṇāṃ śocatām apāhaṃs tasmāt traiśokam
yām asmād apāhan sā puṃścalīṃ prāviśad yām antarikṣāt sā klībaṃ yām amuṣmāt sainasvinam
tasmāt teṣāṃ nāśaitavyā ya eṣām āśāmeti tasmā eva śuco 'pabhajate
śucā vā eṣa viddho yasya jyog āmayati yat traiśokaṃ brahmasāma bhavati śucam evāsmād apahanti
diveti nidhanam upayanti vyuṣṭir vai divā vy evāsmai vāsayati
āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ pratiṣṭhākāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt
kaṇvo vā etat sāmarte nidhanam apaśyat sa na pratyatiṣṭhat sa vṛṣadaṃśasyāṣ iti kṣuvata upāśṛṇot sa tad eva nidhanam apaśyat tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhad yad etat sāma bhavati pratiṣṭhityai
vasiṣṭhasya janitraṃ prajākāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt
vasiṣṭho vā etat putrahataḥ sāmāpaśyat sa prajayā paśubhiḥ prājāyata yad etat sāma bhavati prajātyai
ātharvaṇaṃ lokakāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt
atharvāṇo vā etal lokakāmāḥ sāmāpaśyaṃs tenāmartyaṃ lokam apaśyan yad etat sāma bhavati svargasya lokasya prajātyai
abhīvartaṃ bhrātṛvyavate brahmasāma kuryāt
abhīvartena vai devā asurān abhyavartanta yad abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavati bhrātṛvyasyābhivṛtyai
śrāyantīyaṃ yajñavibhraṣṭāya brahmasāma kuryāt
prajāpatir uṣasam adhyait svāṃ duhitaraṃ tasya retaḥ parāpatat tad asyāṃ nyaṣicyata tad aśrīṇād idaṃ me mā duṣad iti tat sad akarot paśūn eva
yacchrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati śrīṇāti caivainaṃ sac ca karoti
devāś ca vā asurāś caiṣu lokeṣv aspardhanta te devāḥ prajāpatim upādhāvaṃs tebhya etat sāma prāyacchad etenainān kālayiṣyadhvam iti tenainān ebhyo lokebhyo 'kālayanta yad akālayanta tasmāt kāleyam
ebhyo vai lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ kālayate ya evaṃ veda
stomo vai deveṣu taro nāmāsīd yajño 'sureṣu vidadvasus te devās tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti stomena yajñam asurāṇām avṛñjata
stomena yajñaṃ bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
sādhyā vai nāma devā āsaṃs te 'vacchidya tṛtīyasavanaṃ mādhyandinena savanena saha svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tad devāḥ kāleyena samatanvan yat kāleyaṃ bhavati tṛtīyasavanasya saṃtatyai
vidadvasu vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti prastauti tṛtīyasavanam eva tad abhyativadati
sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇi kāleyaṃ yat padaprastāvaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ yad bṛhato rohān rohati tena bārhataṃ yat stobhavān pratihāras tena bārhataṃ yad dravadiḍaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
sādhyā vai nāma devā āsaṃs te sarveṇa yajñena saha svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs te devāśchandāṃsyabruvan somam āharateti te jagatīṃ prāhiṇvan sā trīṇy akṣarāṇi hitvaikākṣarā bhūtvāgacchat triṣṭubhaṃ prāhiṇvan saikam akṣaraṃ hitvā tryakṣarā bhūtvāgacchad gāyatrīṃ prāhiṇvaṃś caturakṣarāṇi vai tarhi chandāṃsy āsan sā tāni cākṣarāṇi haranty āgacchad aṣṭākṣarā bhūtvā trīṇi ca savanāni hastābhyāṃ dve savane dantair daṃṣṭvā tṛtīyasavanaṃ tasmād dve aṃśumatī savane dhītaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ dantair hi tad daṃṣṭvā dhayanty aharat tasya ye hriyamāṇasyāṃśavaḥ parāpataṃs te pūtīkā abhavan yāni puṣpāṇy avāśīyanta tāny arjunāni yat prāprothat te praprothās tasmāt tṛtīyasavana āśiram avanayanti yam eva taṃ gāvaḥ somam adanti tasya taṃ rasam avanayanti sasomatvāya
te triṣṭubjagatyau gāyatrīm abrūtām upa tvāyāveti sābravīt kiṃ me tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayasa ity abrūtāṃ sābravīn mama sarvaṃ prātaḥsavanam aham uttare savane praṇayānīti tasmād gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ gāyatry uttare savane praṇayati
tāṃ triṣṭup tribhir akṣarair upait saikādaśākṣarā bhūtvā prājāyata tāṃ jagaty ekenākṣareṇopait sā dvādaśākṣarā bhūtvā prājāyata
tasmād āhur gāyatrī vāva sarvāṇi chandāṃsi gāyatrī hy etān poṣān puṣyanty aid iti
indras tṛtīyasavanād bībhatsamāna udakrāmat tad devāḥ svādiṣṭhayeti asvadayan madiṣṭhayeti madvad akurvan pavasva soma dhārayety apāvayann indrāya pātave suta iti tato vai tad indra upāvartata yat svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayeti prastauti tṛtīyasavanasya sendratvāya
svādiṣṭhā vai deveṣu paśava āsan madiṣṭhā asureṣu te devāḥ svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayeti paśūn asurāṇām avṛñjata
paśūn bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
tāsu saṃhitam
sādhyā vai nāma devā āsaṃs te 'vacchidya tṛtīyasavanaṃ mādhyandinena savanena saha svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tad devāḥ saṃhitena samadadhur yat samadadhus tasmāt saṃhitam
kāleyaṃ purastād bhavati saṃhitam upariṣṭād etābhyāṃ hi tṛtīyasavanaṃ saṃtāyate
sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇi saṃhitaṃ yat padaprastāvaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ yad bṛhato rohān rohati tena bārhataṃ yat padanidhanaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
uṣṇikkakubhāv ete bhavataḥ
uṣṇikkakubbhyāṃ vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat kakubhi parākramatoṣṇihā prāharat tasmāt kakubho madhyamaṃ padaṃ bhūyiṣṭhākṣaraṃ parākramaṇaṃ hi tad abhisamauhat tasmād uṣṇiha uttamaṃ padaṃ bhūyiṣṭhākṣaraṃ puro gurur iva hi vajraḥ
vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati ya evaṃ veda
nāsike vā ete yajñasya yad uṣṇikkakubhau tasmāt samānaṃ chandaḥ satī nānā yajñaṃ vahatas tasmāt samānāyā nāsikāyāḥ satyā nānā prāṇāv uccarataḥ
prāṇā vā uṣṇikkakubhau tasmāt tābhyāṃ na vaṣaṭkurvanti yad vaṣaṭkuryuḥ prāṇān agnau pradadhyuḥ
tāsu saphaṃ vipham iva vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ tṛtīyasavanasya saphatvāyāthaitat pauṣkalam etena vai prajāpatiḥ puṣkalān paśūn asṛjata teṣu rūpam adadhād yad etat sāma bhavati paśuṣv eva rūpaṃ dadhāti
purojitī vo andhasa iti padyā cākṣaryā ca virājau bhavataḥ padyayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyann akṣaryayā ṛṣayo nu prājānan yad ete padyā cākṣaryā ca virājau bhavataḥ svargasya lokasya prajñātyai
tāsu śyāvāśvam
śyāvāśvam ārvanānasaṃ sattram āsīnaṃ dhanvodavahan sa etat sāmāpaśyat tena vṛṣṭim asṛjata tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhat tato gātum avindata gātuvid vā etat sāma
vindate gātuṃ pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
indras tṛtīyasavanād bībhatsamāna udakrāmat taṃ devāḥ śyāvāśvenaihāyi ehiyety anvāhvayan sa upāvartata yad etat sāma bhavati tṛtīyasavanasya sendratvāya
athaitad āndhīgavam andhīgur vā etat paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai madhye nidhanam aiḍaṃ bhavaty etena vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yan madhye nidhanam aiḍaṃ na syād apratiṣṭhitaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ syāt
daśākṣaraṃ madhyato nidhanam upayanti daśākṣarā virāḍ virājy eva pratitiṣṭhati
abhi priyāṇi pavata iti kāvaṃ prājāpatyaṃ sāma
prajā vai priyāṇi paśavaḥ priyāṇi prajāyām eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
raśmī vā etau yajñasya yad auśanakāve devakośo vā eṣa yajñam abhisamubjito yad ete antato bhavato yajñasyāriṣṭyai
devāḥ vai brahma vyabhajanta
tasya yaḥ rasaḥ atyaricyata tat yajñāyajñīyam abhavat
brahmanaḥ vai eṣa rasaḥ yat yajñāyajñīyam
yat yajñāyajñīyena stuvanti brahmanaḥ eva rase yajñam pratiṣṭhāpayati
yoniḥ vai yajñāyajñīyam
etasmāt vai yoneḥ prajāpatiḥ yajñam asṛjata
tasmāt yajñāyajñīyam
tasmāt vai etena purā brāhmaṇāḥ bahiṣpavamānam astoṣata yoneḥ yajñam pratanavāmahai iti
yajñam tatas stuvanti yonau yajñam pratiṣṭhāpayanti
asureṣu vai sarvaḥ yajñaḥ āsīt
te devāḥ yajñāyajñīyam apaśyan
