teṣām yajñā yajñā vaḥ agnaye iti agnihotram avṛñjata girā girā ca dakṣase iti darśa pūrṇamāsau _ _ vayam amṛtam jātavedasam iti cāturmāsyāṇi priyam mitram na śaṃsiṣam iti saumyam adhvaram
yajñā vaḥ agnaye girā ca dakṣase _ vayam amṛtam jātavedasam priyam mitram na śaṃsiṣam iti vai tarhi chandāṃsi āsan
te devāḥ abhyārambham abhinivartyam chandobhiḥ yajñam asurāṇām avṛñjata
chandobhiḥ yajñam bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte yaḥ evam veda
etat ha sma vai āha kūśāmbaḥ svāyavaḥ brahmā lātavyaḥ kam svid adya śiśumārī yajña pathe apyastā gariṣyati
eṣā vai śiśumārī yajña pathe apyastā yajñāyajñīyam
yat girā girā iti āha ātmānam tat udgātā girati
airam kṛtvā udgeyam
irāyām yajñam pratiṣṭhāpayati
a pramāyukaḥ udgātā bhavati
vaiśvānare vai etat udgātā ātmānam pradadhāti yat _ _ vayam iti āha
praprīm vayam iti vaktavyam
vaiśvānaram eva parikrāmati
yaḥ vai nihnuvānam chandaḥ upaiti pāpīyāḥ ujjagivāḥ bhavati
etat vai nihnuvānam chandaḥ yat na śaṃsiṣam iti
nu śaṃsiṣam iti vaktavyam su śaṃsiṣam iti _
na nihnuvānam chandaḥ upaiti
vasīyāḥ ujjagivāḥ bhavati
yasya vai yajñāḥ vāc antāḥ bhavanti vācaḥ chidreṇa sravanti
ete vai yajñāḥ vāc antāḥ ye yajñāyajñīya antāḥ
etat vācaḥ chidram yat anṛtam
yat agniṣṭoma yājī anṛtam āha tat _ asya yajñaḥ sravati
akṣareṇa antatas pratiṣṭhāpyam
akṣareṇa eva yajñasya chidram apidadhāti
virājaḥ vai etat rūpam yat akṣaram
virāji eva antatas pratitiṣṭhati
ito vai prātar ūrdhvāṇi chandāṃsi yujyante 'muto 'vāñci yajñāyajñīyasya stotre yujyante yajñā vo agnaye girā ca dakṣasa iti dvādaśākṣaraṃ pra vayam amṛtaṃ jātavedasam ity ekādaśākṣaraṃ priyaṃ mitraṃ na śaṃsiṣam ity aṣṭākṣaram
anuṣṭubham uttamāṃ sampādayatīyaṃ vā anuṣṭub asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati
vāg vā anuṣṭub vācy eva pratitiṣṭhati jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vā anuṣṭub jyaiṣṭhya eva pratitiṣṭhati
katham iva yajñāyajñīyaṃ geyam ity āhur yathānaḍvān prasrāvayamāṇa ittham iva cettham iva ceti
vaiśvānaraṃ vā etad udgātānu prasīdann etīty āhur yad yajñāyajñīyasyarcaṃ saṃpratyāheti parikrāmatevodgeyaṃ vaiśvānaram eva parikrāmati
vaiśvānare vā etad adhvaryuḥ sadasyān abhisṛjati yad yajñāyajñīyasya stotram upāvartayati prāvṛtenodgeyaṃ vaiśvānareṇānabhidāhāya
na ha tu vai pitaraḥ prāvṛtaṃ jānanti yajñāyajñīyasya vai stotre pitaro yathāyathaṃ jijñāsanta ākarṇābhyāṃ prāvṛtyaṃ tad eva prāvṛtaṃ tad aprāvṛtaṃ jānanti pitaro na vaiśvānaro hinasti
apaḥ paścāt patnya upasṛjanti vaiśvānaram eva tacchamayanty āpo hi śāntiḥ
atho reta eva tat siñcanty āpo hi retaḥ
dakṣiṇān ūrūn abhiṣiñcanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyate
mahad iva pratyūhyaṃ mana evāsya tajjanayanti
udgātrā patnīḥ saṃkhyāpayanti retodheyāya
hiṅkāraṃ prati saṃkhyāpayanti hiṃkṛtāddhi reto dhīyate
ā tṛtīyāyāḥ saṃkhyāpayanti trivṛddhi retaḥ
devā vā agniṣṭomam abhijityokthāni nāśaknuvann abhijetuṃ te 'gnim abruvaṃs tvayā mukhenedaṃ jayāmeti so 'bravīt kiṃ me tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayasa ity abruvan so 'bravīn maddevatyāsūkthāni praṇayān iti
tasmād āgneyīṣūkthāni praṇayanti
tasmād u gāyatrīṣu gāyatracchandā hy agniḥ
te 'gniṃ mukhaṃ kṛtvā sākam aśvenābhyakrāman yat sākam aśvenābhyakrāmaṃs tasmāt sākamaśvam
tasmāt sākamaśvenokthāni praṇayanty etena hi tāny agre 'bhyajayan
sa indro 'bravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti varuṇas taṃ varuṇo 'nvatiṣṭhad indra āharat tasmād aindrāvaruṇam anuśasyate
sa evābravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti bṛhaspatis taṃ bṛhaspatir anvatiṣṭhad indra āharat tasmād aindrābārhaspatyam anuśasyate sa evābravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti viṣṇus taṃ viṣṇur anvatiṣṭhad indra āharat tasmād aindrāvaiṣṇavam anuśasyate
paśūn vā ebhyas tān āharat paśavo vā ukthāni paśukāma ukthena stuvīta paśumān bhavati
bṛhatā vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat tasya tejaḥ parāpatat tat saubharam abhavat
jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yad rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ rathantaraṃ saṃdhir nāntarā bṛhatā stuvantīti yat saubhareṇa stuvanti bṛhataiva tad antarā stuvanti bṛhato hy etat tejo yat saubharam
yadi bṛhatsāmātirātraḥ syāt saubharam ukthānāṃ brahmasāma kāryaṃ bṛhad eva tat tejasā samardhayati
yadi rathantarasāmnā saubharaṃ kuryād ajāmitāyai
devānāṃ vai svargaṃ lokaṃ yatāṃ diśo 'vlīyanta tāḥ saubhareṇo ity udastabhnuvaṃs tato vai tā adṛṃhanta tataḥ pratyatiṣṭhaṃs tataḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prājānan yaḥ svargakāmaḥ syād yaḥ pratiṣṭhākāmaḥ saubhareṇa stuvīta pra svargaṃ lokaṃ jānāti pratitiṣṭhati
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā āśanāyaṃs tābhyaḥ saubhareṇorg ity annaṃ prāyacchat tato vai tāḥ samaidhanta
samedhante tāṃ samāṃ prajā yatraivaṃ vidvān saubhareṇodgāyati
tā abruvan subhṛtaṃ no 'bhārṣīr iti tasmāt saubharam
vṛṣṭiṃ vā abhyastāṃ prāyacchad annam eva
yo vṛṣṭikāmaḥ syād yo 'nnādyakāmo yaḥ svargakāmaḥ saubhareṇa stuvīta
hīṣiti vṛṣṭikāmāya nidhanaṃ kuryād ūrg ity annādyakāmāyo iti svargakāmāya
sarve vai kāmāḥ saubharaṃ sarveṣv eva kāmeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
athaitan nārmedham
nṛmedhasam āṅgirasaṃ sattram āsīnaṃ śvabhir abhyāhvayan so 'gnim upādhāvat pāhi no agna ekayeti taṃ vaiśvānaraḥ paryudatiṣṭhat tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhat tato gātum avindata
gātuvid vā etat sāma vindate gātuṃ pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
naiva hy etad ahno rūpaṃ na rātrer yad ukthānām
kakup prathamāthoṣṇig atha purauṣṇig anuṣṭup tenānuṣṭubho na yanty acchāvākasāmnaḥ
hārivarṇaṃ bhavati
asurā vā eṣu lokeṣv āsaṃs tān devā hariśriyam ity asmāl lokāt prāṇudanta virājasīty antarikṣād divo diva ity amuṣmāt
tad ya evaṃ vedaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudyemāṃl lokān abhyārohati
harivarṇo vā etat paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai
aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ yato rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tāny etena harivarṇo 'pāhanta yad etat sāma bhavati rakṣasām apahatyai
pṛṣṭhāni vā asṛjyanta teṣāṃ yat tejo raso 'tyaricyata tad devāḥ samabharaṃs tad udvaṃśīyam abhavat
sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ tejo yad udvaṃśīyaṃ tasmād vā etat purā sajātāya nākran pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyai
eṣa hy eva pṛṣṭhais tuṣṭuvāno ya udvaṃśīyena stuvate
sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇy udvaṃśīyam
gāyanti tvā gāyatriṇa eti rathantarasya rūpam eti hi rathantaram
ādir bṛhata ūrdhvam iva hi bṛhat
pariṣṭobho vairūpasya pariṣṭubhaṃ hi vairūpam
anutodo vairājasyānutunnaṃ hi vairājam
ardheḍā śakvarīṇām atisvāro revatīnām
ardheḍayā vai devā asurān avahatyātisvāreṇa svargaṃ lokam ārohan
tad ya evaṃ vedārdheḍayaiva bhrātṛvyam avahatyātisvāreṇa svargaṃ lokam ārohati
ardheḍayā vai pūrvaṃ yajñaṃ saṃsthāpayanty atisvāreṇottaram ārabhante
upainam uttaro yajño namati ya evaṃ veda
pāṅktaṃ vā etat sāma pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavo yajña eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
āṣṭādaṃṣṭre ṛddhikāmāya kuryāt
aṣṭādaṃṣṭro vairūpo 'putro 'prajā ajīryat sa imāṃ lokān vicichidivān amanyata sa ete jarasi sāmanī apaśyat tayor aprayogād abibhet so 'bravīd ṛdhnavad yobhe sāmabhyāṃ stavātā iti
ṛṣer vā etat prāśodbhūtaṃ yad āṣṭādaṃṣṭre bhavata ṛddhyā eva
gāyatrīṣu brahmavarcasakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur gāyatryāṃ brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā gāyatrī saṃpadyate
tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarunddhe
gāyatrīṣu paśukāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣoṣṇik saṃpadyate
paśavo vā uṣṇik paśūn evāvarunddhe
gāyatrīṣu puruṣakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyuḥ kakubhi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā kakup saṃpadyate
puruṣo vai kakup puruṣān evāvarunddhe
virāṭsv annādyakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā virāṭ saṃpadyate
annaṃ virāḍ annādyam evāvarunddhe
akṣarapaṅktiṣu jyaiṣṭhyakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣānuṣṭup saṃpadyate
jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vā anuṣṭub jyaiṣṭhyam evāvarunddhe
devā vā ukthāny abhijitya rātriṃ nāśaknuvann abhijetuṃ te 'surān rātriṃ tamaḥ praviṣṭān nānuvyapaśyaṃs ta etam anuṣṭupśirasaṃ pragātham apaśyan virājaṃ jyotiḥ tān virājā jyotiṣānupaśyanto 'nuṣṭubhā vajreṇa rātrer nirāghnan
yad eṣo 'nuṣṭupśirāḥ pragātho bhavati virājaiva jyotiṣānupaśyann anuṣṭubhā vajreṇa rātrer bhrātṛvyaṃ nirhanti
tān samantaṃ paryāyaṃ prāṇudanta yat paryāyaṃ prāṇudanta tat paryāyāṇāṃ paryāyatvam
prathamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanti prathamasya paryāyasya
prathamair hi padaiḥ punar ādāya prathamarātrāt prāṇudanta
pāntam ā vo andhasa iti prastauti
ahar vai pāntam andho rātrir ahnaiva tad rātrim ārabhante
tāsu vaitahavyam
vītahavyaḥ śrāyaso jyog niruddha etat sāmāpaśyat so 'vagacchat pratyatiṣṭhad avagacchati pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
tama iva vā ete praviśanti ye rātrim upayanti yad oko nidhanaṃ rātrer mukhe bhavati prajñātyai
yadā vai puruṣaḥ svam oka āgacchati sarvaṃ tarhi prajānāti sarvam asmai divā bhavati
te madhyamaṃ paryāyam aśrayanta teṣām aurdhvasadmanena vācam avṛñjata
vācaṃ bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
triṇidhanaṃ bhavati
yathā vā ahno mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ triṇidhanāyatanam evam eṣa rātrer madhyamaḥ paryāyas triṇidhanāyatanaḥ salokatvāya
madhyamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanti madhyamasya paryāyasya madhyamair hi padaiḥ punar ādāyaṃ madhyamarātrāt prāṇudanta
ta uttamaṃ paryāyam aśrayanta teṣāṃ ghṛtaścyunnidhanena paśūn avṛñjata paśavo vai ghṛtaścyutaḥ
paśūn bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
uttamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanty uttamasya paryāyasyottamair hi padaiḥ punar ādāyam uttamarātrāt prāṇudanta
tān sandhinābhipalāyanta
tān āśvinenāsaṃhāyyam agamayan
asaṃhāyyaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ gamayati ya evaṃ veda
eṣā vā agniṣṭomasya saṃmā yad rātriḥ
dvādaśa stotrāṇy agniṣṭomo dvādaśa stotrāṇi rātriḥ
eṣā vā ukthasya saṃmā yad rātriḥ
trīṇy ukthāni tridevatyaḥ sandhiḥ
yathā vā ahna ukthāny evam eṣa rātreḥ sandhir nānārūpāṇy ahna ukthāni nānārūpā ete tṛcā bhavanti
rathantaraṃ pratiṣṭhākāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt
iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati
bṛhat svargakāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt
svargo loko bṛhat svarga eva loke pratitiṣṭhati
vāravantīyaṃ vā vāmadevyaṃ vā śrudhyaṃ vaiteṣām ekaṃ paśukāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt
paśavo vā etāni sāmāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
āśvinaṃ hotānuśaṃsati
prajāpatir vā etat sahasram asṛjata tad devebhyaḥ prāyacchat tasmin na samarādhayaṃs te sūryaṃ kāṣṭhāṃ kṛtvājim adhāvan
teṣām aśvinau prathamāv adhāvatāṃ tāv anvavadan saha no 'stviti tāvabrūtāṃ kiṃ tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayethe ityabruvaṃs tāvabrūtām asmaddevatyam idam uktham ucyātā iti tasmād āśvinam ucyate
sarvāḥ khalu devatāḥ śasyante
kṣipraṃ śasyam ājim iva hy ete dhāvanty ā sūryasyodetoḥ śaṃset sūryaṃ hi kāṣṭhām akurvata
pāntam ā vo andhasa iti vaitahavyam anyakṣetraṃ vā ete prayanti ye rātrim upayanti yad okonidhanaṃ rātrer mukhe bhavaty okaso 'pracyāvāya
pra va indrāya mādanam iti gaurīvitam
brahma yad devā vyakurvata tato yad atyaricyata tad gaurīvitam abhavat
atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atiriktam etat stotraṃ yad rātrir atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti
vayam u tvā tad id arthā iti kāṇvam
etena vai kaṇva indrasya sāṃvidyam agacchad indrasyaivaitena sāṃvidyaṃ gacchati
indrāya madvane sutam iti śrautakakṣaṃ kṣatrasāma pra kṣatram evaitena bhavati
ayaṃ ta indra soma iti daivodāsam
agniṣṭomena vai devā imaṃ lokam abhyajayann antarikṣam ukthenātirātreṇāmuṃ ta imaṃ lokaṃ punar abhyakāmayanta ta ihety asmiṃl loke pratyatiṣṭhan yad etat sāma bhavati pratiṣṭhityai
ūrdhvasadmanam api śarvarīṣu prohanti
asurā vā eṣu lokeṣv āsaṃs tān devā ūrdhvasadmanenaibhyo lokebhyaḥ prāṇudanta
tad ya evaṃ vedaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudya sva āyatane sattram āste
ā tū na indra kṣumantam ity ākūpāram
akūpārāṅgirasyāsīt tasyā yathā godhāyās tvag eva tvag āsīt tām etena triḥsāmnendraḥ pūtvā sūryatvacasam akarot tad vāva sā tarhy akāmayata yatkāmā etena sāmnā stuvate sa ebhyaḥ kāmaḥ samṛdhyate
abhi tvā vṛṣabhā sutaṃ ity ārṣabhaṃ kṣatrasāma kṣatram evaitena bhavati
idaṃ vaso sutam andha iti gāram etena vai gara indram aprīṇāt prīta evāsyaitenendro bhavati
idaṃ hy anv ojaseti mādhucchandasaṃ prajāpater vā eṣā tanūr ayātayāmnī prayujyate
ā tv etā niṣīdateti daivātitham
devātithiḥ saputro 'śanāyaṃś carann araṇya urvārūṇy avindat tāny etena sāmnopāsīdat tā asmai gāvaḥ pṛśnayo bhūtvodatiṣṭhan yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai
yoge yoge tavastaram iti saumedhaṃ rātriṣāma rātrer eva samṛddhyai
indra suteṣu someṣv iti kautsam
kutsaś ca luśaś cendraṃ vyahvayetāṃ sa indraḥ kutsam upāvartata taṃ śatena vārdhrībhir āṇḍayor abadhnāt taṃ luśo 'bhyavadat pramucyasva pari kutsād ihāgahi kim u tvāvān āṇḍayor baddha āsātā iti tāḥ saṃchidya prādravat sa etat kutsaḥ sāmāpaśyat tenainam anvavadat sa upāvartata
yad etat sāma bhavati sendratvāya
yadi sattrāya dīkṣerann atha sāmy uttiṣṭhet somam apabhajya viśvajitātirātreṇa yajeta sarvavedasena sarvasmā eva dīkṣate sarvam āpnoti
yā id dakṣiṇā dadāti tābhir iti prayuṅkte
yadi paryāyair astutam abhivyucchet pañcadaśabhir hotre stuyuḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir itarebhyaḥ
agne vivasvad uṣasa iti sandhinā stuyuḥ prāṇā vai trivṛt stomānāṃ pratiṣṭhā rathantaraṃ sāmnāṃ prāṇāṃś caivopayanti pratiṣṭhāṃ ca
ṣaṣṭiṃ ca trīṇi ca śatāni hotā śaṃsati
tāvatyaḥ saṃvatsarasya rātrayaḥ saṃvatsarasaṃmitābhir eva tad ṛgbhir āśīvinam āpnoti
yad arvāk stuvanti tad astutaṃ yat samprati stuvanti tat stutaṃ yad atiṣṭuvanti tat suṣṭutam
yady arvāk stuyur yāvatībhir na stuyus tāvatībhir vātiṣṭuyur bhūyo 'kṣarābhir vā
yady atiṣṭuyur yāvatībhir atiṣṭuyus tāvatībhir vā na stuyuḥ kanīyo 'kṣarābhir vā
yady arvāk stuyus trīḍam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ nidhanam ekeḍayā ye dve tābhyām eva tat samaṃ kriyate
yady atiṣṭuyuḥ svāram agniṣṭomasāma kāryam ūnam iva vā etat sāmno yat svaras tenaiva tat samaṃ kriyate
yadi somau saṃsutau syātāṃ mahati rātreḥ prātaranuvākam upākuryāt
pūrvo vācaṃ pūrvaś chandāṃsi pūrvo devatā vṛṅkte
vṛṣaṇvatīṃ pratipadaṃ kuryād indro vai vṛṣā prātaḥsavanād evaiṣām indraṃ vṛṅkte
atho khalv āhuḥ savanamukhe savanamukhe kāryā savanamukhāt savanamukhād evaiṣām indraṃ vṛṅkte
susamiddhe hotavyam agnir vai sarvā devatāḥ sarvā eva devatāḥ paśyañ juhoti
saṃveśāyopaveśāya gāyatryai chandase 'bhibhūtaye svāhā saṃveśāyopaveśāya triṣṭubhe chandase 'bhibhūtaye svāhā saṃveśāyopaveśāya jagatyai chandase 'bhibhūtaye svāheti juhoti
chandāṃsi vā abhibhūtayas tair evainān abhibhavaty ubhe bṛhadrathantare kārye
yatra vā indrasya harī tad indraḥ indrasya vai harī bṛhadrathantare yad ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavataḥ pūrva evendrasya harī ārabhante
tauraśravase kārye
turaśravasaś ca vai pārāvatānāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata ete turaśravāḥ sāmanī apaśyat tābhyām asmā indraḥ śalmalināṃ yamunāyā havyaṃ nirāvahat yat tauraśravase bhavato havyam evaiṣāṃ vṛṅkte
pūrve 'bhiṣuṇuyuḥ
yā vai pūrvāḥ prasnānti tāḥ pūrvās tīrthaṃ jayanti pūrva evendram ārabhante
vihavyaṃ śasyam
jamadagneś ca vā ṛṣīṇāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata etajjamadagnir vihavyam apaśyat tam indra upāvartata yad vihavyaṃ hotā śaṃsatīndram evaiṣāṃ vṛṅkte
yadītaro 'gniṣṭomaḥ syād ukthaḥ kāryo yady uktho 'tirātro yo vai bhūyān yajñakratuḥ sa indrasya priyo bhūyasaivaiṣāṃ yajñakratunendraṃ vṛṅkte
atho khalv āhur duṣprāpa iva vai paraḥ panthā yam evāgre yajñakratum ārabheta tasmān neyād iti
sajanīyaṃ śasyam agastyasya kayāśubhīyaṃ śasyam
asyā amuṣyā adyaśvān mithunād ahorātrābhyām evainān nirbhajati
yadi somam akrītam apahareyur anyaḥ kretavyaḥ
yadi krītaṃ yo 'nyo 'bhyāśaṃ syāt sa āhṛtyaḥ somavikrayaṇe tu kiṃcid dadyāt
yadi somaṃ na vindeyuḥ pūtīkān abhiṣuṇuyur yadi na pūtīkān arjunāni
gāyatrī somam āharat tasyā anu visṛjya somarakṣiḥ parṇam achinat tasya yo 'ṃśuḥ parāpatat sa pūtīko 'bhavat tasmin devā ūtim avindann ūtīko vā eṣa yat pūtīkān abhiṣuṇvanty ūtim evāsmai vindanti
pratidhuk ca prātaḥ pūtīkāś ca śṛtaṃ ca madhyandine pūtīkāś ca dadhi cāparāhṇe pūtīkāś ca
somapītho vā etasmād apakrāmatīty āhur yasya somam apaharantīti sa oṣadhīś ca paśūṃś ca praviśati tam oṣadhibhyaś ca paśubhyaś cāvarunddhe
indro vṛtram ahaṃs tasya yo nastaḥ somaḥ samadhāvat tāni babhrutūlāny arjunāni yo vapāyā utkhinnāyās tāni lohitatūlāni yāni babhrutūlāny arjunāni tāny abhiṣuṇuyād etad vai brahmaṇo rūpaṃ sākṣād eva somam abhiṣuṇoti
śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma kāryaṃ sad evainaṃ karoti
yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi prohed vācaivainaṃ samardhayati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam indriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyai
pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ
pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam evārabhate
avabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣeta
tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt
yadi kalaśo dīryeta vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ brahmasāma kuryāt
avaṣaṭkṛto vā etasya somaḥ parāsicyate yasya kalaśo dīryate yad vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ brahmasāma bhavati vaṣaṭkṛta evāsya somo bhavati
vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ samane bahūnām ity etāsu kāryam
eṣa hi bahūnāṃ samane dīryate yat kalaśaḥ
tad āhur na vā ārtyārtir anūdyārtyā vā eṣa ārtim anuvadati yaḥ kalaśe dīrṇe dadrāṇavatīṣu karotīti
śrāyantīyam eva kāryam
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno 'manyata sa etacchrāyantīyam apaśyat tenātmānaṃ samaśrīṇāt prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa
dugdha iva eṣa riricāno yasya kalaśo dīryate yacchrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati punar evātmānaṃ saṃśrīṇāti prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa
yadi śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma syād vaiṣṇavīṣv anuṣṭupsu vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ kuryāt
yad vai yajñasya sravati vācaṃ pratisravati vāg anuṣṭup yajño viṣṇur vācaiva yajñasya chidram apidadhāti
yad vai yajñasya sravaty antataḥ sravati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ yajñasyaiva chidraṃ vārayate
yadi prātassavanāt somo 'tiricyeta asti somo ayaṃ suta iti marutvatīṣu gāyatreṣu stuyuḥ
mādhyandinaṃ vā eṣa savanaṃ nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yaḥ prātassavanād atiricyate tasmān marutvatīṣu stuvanti marutvaddhi mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ tasmād u gāyatrīṣu gāyatraṃ hi prātassavanam
yasmāt stomād atiricyate sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāya
aindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati
vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe pratitiṣṭhati
yadi mādhyandināt savanād atiricyeta baṇ mahāṁ asi sūryety ādityavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥ
tṛtīyasavanaṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo mādhyandināt savanād atiricyate tasmād ādityavatīṣu stuvanty ādityaṃ hi tṛtīyasavanaṃ tasmād u bṛhatīṣu bārhataṃ hi mādhyandinaṃ savanam
yasmāt stomād atiricyeta sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāyaindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe pratitiṣṭhati
yadi tṛtīyasavanād atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥ
yajño vai viṣṇuḥ śipiviṣṭo yajña eva viṣṇau pratitiṣṭhaty atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti
etad anyat kuryur ukthāni praṇayeyur ukthāni vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo 'gniṣṭomād atiricyate ya ukthyebhyo 'tiricyetātirātraḥ kāryo rātriṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate ya ukthyebhyo 'tiricyate yadi rātrer atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu bṛhatā stuyur eṣa tu vā atiricyata ity āhur yo rātrer atiricyata iti
amuṃ vā eṣa lokaṃ nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo rātrer atiricyate bṛhatā stuvanti bṛhad amuṃ lokam āptum arhati tam evāpnoti
yadi dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate dagdhvāsthīny upanahya yo nediṣṭhī syāt taṃ dīkṣayitvā saha yajeran
etad anyat kuryur abhiṣutyānyat somam agṛhītvā grahān yāsau dakṣiṇā sraktis tad vā stuyur mārjālīye vā
api vā etasya yajñe yo dīkṣitaḥ pramīyate tam etena niravadayante
yāmena stuvanti yamalokam evainaṃ gamayanti
tisṛbhiḥ stuvanti tṛtīye hi loke pitaraḥ
parācībhiḥ stuvanti parāṅ hīto 'sau lokaḥ
sarparājñyā ṛgbhiḥ stuvanti
arbudaḥ sarpa etābhir mṛtāṃ tvacam apāhata mṛtām evaitābhis tvacam apaghnate
tā ṛco 'nubruvantas trir mārjālīyaṃ pariyanti savyān ūrūn āghnānāḥ
stutam anuśaṃsaty amuṣminn evainaṃ loke nidhunvanti
yanti vā ete patha ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīty aindravāyavāgrān grahān gṛhṇate punaḥ panthānam apiyanti
agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti pratipatkāryā ya eva jīvanti teṣv āyur dadhāti
saṃvatsare 'sthīni yājayeyuḥ saṃvvatsaro vai sarvasya śāntir yat purā saṃvvatsarād yājayeyur vācam aruṣkṛtāṃ krūrām ṛccheyuḥ
asaṃmitaṃ stotraṃ syād asaṃmito hyasau lokas trivṛtaḥ pavamānāḥ syuḥ saptadaśam itarat sarvam
yat trivṛtaḥ pavamānā bhavanti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān evopayanti yat saptadaśam itarat sarvaṃ prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evopayanti
prāṇāpānair vā ete vyṛdhyanta ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīti maitrāvaruṇāgrān grahān gṛhṇate prāṇāpānau mitrāvaruṇau prāṇāpānair eva samṛdhyante
yasya kalaśa upadasyati kalaśam evāsyopadasyantaṃ prāṇo 'nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥ
tad āhuḥ payo 'vanayed iti
atho khalv āhur antarhitam iva vā etad yat payo hiraṇyam evāpo 'bhyavanayeddhiraṇyam abhyunnayed iti
prāṇā vā āpo 'mṛtaṃ hiraṇyam amṛta evāsya prāṇān dadhāti sa sarvam āyur eti
yasya nārāśaṃsa upavāyati nārāśaṃsam evāsyopavāyantaṃ prāṇo 'nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥ
yam adhvaryur antato grahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tasyāptum avanayet
prāyaścittyai vai graho gṛhyate prāyaścittyaivāsmai prāyaścittiṃ karoti
yadi pītāpītau somau saṃgaccheyātām antaḥparidhyaṅgārān nirvartya juhuyāddhutasya cāhutasya cāhutasya hutasya ca pītāpītasya somasyendrāgnī pibataṃ sutaṃ svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
prajāpataye svāhety abhakṣaṇīyasya juhuyād uttarārdhyapūrvārdhya uparavaḥ
indur indum avāgād ity avavṛṣṭasya bhakṣayet
tasya ta indav indrapītasyendriyavataḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra ity ājyenābhyupākṛtasya juhuyād agnīdhraṃ paretya bhūtānāṃ jātaḥ patir eka āsīt sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ dyām utemāṃ tasmai ta indo haviṣā vidhema svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
yadi grāvāpiśīryate paśubhir yajamāno vyṛdhyate paśavo vai grāvāṇo dyutānasya mārutasya sāmnā stuyuḥ
mārutā vai grāvāṇaḥ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
yadi somam abhidahed grahān adhvaryuḥ spāśayeta stotrāṇy udgātā śastrāṇi hotātha yathāpūrvaṃ yajñena careyuḥ pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam ārabhate 'vabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣate tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt purā dvādaśyā dīkṣeta yad dvādaśīm atinayed antardhīyeta
yadi mahāvīro bhidyeta taṃ bhinnam abhimṛśed ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ
asuryaṃ vā etasmād varṇaṃ kṛtvā teja indriyaṃ vīryam annādyaṃ prajāḥ paśavo 'pakrāmanti yasya yūpo virohati sa īśvaraḥ pāpīyān bhavitoḥ
tvāṣṭraṃ paśuṃ bahurūpam ālabheta tvaṣṭā vai paśūnāṃ rūpāṇāṃ vikartā tam eva tad upadhāvati sa enaṃ tejasendriyeṇa vīryeṇānnādyena prajayā paśubhiḥ punas samardhayati saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
agninā pṛthivyauṣadhibhis tenāyaṃ lokas trivṛd vāyunāntarikṣeṇa vayobhis tenaiṣa lokas trivṛd yo 'yam antar ādityena divā nakṣatrais tenāsau lokas trivṛd etad eva trivṛta āyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tam u pratiṣṭhetyāhus trivṛddhy evaiṣu lokeṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥ
ardhamāsa eva pañcadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
taṃ caujo balam ity āhur ardhamāsaśo hi prajāḥ paśava ojo balaṃ puṣyanti
saṃvatsara eva saptadaśasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartava etad eva saptadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tam u prajāpatir ity āhuḥ saṃvatsaraṃ hi prajāḥ paśavo 'nuprajāyante
āditya evaikaviṃśasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśa etad evaikaviṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tam u devatalpa ity āhuḥ pra devatalpam āpnoti ya evaṃ veda
trivṛd eva triṇavasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tam u puṣṭir ity āhus trivṛddhy evaiṣa puṣṭaḥ
devatā eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanaṃ trayastriṃśad devatāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśa etad eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tam u nāka ity āhur na hi prajāpatiḥ kasmaicanākam
chandāṃsy eva chandomānām āyatanam eṣaiṣāṃ bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tān u puṣṭir ity āhuḥ paśavo hi chandomāḥ
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata so 'tāmyat tasmai vāgjyotir udagṛhṇāt so 'bravīt ko me 'yaṃ jyotir udagṛhṇād iti svaiva te vāg ity abravīt tām abravīd virājaṃ tvā chandasāṃ jyotiḥ kṛtvā yajāntā iti
tasmād yo virājaṃ stomaṃ sampadyate taṃ jyotiṣṭomo 'gniṣṭoma ity ācakṣate virāḍḍhi chandasāṃ jyotiḥ
jyotiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
anuṣṭup ca vai saptadaśaś ca samabhavatāṃ sānuṣṭup caturuttarāṇi chandāṃsy asṛjata ṣaḍuttarān stomān saptadaśas tāv etān madhyataḥ prājanayatām
trivṛcca triṇavaś ca rāthantarau tāv ajaś cāśvaś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau rāthantaraṃ prācīnaṃ pradhūnutaḥ
pañcadaśaś caikaviṃśaś ca bārhatau tau gauś cāviś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau bārhataṃ prācīnaṃ bhāskurutaḥ
evaṃ vai vidvāṃsam āhur api grāmyāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ vāca ājānāti
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa ātmann ṛtvam apaśyat tata ṛtvijo 'sṛjata yad ṛtvād asṛjata tad ṛtvijām ṛtviktvaṃ tair etaṃ dvādaśāham upāsīdat so 'rādhnot
pitā no 'rātsīd iti māsā upāsīdaṃs te dīkṣayaivārādhnuvann upasatsu trayodaśam adīkṣayan so 'nuvyam abhavat tasmād upasatsu didīkṣāṇo 'nuvyaṃ bhavaty eva ca hi trayodaśaṃ māsaṃ cakṣate naiva ca
eko dīkṣetaiko hi prajāpatir arādhnod dvādaśa dīkṣeran dvādaśa hi māsā arādhnuvaṃś caturviṃśatir dīkṣeraṃś caturviṃśatir hy ardhamāsā arādhnuvan
yadi pañcaviṃśo dīkṣeteme pañceme pañceme pañceme pañceme catvāro 'sāv eka iti nirdiśeyur yasmā arāddhikāmāḥ syus tam evārāddhir anveti sarva itare rādhnuvanti
yo vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiṃ vedāśnute gārhapataṃ pra gārhapatam āpnoti
saṃvatsaro vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiḥ sa eva prajāpatis tasya māsā eva saha dīkṣiṇaḥ
vindate saha dīkṣiṇo 'śnute gārhapatyaṃ pra gārhapatyaṃ āpnoti ya evaṃ veda
yo vai chandasāṃ svarājaṃ vedāśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ āpnoti bṛhatī vāva chandasāṃ svarāḍ aśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ āpnoti ya evaṃ veda
tām etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ dvādaśa dīkṣā dvādaśopasado dvādaśa prasutaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśad etā rātrayo bhavanti ṣaṭtriṃśadakṣarā bṛhatī
jāyate vāva dīkṣayā punīta upasadbhir devalokam eva sutyayāpyeti
etāvad vāva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ yad etā rātrayo dvādaśa paurṇamāsyo dvādaśaikāṣṭakā dvādaśāmāvāsyā yāvad eva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ tad etenāptvāvarunddhe dvādaśāhena
triṃśadakṣarā vā eṣā virāḍ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva virājā pratitiṣṭhaty ṛtubhir virāji
dvātriṃśadakṣarā vā eṣānuṣṭub vāg anuṣṭup catuṣpādaḥ paśavo vācā paśūn dādhāra tasmād vācā siddhā vācāhūtā āyanti tasmād u nāma jānate
bhūtaṃ pūrvo 'tirātro bhaviṣyad uttaraḥ pṛthivī pūrvo 'tirātro dyaur uttaro 'gniḥ pūrvo 'tirātra āditya uttaraḥ prāṇaḥ pūrvo 'tirātra udāna uttaraḥ
cakṣuṣī atirātrau kanīnike agniṣṭomau yasmād antarā agniṣṭomāv atirātrābhyāṃ tasmād antare satyau kanīnike bhuṅktaḥ
saṃvatsarasya vā etau daṃṣṭrau yad atirātrau tayor na svaptavyaṃ saṃvatsarasya daṃṣṭrayor ātmānaṃ ned apidadhānīti
tad āhuḥ ko 'svaptum arhati yad vāva prāṇo jāgāra tad eva jāgaritam iti
gāyatrīṃ vā etāṃ jyotiḥpakṣām āsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham aṣṭau madhya ukthā agniṣṭomāv abhito bhāsā svargaṃ lokam etyājarasaṃ brahmādyam annam atti dīpyamānaḥ
triḥ purastād rathantaraṃ upayanti tryāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ tanvate
jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yat triḥ purastād rathantaram upayantīti saubharam ukthānāṃ brahmasāma bhavati tenaiva tad ajāmi
pratnavatyaḥ prāyaṇīyasyāhnaḥ pratipado bhavanti teno eva tad ajāmi
trir vevopariṣṭād rathantaram upayanti tryāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhād uttiṣṭhanti
trayo vā ete trirātrā yad eṣa dvādaśāho gāyatramukhaḥ prathamo gāyatramadhyo dvitīyo gāyatrottamas tṛtīyaḥ
yasmād gāyatramukhaḥ prathamas tasmād ūrdhvo 'gnir dīdāya yasmād gāyatramadhyo dvitīyas tasmāt tiryaṅ vāyuḥ pavate yasmād gāyatrottamastṛtīyastasmād arvāṅādityastapati
tejasā vai gāyatrī prathamaṃ trirātraṃ dādhāra padairdvitīyam akṣaraistṛtīyam
trivṛdvai gāyatryāstejas trivṛt prāyaṇīyam ahas tena prathamastrirātro dhṛtas tripadā gāyatrī trirātrī madhye tena dvitīyas trirātro dhṛtaś caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī caturviṃśaḥ saptamam ahas tena tṛtīyastrirātro dhṛtaḥ
tejasā vā ete prayanti tejo madhye dadhati tejo 'bhyudyanti jyotiṣā vā ete prayanti jyotir madhye dadhati jyotir abhyudyanti cakṣuṣā vā ete prayanti cakṣur madhye dadhati cakṣur abhyudyanti prāṇena vā ete prayanti prāṇaṃ madhye dadhati prāṇam abhyudyanti ye gāyatryā prayanti gāyatrīṃ madhye dadhati gāyatrīm abhyudyanti
tantraṃ vā etad vitāyate yad eṣa dvādaśāhas tasyaite mayūkhā yad gāyatry asaṃvyāthāya
girikṣidauccāmanyaveti hovācābhipratārī kākṣaseniḥ kathaṃ dvādaśāha iti yathārān nemiḥ paryety evam enaṃ gāyatrī paryeti avisraṃsāya yathārā nābhau dhṛtā evam asyāṃ dvādaśāho dhṛtaḥ
anuṣṭubhaṃ vā etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham
aṣṭābhir vā akṣarair anuṣṭup prathamaṃ dvādaśāhasyāhar udyacchaty ekādaśabhir dvitīyaṃ dvādaśabhis tṛtīyam
akṣaraṃ tryakṣaram ucchiṣyate tad evottaraṃ trirātram anuvidadhāti
chandāṃsy evāsyās tṛtīyaṃ trirātraṃ vahanti
tāṃ vā etāṃ pratīcīṃ tiraścīṃ parācīm āsate 'nnādyāya tasmāt pratyañcaṃ tiryañcaṃ parāñcaṃ prajāḥ paśum upajīvanti
chandāṃsi vā anyonyasya lokam abhyadhyāyan gāyatrī triṣṭubhas triṣṭub jagatyā jagatī gāyatryās tāni vyauhan yathālokaṃ tato vai tāni yaṃ yaṃ kāmam akāmayanta tam asanvan
yatkāmo vyūḍhacchandasā dvādaśāhena yajate so 'smai kāmaḥ samṛdhyate
oko vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho yatho vai manuṣyā imaṃ lokam āviṣṭā evaṃ devatā dvādaśāham āviṣṭā devatā ha vā etena yajate ya evaṃ vidvān dvādaśāhena yajate
gṛhā vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho nāgṛhatāyā bhayyam
yo vai dvādaśāham agniṣṭomena kalpamānaṃ veda kalpate 'smai prātaḥsavanenaiva prathamas trirātraḥ kalpate mādhyandinena dvitīyas tṛtīyasavanena tṛtīyo 'gniṣṭomasāmnaiva daśamam ahaḥ kalpate
kalpate 'smai ya evaṃ veda
eti prety āśumad vītimad rukmat tejasvad yuñjānaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpaṃ trivṛtaḥ stomasya gāyatrasya chandaso rathantarasya sāmnaḥ
vṛṣavad vṛtravad rayimad viśvavad upasthitaṃ dvitīyasyāhno rūpaṃ pañcadaśasya stomasya traiṣṭubhasya chandaso bṛhataḥ sāmnaḥ
udvat trivad digvat gomad ṛṣabhavat tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ saptadaśasya stomasya jāgatasya chandaso vairūpasya sāmnaḥ
rājanvaj janavadvat sūryavad virāḍanutodavac caturthasyāhno rūpam ekaviṃśasya stomasyānuṣṭubhasya chandaso vairājasya sāmnaḥ
citravacchiśumat paṅktiḥ śakvarī vyūnākṣarā gomad ṛṣabhavad vajryabhimat pañcamasyāhno rūpaṃ triṇavasya stomasya pāṅktasya chandasaḥ śakvarīṇāṃ sāmnaḥ
parivat prativat saptapadā dvipadā vinārāśaṃsā gomad ṛṣabhavat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ trayastriṃśasya stomasya sarveṣāṃ chandasāṃ rūpaṃ revatīnāṃ sāmnaḥ
yasmād eṣā samānā satī ṣaḍahavibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād virūpaḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ
virūpam enam anuprajāyate ya evaṃ veda
agna iti prathamasyāhno rūpam agnivibhakter agnim iti dvitīyasyāgnineti tṛtīyasyāgnir iti caturthasya
devā vai śriyam aicchaṃs tāṃ na prathame 'hany avindan na dvitīye na tṛtīye tāṃ caturthe 'hany avindan vindate śriyaṃ ya evaṃ vedāgner iti pañcamasya teno śrīḥ pratyupoditety āhuḥ
aprativādy enaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
agna iti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti
yasmād eṣā samānā saty agnivibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartvādityas tapati
indreti prathamasyāhno rūpam indravibhakter indram iti dvitīyasyendreṇeti tṛtīyasyendra iti caturthasyendrād iti pañcamasyendreti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti yasmād eṣā samānā satīndravibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartv oṣadhayaḥ pacyante
yad ṛcā prastauti tat prathamasyāhno rūpam svaravibhakter yat purastāt stobhaṃ tad dvitīyasya yad ubhayataḥ stobhaṃ tat tṛtīyasya yad anutunnaṃ tac caturthasya yad abhyārabdhaṃ tat pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam
svarāṇāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī svaravibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartu vāyuḥ pavate
padanidhanaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam nidhanavibhakter bahirṇidhanaṃ dvitīyasya diṅnidhanaṃ tṛtīyasyenidhanaṃ caturthasyāthakāraṇidhanaṃ pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī nidhanavibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād ime lokāḥ saha santo nānaiva
dravadiḍaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam iḍāvibhakter ūrdhveḍaṃ dvitīyasya pariṣṭubdheḍaṃ tṛtīyasyeḍābhir aiḍaṃ caturthasyādhyardheḍaṃ pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam iḍānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satīḍāvibhaktir nānārūpā tasmāt samānāḥ santaḥ paśavo nānārūpāḥ
bharadvājāyanā vai sattram āsata tān apṛcchan kiṃ prathamenāhnā kuruteti praivaimeti kiṃ dvitīyenety avasam evākurmahīti kiṃ tṛtīyeneti pary evāplavāmahīti kiṃ caturtheneti sataiva sad apyadadhmeti kiṃ pañcameneti prāṇān eva vicchindanta aimeti kiṃ ṣaṣṭhenetīdam evāgacchāmeti
yasya padena prastauty atha svāram abhi vāva tena devāḥ paśūn apaśyan yat purastāt stobhaṃ atha svāram ud eva tenāsṛjanta yad ubhayataḥ stobham atha svāram ebhya eva tena lokebhyo devāḥ paśubhyo 'nnādyaṃ prāyacchan yad anutunnam atha svāram upaiva tenāśikṣan yasya madhye nidhanam atha svāraṃ garbhāṃs tenādadhata tān ihavatā svāreṇa prājanayan
imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ padanidhanenābhyajayann amuṃ bahirṇidhanenāntarikṣaṃ diṅnidhanenāmṛtatvam īnidhanenāgacchan brahmavarcasam athanidhanenāvārundhatāsminn eva loka ihanidhanena pratyatiṣṭhan
imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ dravadiḍenābhyajayann amum ūrdhveḍenāntarikṣaṃ pariṣṭubdheḍena pratiṣṭhām iḍābhir aiḍenāvārundhata pratiṣṭhāyādhyardheḍena vyajayantāsminn eva loka iheḍena pratyatiṣṭhan
na vāk saṃvatsaram ativadatīḍaiva saṃvatsaram ativadati garbheṇa saṃvatsare paryāvṛtya prajāyate tenātivadati
tā vā etāś catasraḥ ṣaḍahaṃ parācya iḍā atiyanty eṣānunūtaiṣā viṣūcy eṣā pratīcy etad dvīḍam
saṃvatsaro 'gnir vāk saṃvatsaro yad agnir vibhajyate vācam eva tad vibhajanti
dve dve akṣare vibhajanti dvau dvau hi māsāv ṛtur atho māsānām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
ṣaḍ ahāni vibhajanti ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyā ṛtūnāṃ pratiṣṭhityā atho ṛtūnām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate ṣaḍ u puruṣā yān agnir anuvihriyate
yad idaṃ bahudhāgnir vihriyate tad asāv ādityaḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ pratyaṅ tasmād ete devate vibhaktim ānaśāte nāto 'nyā kācana
stomo yujyate sattriyebhyo 'harbhyaḥ pratnavatībhiś copavatībhiś ca
yat pratnavatyo upavatībhyaḥ pūrvā yujyante brahma tat pūrvaṃ kṣatrād yujyate brahma hi pūrvaṃ kṣatrāt
manas tat pūrvaṃ vāco yujyate mano hi pūrvaṃ vāco yaddhi manasābhigacchati tad vācā vadati
bṛhat tat pūrvaṃ rathantarād yujyate bṛhaddhi pūrvaṃ rathantarād vijityā tu vai rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśe
saṃbhāryās tṛcā bhavanti yathāśiṣṭhān vahiṣṭhān saṃbhared evam evaitān saṃbharanti gatyai
nava bhavanti navāhasya yuktyā ṛcarcaivāhar yunakti yathā prārthasya śamyā avadadhyād evam evaitan navāhasya śamyā avadadhāti gatyai
trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣu
nirāhāvanty ājyāni bhavanti yuktam eva tair āhvayati
agna āyāhi vītaya ā no mitrāvaruṇāyāhi suṣamā hi ta indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ iti
pra somāso vipaścita iti gāyatrī bhavati pretyā abhi droṇāni babhrava ity abhikrāntyai sutā indrāya vāyava iti saṃskṛtyai pra soma deva vītaya iti pretyai pra tu draveti pretyai pra vā etenāhnā yanti
gāyatraṃ bhavati
yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
āśvaṃ bhavati
aśvo vai bhūtvā prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa prājāyata bahur abhavat prajāyate bahur bhavaty āśvena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ekākṣaraṃ nidhanam upayanti rathantarasyānativādāya
anativādyenaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
somasāma bhavati
yathā vā imā anyā oṣadhayaḥ evaṃ soma āsīt sa tapo 'tapyata sa etat somasāmāpaśyat tena rājyamādhipatyam agacchad yaśo 'bhavad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati yaśo bhavati somasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
yaudhājayaṃ bhavati yad eva yaudhājayasya brāhmaṇam
auśanaṃ yad auśanasya stomaḥ
abhi tvā śūra nonuma ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
kayā naś citra ābhuvad iti kavatyas tena prājāpatyāḥ ko hi prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai
taṃ vo dasmam ṛtīṣahaṃ vasor mandānam andhaso 'bhivatsaṃ na svasareṣu dhenava ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
indraṃ gīrbhir havāmaha iti havanta evainam
tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti stomo vai taro yajño vidadvasuḥ stomena vai yajño yujyate yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum ity āha yajñam eva tad yunakti
rathantaraṃ bhavati brahma vai rathantaraṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad brahmākramya prayanti
iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate
vāmadevyaṃ bhavati paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai prājāpatyaṃ vai vāmadevyaṃ prajāpatāv eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate
naudhasaṃ bhavati brahma vai naudhasaṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad brahmākramante
kāleyaṃ bhavati samānaloke vai kāleyaṃ ca rathantaraṃ ceyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ paśavaḥ kāleyam asyāṃ caiva paśuṣu ca pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate
dravadiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
pra somāso madacyuta iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāty ayā pavasva devayur ity eti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ pavate 'har yato harir iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bṛhad eva tad etasminn ahani yunakti tad yuktaṃ śva ārabhante pra sunvānāyāndhasa iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṇyam iva hy etad ahar abhi priyāṇi pavate canohita ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
yajñā yajñā vo agnaya ity agnir vai yajño yajña eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
saṃhitaṃ bhavati vyakṣaraṇidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai pratiṣṭhāyaiva sattram āsate
saphaṃ bhavati
saphena vai devā imān lokān samāpnuvan yat samāpnuvaṃs tat saphasya saphatvam imān evaitena lokān samāpya sattram āsate
ākṣāraṃ bhavati
aṣṭau vā etāḥ kāmadughā āsaṃs tāsām ekā samaśīryata sā kṛṣir abhavad ṛdhyate 'smai kṛṣau ya evaṃ veda
tāsu devāsurā aspardhanta te devā asurān kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇānudanta nudate bhrātṛvyaṃ kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ebhyo vai lokebhyo raso 'pākrāmat taṃ prajāpatir ākṣāreṇākṣārayad yad ākṣārayat tad ākṣārasyākṣāratvam
tasmād yaḥ purā puṇyo bhūtvā paścāt pāpīyān syād ākṣāraṃ brahmasāma kurvītātmany eved indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam ākṣārayati
januṣaikarcau bhavato 'hno dhṛtyai yad vā etasyāhno 'dhṛtaṃ tad etābhyāṃ dādhāra
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
gaurīvitir vā etacchāktyo brāhmaṇo 'tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam abhavat
atiriktaṃ vā etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitenāhīnāñchvastanavad bhavaty api prajāyā upakﾱptam
vṛṣā vā etad vājisāma vṛṣabho retodhā adya stuvanti śvaḥ prajāyate
anuṣṭubhi chandasāṃ kriyate 'nuṣṭubbhi chandasāṃ yoniḥ svāyām eva tad yonau reto dhatte prajātyai
prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda
dvyudāsaṃ bhavaty etau vā udāsau svargasya lokasyāvasānadarśau pūrveṇa pūrvam ahaḥ saṃsthāpayanty uttareṇottaram ahar abhyativadanti
tad yathādaḥ pūrvedyuḥ spaṣṭaṃ tṛṇodakam anvavasyanto yanty evam eva tābhyāṃ svargaṃ lokam anvavasyanto yanti
gautamaṃ bhavati
sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāllokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
yad u caivānuṣṭubhasya madhye nidhanasya brāhmaṇaṃ tad u caitasya
kāvaṃ bhavati
lokavindu sāma vindate lokaṃ kāvena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
svāram u svareṇa svareṇa hi devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ prayacchati
yajñāyajñīyaṃ bhavati
vāg yajñāyajñīyaṃ vāci yajñaḥ pratiṣṭhito vācy eva tad yajñam antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayanti taṃ vāco 'dhi śva ārabhante
trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
pavasva vāco agriya iti dvitīyasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
pavasveti rāthantaraṃ rūpam agriya iti bārhatam ubhe rūpe samārabhate dvirātrasyāvisraṃsāya
pavasvendo vṛṣāsuta ity anurūpo bhavati vṛṣaṇvad vā etad aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
pūrvam u tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam
anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda
stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai
vṛṣaṇvantas tṛcā bhavatīndriyasya vīryasyāvaruddhyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati
yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
pañcadaśa eva stomo bhavati
ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhati ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ
ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣu
nirāhopasthitāny ājyāni bhavanti
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha indram id gāthino bṛhad indre agnā namo bṛhad iti bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ
vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
punānas soma dhārayeti dhṛtyai
vṛṣā śoṇo abhikanikradad gā iti
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa samṛddhā vṛṣaṇvad vā etad aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
yauktāśvaṃ bhavati
yuktāśvo vā āṅgirasaḥ śiśū jātau viparyaharat tasmān mantro 'pākrāmat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad yauktāśvam apaśyat taṃ mantra upāvartata tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma yauktāśvaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
āyāsye bhavataḥ
ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annādyam āśnāt taṃ śug ārchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa ete āyāsye apaśyat tābhyāṃ śucam apāhatāpa śucaṃ hata āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tām ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayati vṛṣṭim āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ
annādyaṃ vāva tad ebhyo lokebhyo 'pākrāmat tad ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayaty annādyam āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati
vasiṣṭho vā etena vaiḍavaḥ stutvāñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
tvām iddhi havāmaha iti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
abhipravaḥ surādhasam iti yuñjate vai pūrveṇāhnā hy etena prayanti
tvām idā hyo nara ity adya caiva hyaś ca samārabhate dvirātrasyāvisraṃsāya
bṛhad bhavati varṣma vai bṛhad varṣma dvitīyam ahar varṣmaṇa eva tad varṣmākramante
śyaitaṃ bhavati sāmnorvāho yajñasya santatyai
mādhucchandasaṃ bhavati sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ūrdhveḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
yas te mado vareṇya iti gāyatrī bhavati
madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
pavasva madhumattama iti pavanta iva hy etenāhnā madhumattama ity annaṃ vai madhv annādyam eva tad yajamāne dadhāti
indram accha sutā ima itīndriyasya vīryasyāvaruddhyai
ayaṃ pūṣā rayir bhaga ity anuṣṭubhaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
vṛṣāmatīnāṃ pavate vicakṣaṇa iti jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
hāviṣmataṃ bhavati
haviṣmāṃś ca vai haviṣkṛccāṅgirasāvāstāṃ dvitīye 'hani haviṣmān arādhnon navame 'hani haviṣkṛt
ayaṃ haviṣmān ity eva jātam ahar jātaṃ somaṃ prāha devebhyaḥ sāmnaivāsmā āśiṣam āśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ
śaṅku bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai yad vā adhṛtaṃ śaṅkunā tad dādhāra
tad u sīdantīyam ity āhur etena vai prajāpatir ūrdhva imān lokān asīdad yad asīdat tat sīdantīyasya sīdantīyatvam ūrdhva imān lokān sīdati sīdantīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
sujñānaṃ bhavati
svarvad vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ svarṇidhanaṃ bārhatam
svarṇidhanaṃ bhavati tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
plavau vā etāv upohante svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
krauñcaṃ bhavati
vāg vai krauñcaṃ vāg dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyai
yāmaṃ bhavati
etena vai yamo 'napajayyam amuṣya lokasyādhipatyam āśnutānapajayyam amuṣya lokasyādhipatyam aśnute yāmena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
etena vai yamī yamaṃ svargaṃ lokam agamayat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
ehy ū ṣu bravāṇi ta ity ehivatyo bhavanti tṛtīyasyāhna upahavāya santatyai
apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāya
evā hy asi vīrayur iti samānaṃ vadantīdam ittham asad iti
indraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhann ity avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam evaitayā vardhanti
sākamaśvaṃ bhavaty ukthānām abhijityā abhikrāntyai
etena hy agra ukthāny adhyajayann etenābhyakrāman
āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kﾱptiś cānnādyaṃ ca samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyata idam ittham asad iti
kṣatraṃ vā etad ahar abhinirvadati yat pañcadaśaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahmasāma bhavati brahma caiva tat kṣatraṃ ca sayujī karoti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhati brahmaṇe kṣatraṃ ca viśaṃ cānuge karoti
brahma vai pūrvam ahaḥ kṣatraṃ dvitīyaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahmasāma bhavati brahma tad yaśasārdhayati brahma hi gāyatrī
tad u samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyate samṛddhyai
āṣṭādaṃṣṭre bhavataḥ
aiyāhā iti vā indro vṛtram ahann aiyādohoveti nyagṛhṇād vārtraghne sāmanī vīryavatī
ojo evaitābhyāṃ vīryam avarunddhe
pañcadaśa eva stomo bhavaty ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ
davidyutatyā ruceti tṛtīyasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
davidyutatī vai gāyatrī pariṣṭobhantī triṣṭub gavāśīr jagatī trīṇi rūpāṇi samārabhate trirātrasyāvisraṃsāya
ete asṛgram indava ity anurūpo bhavati
eta iti vai prajāpatir devān asṛjatāsṛgram iti manuṣyān indava iti pitṝṃs tad eva tad abhivadati
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda
stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai
rājā medhābhir īyate pavamāno manāv adhy antarikṣeṇa yātava iti
antarikṣadevatyas tṛco bhavaty antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
pañcarco bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyupayanti
saptadaśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
agnināgniḥ samidhyata ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
pūrve eva tad ahanī samiddhe tṛtīyam ahar abhisaminddhe
mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣam iti rāthantaram maitrāvaruṇam
huva iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpam
rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati
indreṇa saṃ hi dṛkṣusa ity aindram
sam iva vā ime lokā dadṛśire 'ntarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
tā huve yayor idam iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
huva iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ
uccā te jātam andhasa iti gāyatrī bhavati
udvad vā etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
andhasvatī bhavaty ahar vā andho 'hna ārambhaḥ
abhi somāsa āyava iti
abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaityubhau hi varṇāvetad ahaḥ
tisro vāca īrayati pravahnir iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhante
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hyetad ahaḥ
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
vaiṣṭambhaṃ bhavati
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā vaiṣṭambhair vyaṣṭabhnuvaṃs tad vaiṣṭambhasya vaiṣṭambhatvam
diśa iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
paurūmadgaṃ bhavati
ahar vā etad avlīyamānaṃ tad rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tasmād devāḥ paurūmadgena rakṣāṃsyapāghnann apa pāpmānaṃ hate paurūmadgena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
devāś ca vāsurāś cāspardhanta te devā asurāṇāṃ paurūmadgena puro 'majjayan yat puro 'majjayaṃstasmāt paurūmadgaṃ pāpmānam evaitena bhrātṛvyaṃ majjayati
gautamaṃ bhavati
yad eva gautamasya brāhmaṇam
ubhayataḥstobhaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
antarikṣaṃ bhavati
antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyam antarikṣa eva tad antarikṣeṇa stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ bhavati
as iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ has iti bārhataṃ tṛtīyam eva tad rūpam upayanti samṛddhyai
aṅgirasāṃ saṃkrośo bhavati
etena vā aṅgirasaḥ saṃkrośamānāḥ svargaṃ lokam āpan svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
yaddyāva indra te śatam iti śatavatyo bhavanti
śatavad vai paśūnāṃ rūpaṃ sahasravat paśūnām evaitābhī rūpam avarunddhe
vayaṃ gha tvā sutāvanta iti satobṛhatyo varṣīyaś chanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
taraṇir it siṣāsati vājaṃ purandhyā yujā ā va indraṃ puruhūtaṃ name girety āvad akṣaram uddhatam iva vai tṛtīyam ahar yad etad āvadakṣaraṃ bhavaty ahar evaitena pratiṣṭhāpayati
pañcanidhanaṃ vairūpaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati diśāṃ dhṛtyai
pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai
diśāṃ vā etat sāma yad vairūpaṃ diśo hy evaitenābhivadati
atha yat pañcanidhanaṃ tenartūnāṃ pañca hy ṛtavaḥ
ṛtubhiś ca vā ime lokā digbhiś cāvṛtās teṣv evobhayeṣu yajamānaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati yajamānaṃ vā anupratitiṣṭhantam udgātā pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ vidvān vairūpeṇodgāyati
digvad bhavati bhrātṛvyasyāpanuttyai
diśaṃ viśam iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
has ity upariṣṭād diśāṃ nidhanam upayanti tena bārhatam
rāthantaro vā ayaṃ loko bārhato 'sāv ubhe eva tad bṛhadrathantarayo rūpeṇāparādhnoti
anaḍvāhau vā etau devayānau yajamānasya yad bṛhadrathantare tāv eva tad yunakti svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
aśvavad bhavati prajātyai
yathā maṇḍūka āṭ karoty evaṃ nidhanam upayanty ayātayāmatāyai
dvādaśa vairūpāṇi bhavanti dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati
virūpaḥ saṃvatsaro virūpam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai
mahāvaiṣṭambhaṃ brahmasāma bhavaty annādyasyāvaruddhyai
yadā vai puruṣo 'nnam atty athāntarato viṣṭabdhaḥ
diśa iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
satobṛhatīṣu stuvanti pūrvayor ahnoḥ pratyudyamāya
rauravam acchāvākasāma bhavati
agnir vai rūro rudro 'gniḥ
agnir vā etasya paśūn apakramayati yasya paśavo 'pakrāmanty agnir eva tasya paśūn abhikramayati yasya paśavo 'bhikrāmanti
abhy abhy evāsya paśavaḥ krāmanti ya evaṃ vidvān rauraveṇa stuvate
pariṣṭubdheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
tisro vāca udīrata iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhante
udvad vā etat trivad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
ā sotā pariṣiñcateti parivatyo bhavanti
anto vai tṛtīyam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
sakhāya āniṣīdatety uddhatam iva vai tṛtīyam ahar yad āha niṣīdatety ahar evaitena pratiṣṭhāpayati
sutāso madhumattamā ity anuṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspata iti
vitatam iva vā idam antarikṣam antareme antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
pāṣṭhauhaṃ bhavati
paṣṭhavāḍvā etenāṅgirasaś caturthasyāhno vācaṃ vadantīm upāśṛṇot sa ho vāg iti nidhanam upait tad asyābhyuditaṃ tad ahar avasat
vācaḥ sāma bhavati
vāg vai dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyai
niṣkirīyāḥ sattram āsata te tṛtīyam ahar na prājānaṃs tān etat sāma gāyamānān vāg upāplavat tena tṛtīyam ahaḥ prājānaṃs te 'bruvann iyaṃ vāva nas tṛtīyam ahar adīdṛśad iti tṛtīyasyaivaiṣāhno dṛṣṭiḥ
śauktaṃ bhavati
śuktir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāllokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
tvāṣṭrīsāma bhavati
indraṃ vā akṣyāmayiṇaṃ bhūtāni nāsvāpayaṃs tam etena tvāṣṭryo 'svāpayaṃs tad vāva tās tarhy akāmayanta
kāmasani sāma tvāṣṭrīsāma kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
indro vṛtrād bibhyad gāṃ prāviśat taṃ tvāṣṭryo 'bruvañ janayāmeti tam etaiḥ sāmabhir ajanayañ jāyāmahā iti vai sattram āsate jāyanta eva
ariṣṭaṃ bhavati
devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta yaṃ devānām aghnan na sa samabhavad yam asurāṇāṃ saṃ so 'bhavat te devās tapo 'tapyanta ta etad ariṣṭam apaśyaṃs tato yaṃ devānām aghnat saṃ so 'bhavad yam asurāṇāṃ na sa samabhavad anenāriṣāmeti tad ariṣṭasyāriṣṭatvam ariṣṭyā evāriṣṭam antataḥ kriyate
trīḍaṃ bhavati trirātrasya dhṛtyai
dravantīm iḍām uttamām upayanti caturthasyāhnaḥ santatyai stomaḥ
pra maṃhiṣṭhāya gāyateti
yad gāyateti mahasa eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
taṃ te madaṃ gṛṇīmasīti madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
śrudhī havaṃ tiraścyā iti śrutyā eva
pramaṃhiṣṭhīyaṃ bhavati
pramaṃhiṣṭhīyena vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāvartayat tam astṛṇuta bhrātṛvyavān pramaṃhiṣṭhīyenokthāni praṇayeta stṛṇute bhrātṛvyaṃ vasīyān ātmanā bhavati
hārivarṇaṃ bhavati
indraś ca vai namuciś cāsuraḥ samadadhātāṃ na no naktaṃ na divā hanan nārdreṇa na śuṣkeṇeti tasya vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditye 'pāṃ phenena śiro 'chinad etad vai na naktaṃ na divā yat vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditya etan nārdraṃ na śuṣkaṃ yad apāṃ phenas tad enaṃ pāpīyaṃ vācaṃ vadad anvavartata vīrahannadruho 'druha iti tan narcā na sāmnāpahantum aśaknot
hārivarṇasyaiva nidhanenāpāhata
apa śucaṃ hate hārivarṇasya nidhanena śriyaṃ ca haraś copaiti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
tairaścyaṃ bhavati
aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ yanto rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tāny etena tiraścyāṅgirasas tiryaṅ paryavaid yat tiryaṅ paryavait tasmāt tairaścyaṃ pāpmā vāva sa tān asacata taṃ tairaścyenāpāghnatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate tairaścyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
saptadaśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
pra ta āśvinīḥ pavamāna dhenava iti caturthasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
āpte trirātre gāyatryā rūpeṇa prayanti prati vai gāyatryā rūpam
jagatī pratipad bhavati jāgatam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ jagatyā eva taj jagatīm abhisaṃkrāmanti
yad ato 'nyā pratipatsyāt pratikūlaṃ vānukūlaṃ vā syāt
pavamāno ajījanad ity anurūpo bhavati
janadvad vā etad ahar yac caturtham annādyaṃ janayati virājaṃ janayaty ekaviṃśaṃ stomaṃ janayati
pūrvam u caiva tadrūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda
stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai
ṣaḍṛcau bhavata ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanty ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
janasya gopā ajaniṣṭa jāgṛviḥ ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
janadvad vā etad ahar yac caturtham annādyaṃ janayati virājaṃ janayaty ekaviṃśaṃ stomaṃ janayati
ayaṃ vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā iti bārhataṃ maitrāvaruṇam
bṛhad etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati
indro dadhīco asthibhir iti dādhīcas tṛco bhavati
dadhyaṅ vā āṅgiraso devānāṃ purodhānīya āsīd annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhā annādyasyāvaruddhyai
iyaṃ vām asya manmana ity aindrāgnam
indrāgnī pūrvyastutir abhrād vṛṣṭir ivājanīty ānuṣṭubhī vai vṛṣṭir ānuṣṭubham etad ahar yac caturthaṃ samīcyau virājau dadhāty annādyāya stomaḥ
pavasva dakṣasādhana iti gāyatrī bhavati siddhyai
yat pavasveti tad bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
tavāhaṃ soma rarāṇa sakhya indo dive dive purūṇi babhro ni caranti māmava paridhīṃr ati tāṁ ihīti
ati hy āyañchakunā iva paptimety ati hy apatat
punāno akramīd abhīti
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
caturṇidhanam ātharvaṇaṃ bhavati catūrātrasya dhṛtyai
catuṣpadānuṣṭub ānuṣṭubham etad ahar yaccaturtham
bheṣajaṃ vā ātharvaṇāni bheṣajam eva tat karoti
nidhanakāmaṃ bhavati
ekaṃ vā anyena niruktena nidhanena kāmaṃ sanoty athaitan nidhanakāmaṃ sarveṣāṃ kāmānām avaruddhyai
āṣṭādaṃṣṭraṃ bhavati
yad evāṣṭādaṃṣṭrasya brāhmaṇam
ābhīśavaṃ bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
yad vā adhṛtam abhīśunā tad dādhāra
anutunnaṃ gāyati tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
caturṇidhanam āṅgirasaṃ bhavati catūrātrasya dhṛtyai
svaḥpṛṣṭhaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
sattrāsāhīyaṃ bhavati
yad vā asurāṇām asoḍham āsīt tad devāḥ sattrāsāhīyenāsahanta satrainān asakṣmahīti tat sattrāsāhīyasya sattrāsāhīyatvam
satrā bhrātṛvyaṃ sahate sattrāsāhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
vṛṣaṇvatyo gāyatrayo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ
pibā somam indra mandatu tvā yaṃ te suṣāva haryaśvādriḥ sotur bāhubhyāṃ suyato 'nārvety āyatam iva vai caturtham ahas tasyaiva yatyai
viśvāḥ pṛtanā abhibhūtaraṃ nara ity atijagatī varṣīyaś chanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yajjyāyasaś chandasaḥ kanīyaś chanda upaiti yad eṣā caturthe 'hany atijagatī kriyate 'napabhraṃśāya
yo rājā carṣaṇīnām iti
rājye hy etarhi vāco 'gacchan rājyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
chandobhir vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃ lokam aharan sa nādhriyata taṃ vairājasya nidhanenādṛṃhaṃs tasmāt parāṅ cārvāṅ cādityas tapati parāṅ cārvāṅ cekāraḥ
prastāvaṃ prastutya viṣṭambhān viṣṭabhnoti mukhata eva tad annādyaṃ dhatte mukhaṃ hi sāmnaḥ prastāvaḥ
daśakṛtvo viṣṭabhnoti daśākṣarā virāḍ vairājam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai
triṃśatkṛtvo viṣṭabhnoti bhūyaso 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai
vairājaṃ sāma bhavati virāṭsu stuvanti vairājā viṣṭambhāḥ samīcīr virājo dadhāty annādyāya
anutunnaṃ gāyati retodheyāyānutunnāddhi reto dhīyate
dakṣiṇa ūrāv udgātur agniṃ manthanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyate
upākṛte 'hiṅkṛte manthanti jātam abhihiṅkaroti
tasmājjātaṃ putraṃ paśavo 'bhihiṅkurvanti
tasmai jātāyāmīmāṃsanta gārhapatye praharāmā3 āgnīdhrā3 āhavanīyā3 iti
āhavanīye praharanty etadāyatano vai yajamāno yadāhavanīye svam eva tad āyatanaṃ jyotiṣmat karoti
jyotiṣmān brahmavarcasī bhavati ya evaṃ veda
abhijuhoti śāntyā ājyenābhijuhoti tejo vā ājyaṃ teja eva tad ātman dhatte
preddho agne dīdihi puro na iti virājābhijuhoty annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvaruddhyai
traiśokaṃ brahmasāma bhavati
atijagatīṣu stuvanty ahna utkrāntyā ud vā etenāhnā krāmanti
diveti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano 'pahatyā apa pāpmānaṃ hate traiśokena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
bhāradvājasya pṛśny achāvākasāma bhavati
annaṃ vai devāḥ pṛśnīti vadanty annādyasyāvaruddhyai
iḍābhir aiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
pari priyā divaḥ kavir iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai caturtham ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
tvaṃ hy aṅga daivyeti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
somaḥ punāna ūrmiṇāvyavāraṃ vidhāvati agre vācaḥ pavamānaḥ kanikradad iti
agraṃ hy etarhi vāco 'gacchann agram evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
purojitī vo andhasa iti virājau vairājaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
somaḥ pavate janitā matīnām iti prātassavane ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītaṃ taṃ tṛtīyasavane prajanayanti
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
aurṇāyavaṃ bhavati
aṅgiraso vai sattram āsata teṣām āptaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo loka āsīt panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ na prājānaṃs teṣāṃ kalyāṇa āṅgiraso dhyāyam udavrajat sa ūrṇāyuṃ gandharvam apsarasāṃ madhye preṅkhayamāṇam upait sa iyām iti yāṃ yām abhyadiśat sainam akāmayata tam abhyavadat kalyāṇā3 ity āpto vai vaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ na prajānīthedaṃ sāma svargyaṃ tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam eṣy atha mā tu voco 'ham adarśam iti
sa ait kalyāṇaḥ so 'bravīd āpto vai naḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ na prajānīma idaṃ sāma svargyaṃ tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam eṣyāma iti kas te 'vocad ity aham evādarśam iti tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam āyann ahīyata kalyāṇo 'nṛtaṃ hi so 'vadat sa eṣaḥ śvitraḥ
svargyaṃ vā etat sāma svargalokaḥ puṇyaloko bhavaty aurṇāyavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
bṛhatkaṃ bhavati
sāmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ tvaṃ hīty annādyasyāvaruddhyai hīti vā annaṃ pradīyate ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchati
ātīṣādīyaṃ bhavati
āyur vā ātīṣādīyam āyuṣo 'varuddhyai
ā tamitor nidhanam upayanty āyur eva sarvam āpnuvanti
nānadaṃ bhavati
jyāyo'bhyārambham atihāya pañcamam ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhna ārambhas tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
ṣoḍaśākṣareṇa prastauti ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchati
āndhīgavaṃ bhavati
padyā vā anyā virāḍ akṣaryānyāsmāl lokāt padyayā virājānnādyamavarunddhe 'muṣmād akṣaryayobhayor anayor lokayor annādyam avarunddha āndhīgavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vātsapraṃ bhavati
etasmin vai vairājaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ pratitiṣṭhati vātsapreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vatsaprīr bhālandanaḥ śraddhāṃ nāvindata sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad vātsapram apaśyat sa śraddhām avindata śraddhāṃ vindāmahā iti vai sattram āsate vindate śraddhām
īnidhanaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
agniṃ vo vṛdhantam iti
avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam eva tathā vardhayanti
vayam u tvām apūrvyety apūrvāṃ hy etarhi prajāpates tanūm agacchann apūrvam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
imam indra sutaṃ piba jyeṣṭham amartyaṃ madam iti jyaiṣṭhyaṃ hy etarhi vāco 'gacchan jyaiṣṭhyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati
sindhukṣid vai rājanyarṣir jyog aparuddhaś caran sa etat saindhukṣitam apaśyat so 'vāgacchat pratyatiṣṭhad avagacchati pratitiṣṭhati saindhukṣitena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
saubharaṃ bhavati bṛhatas tejaḥ
pannam iva vai caturtham ahas tad etena bṛhatas tejasottabhnoti saubhareṇa
vasiṣṭhasya priyaṃ bhavati
etena vai vasiṣṭha indrasya premāṇam agacchat premāṇaṃ devatānāṃ gacchati vāsiṣṭhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
indraśca bṛhacca samabhavatāṃ tam indraṃ bṛhad ekayā tanvātyaricyata tasyā abibhedanayā mābhibhaviṣyatīti so 'bravīt ṣoḍaśī te 'yaṃ yajñakratur astv iti sa ṣoḍaśy abhavat tad asya janma
ati śriyā bhrātṛvyaṃ ricyate yo gāyatrīṣu dvipadāsu bṛhatā ṣoḍaśinā stute
upa no haribhiḥ sutam ity etā vai gāyatryo dvipadā etāsu stotavyam
indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etām anuṣṭubham apaharasaṃ prāyacchat tayā nāstṛṇuta yad astṛto vyanadat tan nānadasya nānadatvam
taṃ punar upādhāvat tasmai saptānāṃ hotrāṇāṃ haro nirmāya prāyacchat tam astṛṇuta
stṛṇute taṃ yaṃ tustūrṣate ya evaṃ veda
tasmāddharivatīṣu stuvanti harivatīḥ śaṃsanti harivatīṣu graho gṛhyate haro hy asmai nirmāya prāyacchat
ekaviṃśāyatano vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī sapta hi prātassavane hotrā vaṣaṭkurvanti sapta mādhyandine savane sapta tṛtīyasavane
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
gaurīvitirvā etacchāktyo brahmaṇo 'tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam abhavad atiriktaṃ etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinaṃ śvastanavān bhavaty api prajāyā upakﾱptaḥ
viśālaṃ libujayā bhūtyābhyadhād iti hovācopoditir gopāleyo 'nuṣṭubhi nānadam akar gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinam astoṣṭāñjasā śriyam upāgān na śriyā avapadyata iti
eṣa vai viśālaṃ libujayā bhūtyābhidadhāti yo 'nuṣṭubhi nānadaṃ kṛtvā gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinā stute 'ñjasā śriyam upaiti na śriyā avapadyate
śakvarīṣu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta vajrī syām iti
vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vajraḥ śakvaryo vajreṇaivāsmai vajraṃ spṛṇoti vajrī bhavati
anuṣṭupsu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta na mā vāg ativadet
vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vāg anuṣṭub vajreṇaivāsmai vācaṃ spṛṇoti nainaṃ vāg ativadati
asāvi soma indra ta ity etāsu stotavyam
virāṭsv annādyakāmaḥ ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vairājam annaṃ vajreṇaivāsmā annaṃ spṛṇoty annādo bhavati
pra vo mahe mahe vṛdhe bharadhvam ity etāsu stotavyam
trayastriṃśadakṣarā vā etā virājo yad ekaviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhā sā yad dvādaśa prajātiḥ sā
pratiṣṭhāya prajāyate no cāntasthāyāṃ jīyate ya evaṃ veda
atha vā etā ekapadās tryakṣarā viṣṇoś chando bhurijaḥ śakvaryaḥ
etābhir vā indro vṛtram ahan kṣipraṃ vā etābhiḥ pāpmānaṃ hanti kṣipraṃ vasīyān bhavati
catustriṃśadakṣarāḥ saṃstuto bhavati trayastriṃśad devatāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśo devatānāṃ prajāpatim evopayanty ariṣṭyai
hiraṇyaṃ saṃpradāyaṃ ṣoḍaśinā stuvate jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati
aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa upatiṣṭhati sāmyekṣyāya bhrātṛvyalokam eva sa vidhamaṃs tiṣṭhati
ekākṣaraṃ vai devānām avamaṃ chanda āsīt saptākṣaraṃ paramaṃ navākṣaram asurāṇām avamaṃ chanda āsīt pañcadaśākṣaraṃ paramaṃ devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta tān prajāpatir ānuṣṭubho bhūtvāntarātiṣṭhat taṃ devāsurā vyahvayanta sa devān upāvartata tato devā abhavan parāsurāḥ
bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
te devā asurāṇām ekākṣareṇaiva pañcadaśākṣaram avṛñjata dvyakṣareṇa caturdaśākṣaraṃ tryakṣareṇa trayodaśākṣaraṃ caturakṣareṇa dvādaśākṣaraṃ pañcākṣareṇaikādaśākṣaraṃ ṣaḍakṣareṇa daśākṣaraṃ saptākṣareṇa navākṣaram aṣṭābhir evāṣṭāv avṛñjata
evam eva bhrātṛvyād bhūtiṃ vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
aparuddhayajña iva vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī kanīyasvina iva vai tarhi devā āsan bhūyasvino 'surāḥ kanīyasvinaḥ bhūyasvinaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
yasmād anyo na paro 'sti jāto ya ābabhūva bhuvanāni viśvā
jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati ya evaṃ veda
ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
govit pavasva vasuviddhiraṇyavid iti pañcamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
govid vā etad vasuviddhiraṇyavid yacchakvaryaḥ
paśavaś śakvaryaḥ sarvaṃ paśubhir vindate
tvaṃ suvīro asi soma viśvavid ityeṣa vāva suvīro yasya paśavas tad eva tad abhivadati
tās te kṣarantu madhumad ghṛtaṃ paya iti madhumad vai ghṛtaṃ payaḥ paśavaḥ kṣaranti tad eva tad abhivadati
pavamānasya viśvavid ity anurūpo bhavati
viśvam eva tad vittam abhivadati viśvaṃ hi paśubhir vindate
pra te sargā asṛkṣateti sṛṣṭānīva hyetarhyahāni
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai
saptarcau bhavataḥ chandasāṃ dhṛtyai
caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭaḥ
tava śriyo varṣyasyeva vidyuta ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
śrīr vai paśavaḥ śrīḥ śakvaryaḥ tad eva tad abhivadati
agneś cikitra uṣasām ivetaya itītānīva hyetarhyahānīty ā te yatante rathyo yathā pṛthag ity eva hyetarhyahāni yatante
purūruṇā ciddhy asty avo nūnaṃ vāṃ varuṇeti maitrāvaruṇaṃ yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajati
uttiṣṭhann ojasā sahety aindram
pañca vā ṛtava utthānasya rūpam ojasā sahety ojasaiva vīryeṇa sahottiṣṭhanti
indrāgnī yuvām ima iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yacchakvaryo rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ
arṣā soma dyumattama iti viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti
brahma vai gāyatrī yajño viṣṇur brahmaṇy eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
soma uṣvāṇa stotṛbhir iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaitās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
yat soma citram ukthyam iti gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
yaṇvaṃ bhavati paśavo vai yaṇvaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai
santataṃ gāyati yajñasya saṃtatyai
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
śākalaṃ bhavati
etena vai śakalaḥ pañcame 'hani pratyatiṣṭhat pratitiṣṭhati śākalena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vārśaṃ bhavati
vṛśo vaijānas tryaruṇasya traidhātavasyaikṣvākasya purohita āsīt sa aikṣvāko 'dhāvayat brāhmaṇakumāraṃ rathena vyachinat sa purohitam abravīt tava mā purodhāyām idam īdṛg upāgād iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vārśaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
mānavaṃ bhavati
etena vai manuḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati mānavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ānūpaṃ bhavati
etena vai vadhryaśva ānūpaḥ paśūnāṃ bhūmānam āśnuta paśūnāṃ bhūmānam aśnuta ānūpena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vāmraṃ bhavati
sāmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ yaṃ vai gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ praśaṃsanti vāma iti taṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsanti
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
triṇidhanam āgneyaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
agniḥ sṛṣṭo nodadīpyata taṃ prajāpatir etena sāmnopādhamat sa udadīpyata dīptiś ca vā etat sāma brahmavarcasaṃ ca dīptiṃ caivaitena brahmavarcasaṃ cāvarunddhe
śaiśavaṃ bhavati
śiśur vā āṅgiraso mantrakṛtāṃ mantrakṛd āsīt sa pitṝn putrakā ity āmantrayata taṃ pitaro 'bruvan na dharmaṃ karoṣi yo naḥ pitṝn sataḥ putrakā ity āmantrayasa iti so 'bravīd ahaṃ vāva vaḥ pitāsmi yo mantrakṛd asmīti te deveṣv apṛcchanta te devā abruvann eṣa vāva pitā yo mantrakṛd iti tad vai sa udajayad ujjayati śaiśavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ
indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etacchandobhya indriyaṃ vīryaṃ nirmāya prāyacchad etena śaknuhīti tacchakvarīṇāṃ śakvarītvaṃ sīmānam abhinat tat simā mahnyām akarot tan mahnyā mahān ghoṣa āsīt tan mahānāmnyaḥ
diśaḥ pañcapadā dādhārartūn ṣaṭpadā chandāṃsi saptapadā puruṣaṃ dvipadā
dvyopaśāḥ saṃstutā bhavanti tasmād dvyopaśāḥ paśavaḥ
iḍe abhito 'thakāraṃ tasmācchṛṅge tīkṣṇīyasī stūpāt
upakṣudrā gāyati tasmād upakṣudrāḥ paśavaḥ
asaṃśliṣṭā gāyati tasmād asaṃśliṣṭāḥ paśavaḥ
nānārūpā gāyati tasmān nānārūpāḥ paśavaḥ
āpo vai kṣīrarasā āsaṃste devāḥ pāpavasīyasād abibhayur yad apa upanidhāya stuvate pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyai
vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃ veda
gāyatram ayanaṃ bhavati brahmavarcasakāmasya svarṇidhanaṃ madhunāmuṣmiṃlloka upatiṣṭhate traiṣṭubham ayanaṃ bhavaty ojaskāmasyāthakāraṇidhanam ājyenāmuṣmiṃlloka upatiṣṭhate jāgatam ayanaṃ bhavati paśukāmasyeḍānidhanaṃ payasāmuṣmiṃlloka upatiṣṭhate
añjasāryo mālyaḥ śakvarīḥ prārautsīd iti hovācālammaṃ pārijānataṃ rajanaḥ kauṇeyo yady enāḥ pratiṣṭhāpaṃ śakṣyatīty etad vā etāsām añja etat pratiṣṭhitā ya ābhiḥ kṣipraṃ prastutya kṣipram udgāyati
śakvarībhiḥ stutvā purīṣeṇa stuvate
paśavo vai śakvaryo goṣṭhaḥ purīṣaṃ goṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartayanty avisraṃsāya
indro madāya vāvṛdha ity avardhanta hy etarhi
tāsu bārhadgiram
svādor itthā viṣuvata iti viṣuvān vai pañcamam ahas tāsu rāyovājīyam
indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat teṣāṃ traya udaśiṣyanta pṛthuraśmir bṛhadgirī rāyovājas te 'bruvan ko na imān putrān bhariṣyatīty aham itīndro 'bravīt tān adhinidhāya paricārya caran vardhayaṃs tān vardhayitvābravīt kumārakā varān vṛṇīdhvam iti kṣatraṃ mahyam ity abravīt pṛthuraśmis tasmā etena pārthuraśmena kṣatraṃ prāyacchat kṣatrakāma etena stuvīta kṣatrasyaivāsya prakāśo bhavati brahmavarcasaṃ mahyam ity abravīt bṛhadgiris tasmā etena bārhadgireṇa prāyacchat brahmavarcasakāma etena stuvīta brahmavarcasī bhavati paśūn mahyam ity abravīd rāyovājas tasmā etena rāyovājīyena paśūn prāyacchat paśukāma etena stuvīta paśumān bhavati
pārthuraśmaṃ rājanyāya brahmasāma kuryāt bārhadgiraṃ brāhmaṇāya rāyovājīyaṃ vaiśyāya svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati stomaḥ
asāvy aṃśur madāyeti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
abhi dyumnaṃ bṛhad yaśa ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaityubhau hi varṇāvetad ahaḥ
prāṇā śiśur mahīnām iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ mahyo hi simāḥ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
pavasva vājasātaya iti vaiṣṇavyo 'nuṣṭubho bhavanti
yajño vai viṣṇur yad atra nāpi kriyate tad viṣṇunā yajñenāpi karoti
indur vājī pavate gonyoghā iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
saṃtani bhavati pañcamasyāhnas santatyai
vāg vā eṣā pratatā yad dvādaśāhas tasyā eṣa viṣuvān yat pañcamam ahas tām evaitena saṃtanoti
cyāvanaṃ bhavati
prajātir vai cyāvanaṃ prajāyate bahur bhavati cyāvanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tāṃ prajāpatiś cyāvanenācyāvayad yad acyāvayat taccyāvanasya cyāvanatvaṃ cyāvayati vṛṣṭiṃ cyāvanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
krośaṃ bhavati
etena vā indra indrakrośe viśvāmitrajamadagnī imā gāva ityākrośat paśūnām avaruddhyai krośaṃ kriyate
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
ṛṣabhaḥ śākvaro bhavati
paśavo vai śakvaryaḥ paśuṣveva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
pārthaṃ bhavati
etena vai pṛthī vainya ubhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam āśnutobhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam aśnute pārthena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
aṣṭeḍaḥ padastobho bhavati
indro vṛtrāya vajram udayacchat taṃ ṣoḍaśabhir bhogaiḥ paryabhujat sa etaṃ padastobham apaśyat tenāpāveṣṭayad apaveṣṭayann iva gāyet pāpmano 'pahatyai
pāpmā vāva sa tam agṛhṇāt taṃ padastobhenāpāhatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate padastobhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
pador uttamam apaśyat tat padastobhasya padastobhatvam
dvādaśanidhano bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
dāśaspatyaṃ bhavati
yāṃ vai gāṃ praśaṃsanti dāśaspatyeti tāṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsanti
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
ā te agna idhīmahi iti
apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāyaiva
indrāya sāma gāyateti pūrṇāḥ kakubhas tenānaśanāyuko bhavati
puruṣo vai kakup puruṣam eva tan madhyataḥ prīṇāti
asāvi soma indra ta iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
saṃjayaṃ bhavati
devāś ca vā asurāśca samadadhata yatare naḥ saṃjayāṃs teṣāṃ naḥ paśavo 'sān iti te devā asurān saṃjayena samajayan yat samajayaṃs tasmāt saṃjayaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai saṃjayaṃ kriyate
saumitraṃ bhavati
dīrghajihvī vā idaṃ rakṣo yajñahā yajñiyān avalihaty acarat tām indraḥ kayācana māyayā hantuṃ nāśaṃsatātha ha sumitraḥ kutsaḥ kalyāṇa āsa tam abravīd imām acchābrūṣveti tām acchābrūta sainam abravīn nāhaitanna śuśruva priyam iva tu me hṛdayasyeti tām ajñapayat tāṃ saṃskṛte 'hatāṃ tad vāva tau tarhy akāmayetāṃ kāmasani sāma saumitraṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
sumitraḥ san krūram akar ity enaṃ vāg abhyavadat taṃ śug ārchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etat saumitram apaśyat tena śucam apāhatāpa śucaṃ hate saumitreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
mahāvaiśvāmitraṃ bhavati
pāpmānaṃ hatvā yad amahīyanta tan mahāvaiśvāmitrasya mahāvaiśvāmitratvam
hāyā ihayā ohā oheti paśūn evaitena nyauhanta
trīḍaṃ bhavati trirātrasya dhṛtyai
dravantīm iḍām uttamām upayanti ṣaṣṭhasyāhnaḥ santatyai
triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭaḥ
jyotir yajñasya pavate madhu priyam iti ṣaṣṭhasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
jyotir vai gāyatrī chandasāṃ jyotiḥ revatī sāmnāṃ jyotis trayastriṃśaḥ stomānāṃ jyotir eva tat samyak saṃdadhāty api ha putrasya putro jyotiṣmān bhavati
madhu priyam iti paśavo vai revatyo madhu priyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
madintamo matsara indriyo rasa itīndriyaṃ vai vīryaṃ rasaḥ paśavas tad eva tad abhivadati
asṛkṣata pra vājina ity anurūpo bhavati
sṛṣṭānīva hy etarhy ahāni
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai
daśarcau bhavato daśākṣarā virāṭ vairājam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai
uttaro daśarco bhavati sodarka indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya
yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
dhvasre vai puruṣantī tarantapurumīḍhābhyāṃ vaidadaśvibhyāṃ sahasrāṇy aditsatāṃ tāv aikṣetāṃ kathaṃ nāv idam āttam apratigṛhītaṃ syād iti tau praty etāṃ dhvasrayoḥ puruṣantyor ā sahasrāṇi dadmahe tarat sa mandī dhāvatīti tato vai tat tayor āttam apratigṛhītam abhavat
āttam asyāpratigṛhītaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
vinārāśaṃso bhavaty ubhayasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai mānuṣasya ca daivasya ca
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
imaṃ stomam arhate jātavedasa ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
prati vāṃ sūra udita iti sūravan maitrāvaruṇam
anto vai sūro 'nta etat ṣaṣṭham ahar ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
bhinddhi viśvā apa dviṣa ity aindraṃ sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
yajñasya hi stha ṛtvija ity aindrāgnaṃ sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan stomaḥ
indrāyendo marutvata iti marutvatyo gāyatryo bhavanti
marutvaddhi mādhyandinaṃ savanam
mṛjyamānaḥ suhastya iti simānāṃ rūpam
samānaṃ vai simānāṃ rūpaṃ revatīnāṃ ca simābhyo hy adhi revatyaḥ prajāyante
etam u tyaṃ daśa kṣipa ity ādityā ādityā vā imāḥ prajās tāsām eva madhyataḥ pratitiṣṭhati
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
iṣovṛdhīyaṃ bhavati
paśavo vā iṣovṛdhīyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyā iṣe vai pañcamam ahar vṛdhe ṣaṣṭham avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam evaitena vardhayanti
krauñcaṃ bhavati
kruṅṅ eṣyam ahar avindad eṣyam iva vai ṣaṣṭham ahar ahar evaitena vindanti
vājadāvaryo bhavanti
annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai yadā hi vā annam atha gaur athāśvo 'tha puruṣo vājī
revatyo bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai
ṣaṇṇidhanī ṣaḍrātrasya dhṛtyai
āpo vai revatyas tā yat pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryur apaśur yajamānaḥ syāt paśūn asya nirdaheyur yatra vā āpo vivartante tad oṣadhayo jāyante 'tha yatrāvatiṣṭhante nirmṛtukās tatra bhavanti tasmāt pavamāne kurvanti parācā hi pavamānena stuvate
methī vā iṣovṛdhīyaṃ rajjuḥ krauñcaṃ vatso vājadāvaryo revatyo mātaro yad etāny evaṃ sāmāni kriyanta evam eva prattāṃ dugdhe
aukṣṇorandhre bhavataḥ
ukṣṇorandhro vā etābhyāṃ kāvyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vājajid bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvaṃ vā ete vājaṃ jayanti ye ṣaṣṭham ahar āgacchanti
annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai
varuṇasāma bhavati
etena vai varuṇo rājyam ādhipatyam agacchad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati varuṇasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
aṅgirasāṃ goṣṭho bhavati
paśavo vai revatyo goṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartayanty avisraṃsāya
ihavad vāmadevyaṃ bhavati
etena vai vāmadevo 'nnasya purodhām agacchad annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhānnasyāvaruddhyai
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
marutvatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ
yātayāmāny anyāni chandāṃsy ayātayāmā gāyatrī tasmād gāyatrīṣu stuvanti
surūpakṛtnum ūtaya ity abhyārambheṇa ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
ubhe yad indra rodasī iti ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
revatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati
apāṃ vā eṣa raso yad revatyo revatīnāṃ raso yad vāravantīyaṃ sarasā eva tad revatīḥ prayuṅkte yad vāravantīyena pṛṣṭhena stuvate
revad vā etad raivatyaṃ yad vāravantīyam asya revān raivatyo jāyate
revān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
keśine vā etad dālbhyāya sāmāvirabhavat tad enam abravīd agātāro mā gāyanti mā mayodgāsiṣur iti kathaṃ ta āgā bhagava ity abravīd āgeyam evāsmy āgāyann iva gāyet pratiṣṭhāyai tad alammaṃ pārijānataṃ paścādakṣaṃ śayānam etām āgāṃ gāyantam ajānāt tam abravīt puras tvā dadhā iti tam abruvan ko nv ayaṃ kasmā alam ity alaṃ nu vai mahyam iti tad alammasyālammatvam
iheheti gāyet pratiṣṭhāyai
ṛṣabho raivato bhavati
paśavo vai raivatyaḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
śyeno bhavati
śyeno ha vai pūrvapretāni vayāṃsy āpnoti pūrvapretānīva vai pūrvāṇy ahāni teṣām āptyai śyenaḥ kriyate
śyeno vā etad ahaḥ saṃpārayitum arhati sa hi vayasām āśiṣṭhas tasyānapahananāya sampāraṇāyaitat kriyate 'nto hi ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhaḥ saptamaṃ ca
brahmavādino vadanti yad bṛhadāyatanāni pṛṣṭhāny athaite dve gāyatryau dve jagatyau kva tarhi bṛhatyo bhavantīti
ye dve jagatyoḥ pade te gāyatryā upasaṃpadyete tat sarvā bṛhatyo bhavanty āyatane pṛṣṭhāni yātayatyāyatanavān bhavati
ṣaṭpadāsu stuvanti ṣaḍrātrasya dhṛtyai
saptapadayā yajati saptamasyāhnaḥ santatyai stomaḥ
parisvāno giriṣṭhā iti parivatyo gāyatryo bhavanti sarvasya paryāptyai
samunveyo vasūnām iti paśavo vai vasu paśūnām avaruddhyai
taṃ vaḥ sakhāyo madāyeti vālakhilyāḥ
vālakhilyāv etau tṛcau ṣaṣṭhe cāhani saptame ca
yad etau vālakhilyau tṛcau bhavato 'hnor eva vyatiṣaṅgāyāvyavasraṃsāya santatyai
somāḥ pavanta indava ity anuṣṭubho nibhasado bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai
ayā pavā pavasvainā vasūnīti triṣṭubhas satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
vaidanvatāni bhavanti
vidanvān vai bhārgava indrasya pratyahaṃs taṃ śug ārchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etāni vaidanvatāny apaśyat taiḥ śucam apāhatāpa śucaṃ hate vaidanvatais tuṣṭuvānaḥ
bharadvājasya loma bhavati paśavo vai loma paśūnām avaruddhyai
tad u dīrgham ity āhur āyur vai dīrgham āyuṣo 'varuddhyai
kārṇaśravasaṃ bhavati śṛṇvanti tuṣṭuvānam
karṇaśravā vā etad āṅgirasaḥ paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
madhuścyunnidhanaṃ bhavati
paramasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai paramaṃ vā etad annādyaṃ yan madhu
prajāpater vā etau stanau yad ghṛtaścyunnidhanaṃ ca madhuścyunnidhanaṃ ca yajño vai prajāpatis tam etābhyāṃ dugdhe yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ dugdhe
krauñce bhavataḥ
kruṅṅ eṣyam ahar avindad eṣyamiva vai ṣaṣṭham ahar aharevaitābhyām vindati
śnauṣṭaṃ bhavati
śnuṣṭir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāt lokānna cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
agner vā etad vaiśvānarasya sāma dīdihīti nidhanam upayanti dīdāyeva hy agnir vaiśvānaraḥ
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
brahmavādino vadanti prāyaṇato dvipadāḥ kāryā udayanatā3 iti
udayanata eva kāryāḥ puruṣo vai dvipadāḥ pratiṣṭhāyai
vācā vai sarvaṃ yajñaṃ tanvate tasmāt sarvāṃ vācaṃ puruṣo vadati sarvā hy asmin saṃstutā pratitiṣṭhati
gūrdo bhavati
gaupāyanānāṃ vai sattram āsīnānāṃ kirātakulyāv asuramāye antaḥparidhy asūn prākiratāṃ te agne tvaṃ no antama ity agnim upāsīdaṃs tenāsūn aspṛṇvaṃs tad vāva te tarhy akāmayanta kāmasani sāma gūrdaḥ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
gotamasya bhadraṃ bhavati
āśiṣam evāsmā etenāśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ
etena vai gotamo jemānaṃ mahimānam agacchat tasmād ye ca parāñco gotamād ye cārvāñcas ta ubhaye gotamā ṛṣayo bruvate
udvaṃśaputro bhavati
yad vā udvaṃśīyaṃ tad udvaṃśaputraḥ
ardheḍām atisvarati
tasmād ūdhar dhārā atikṣarantīḍāyām antataḥ paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
kﾱpta upariṣṭād ṛk sāma ca vimucyete abhy u svareṇa saptamam ahaḥ svarati santatyai
ūhuṣīva vā etarhi vāg yadā ṣaḍahaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate na bahu vaden nānyaṃ pṛcchen nānyasmai prabrūyāt
madhu vāśayed ghṛtaṃ vā yathohuṣo vahaṃ pratyanakti tathā tat
trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
āpyante vā etat stomāś chandāṃsi yat ṣaḍaha āpyate
āpte ṣaḍahe chandāṃsi stomān kṛtvā prayanti
pra kāvyam uśaneva bruvāṇa iti gāyatryā rūpeṇa prayanti
iyaṃ vai gāyatry asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya prayanti
triṣṭup pratipad bhavati
ojo vīryaṃ triṣṭub ojasyeva vīrye parākramya prayanti
stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai
harivatyo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
dvādaśarcau bhavataḥ
dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram eva tatpūrvasmai ṣaḍahāya pratyudyacchati savīvadhatāyai
caturviṃśatir bhavanti caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram eva tatpūrvasmai ṣaḍahāya pratyudyacchati savīvadhatāyai
dṛta aindrota iti hovācābhipratārī kākṣasenir ye mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ gacchanti kva te tato bhavanti pra rājan pakṣiṇaḥ patanty avāpakṣāḥ padyante
ye vai vidvāṃsas te pakṣiṇo ye 'vidvāṃsas te 'pakṣās trivṛtpañcadaśāv eva stomau pakṣau kṛtvā svargaṃ lokaṃ prayanti
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
mūrdhānaṃ divo aratim pṛthivyā ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
mūrdhā vā eṣa divo yas tṛtīyas trirātraḥ
vaiśvānaram ṛta ājātam agnim iti vaiśvānara iti vā agneḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainaṃ tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati
pra vo mitrāya gāyateti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ maitrāvaruṇaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī vai mitrāvaruṇayoḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainau tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati
indrāyāhi citrabhānav ity ārbhavam aindram ṛbhavo vā indrasya priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainaṃ tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati
tam īḍiṣva yo arciṣety aniruktam aindrāgnaṃ devatānām anabhidharṣāyottamārdhe nirāha devatānām apraṇāśāya stomaḥ
vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti gāyatrī bhavatyahno dhṛtyai
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hyetad ahaḥ
punānaḥ soma dhārayeti dhṛtyai
