pro ayāsīd indur indrasya niṣkṛtam iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṣeṇyam iva hyetad ahaḥ
jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
saṃtani bhavati saptamasyāhnaḥ santatyai
yathā vai vyokasau vipradravata evam ete ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhaḥ saptamaṃ ca vipradravatas tau yathā samānīya saṃyujyād evam evaite etena sāmnā saṃyunakti
sauparṇaṃ bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
yajño vai devebhyo 'pākrāmat sa suparṇarūpaṃ kṛtvācarat taṃ devā etaiḥ sāmabhirārabhanta yajña iva vā eṣa yacchandomā yajñasyaivaiṣa ārambhaḥ
rohitakūlīyaṃ bhavaty ājijityāyai
etena vai viśvāmitro rohitābhyāṃ rohitakūla ājim ajayat
viśvāmitro bharatānām anasvatyāyāt so 'dantibhir nāma janatayāṃśaṃ prāsyatemāṃ māṃ yūyaṃ vasnikāṃ jayāthemāni mahyaṃ yūyaṃ pūrayātha yadīmāvidaṃ rohitāvaśmācitaṃ kūlam udvahāta iti sa ete sāmanī apaśyat tābhyāṃ yuktvā prāsedhat sa udajayat
ājir vā eṣa pratato yad dvādaśāhas tasyaite ujjityai
kaṇvarathantaraṃ bhavati
tejo vā etad rathantarasya yat kaṇvarathantaram sarasam eva tad rathantaraṃ prayuṅkte yat kaṇvarathantareṇa saptame 'hani stuvate
jāmi dvādaśāhasyāstīti ha smāhogradevo rājanir bārhataṃ ṣaṣṭham ahar bārhataṃ saptamaṃ yat kaṇvarathantaraṃ bhavati tenājāmi
gauṅgavaṃ bhavati
agnir akāmayatānnādaḥ syām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad gauṅgavam apaśyat tenānnādo 'bhavad yad annaṃ vitvā agardad yad agaṅgūyat tad gauṅgavasya gauṅgavatvam annādyasyāvaruddhyai gauṅgavaṃ kriyate
yat sāma devatāḥ praśaṃsati tena yajamānāḥ satyāśiṣaḥ satyāśiṣo 'sāmeti vai sattram āsate satyāśiṣa eva bhavanti
āyāsyaṃ bhavati tiraścīnanidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai
ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annam āśnāt sa vyabhraṃśata sa etāny āyāsyāny apaśyat tair ātmānaṃ samaśrīṇād vibhraṣṭam iva vai saptamam ahar yad etat sāma bhavaty ahar eva tena saṃśrīṇāti
pravadbhargavaṃ bhavati
pravatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyannudvatodāyan
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavantyahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
vayaṃ gha tvā sutāvanta iti satobṛhatyo varṣīyaśchanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
nakiṣṭaṃ karmaṇā naśad iti bṛhatyaḥ satyo 'bhyārambheṇa jagatyaḥ
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yajjyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etā abhyārambheṇa jagatyo bhavanty ahna eva pratyuttambhāya
abhinidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ bhavati
abhinidhanena vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat tam astṛṇuta stṛṇute bhrātṛvyam abhinidhanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vaikhānasaṃ bhavati
vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsaṃs tān rahasyur devamalimluḍ munimaraṇe 'mārayat taṃ devā abruvan kva tarṣayo 'bhūvann iti tān praiṣam aicchat tān nāvindat sa imān lokān ekadhāreṇāpunāt tān munimaraṇe 'vindat tān etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vaikhānasaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe stomaḥ
yas te mado vareṇya iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
eṣa sya dhārayā suta iti kakubhaḥ satyo 'bhyārambheṇa triṣṭubhaḥ
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yat jyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etā abhyārambheṇa triṣṭubho bhavanty ahna eva pratyuttambhāya
sakhāya āniṣīdateti vālakhilyā vālakhilyāv etau tṛcau ṣaṣṭhe cāhani saptame ca yad etau vālakhilyau tṛcau bhavato 'hnor eva vyatiṣaṅgāyāvyavasraṃsāya santatyai
purojitī vo andhasa iti virāḍ annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvaruddhyai
pra vājy akṣār ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtiḥ
atho etaddhyevaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ kriyante
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā ity etacchandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt
ye somāsaḥ parāvatīti parāvatam iva vā etarhi yajño gatas tam evaitenānvicchanti
gāyatryaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
dakṣaṇidhanaṃ bhavati
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmāt sṛṣṭā abalā ivācchadayaṃs tāsv etena sāmnā dakṣāyety ojo vīryam adadhād yad etat sāma bhavaty oja eva vīryam ātman dhatte
śārkaraṃ bhavati
indraṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny astuvan sa śarkaraṃ śiśumārarṣim upetyābravīt stuhi meti so 'paḥ praskandann abravīd etāvato 'haṃ tvāṃ stuyām iti tasmād apāṃ vegam avejayat sa hīna ivāmanyata sa etat sāmāpaśyat tenāpo 'nusamāśnuta tad vāva sa tarhyakāmayata kāmasani sāma śārkaraṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
plavo bhavati
samudraṃ vā ete prasnāntīty āhur ye dvādaśāham upayantīti yo vā aplavaḥ samudraṃ prasnāti na sa tata udeti yat plavo bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
ativiśvāni duritā taremeti yad evaiṣāṃ duṣṭutaṃ duśśastaṃ tad etena taranti
ekādaśākṣaraṇidhano bhavaty ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub ojovīryaṃ triṣṭub ojasy eva vīrye pratitiṣṭhati
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
kārtayaśaṃ bhavati
hīti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano 'pahatyai
apa pāpmānaṃ hate kārtayaśena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
sauhaviṣaṃ bhavati
suhavir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā iti puruṣaś chandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadā chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
jarābodhīyaṃ bhavaty annādyasyāvaruddhyai
annaṃ vai jarābodhīyaṃ mukhaṃ gāyatrī mukha eva tad annaṃ dhatte 'nnam atti
annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
iḍāntāḥ pāvamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍāḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
ā te vatso mano yamad ity apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāyaiva
tvaṃ na indrābhareti pūrṇāḥ kakubhaḥ
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yajjyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etāḥ pūrṇāḥ kakubho bhavanty anapabhraṃśāya
yad indra citraṃ ma iha nāsti tvādātam adrivo rādhas tanno vidadvasa ubhayāhastyābhareti rāddhim evaitenāvarunddhe
vātsaṃ bhavati
vatsaś ca vai medhātithiś ca kāṇvāv āstāṃ taṃ vatsaṃ medhātithir ākrośad abrāhmaṇo 'si śūdrāputra iti so 'bravīd ṛtenāgniṃ vyayāva yataro nau brahmīyān iti vātsena vatso vyain maidhātithena medhātithis tasya na loma ca nauṣat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vātsaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
sauśravasaṃ bhavati
upagur vai sauśravasaḥ kutsasyauravasya purohita āsīt sa kutsaḥ paryaśapad ya indraṃ yajātā iti sa indraḥ suśravasam upetyābravīd yajasva māśanāyāmi vā iti tam ayajata sa indraḥ puroḍāśahastaḥ kutsam upetyābravīd ayakṣata mā kva te pariśaptam abhūd iti kas tvā yaṣṭeti suśravā iti sa kutsa aurava upagoḥ sauśravasasyodgāyata audumbaryā śiro 'chinat sa suśravā indram abravīt tvattanād vai medam īdṛg upāgād iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma sauśravasaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
vīṅkaṃ bhavati
cyavano vai dādhīco 'śvinoḥ priya āsīt so 'jīryat tam etena sāmnāpsu vyaiṅkayatāṃ taṃ punaryuvānam akurutāṃ tad vāva tau tarhy akāmayetāṃ kāmasani sāma vīṅkaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
śiśuṃ jajñānaṃ haryataṃ mṛjantīty aṣṭamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
śiśur iva vā eṣa saptamenāhnā jāyate tam aṣṭamenāhnā mṛjanti
stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai
harivatyo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
navarcā bhavanti
pañcarco bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai
vāṇavān bhavaty anto vai vāṇo 'nta etad aṣṭamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
trayas tṛcā bhavanti prāṇāpānānāṃ santatyai
catuścatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavatyojasyeva tadvīrye pratitiṣṭhatyojovīryaṃ triṣṭup
agniṃ vo devam agnibhiḥ sajoṣā ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
agnibhir ity eva pūrvāṇy ahāni abhisamiddhānyaṣṭamam ahar abhisaminddhe
mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha iti bārhataṃ maitrāvaruṇam
ugragādham iva vā etad yacchandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya
tam indraṃ vājayāmasītyaindram
aṣṭamena vai devā ahnendram avājayan navamena pāpmānam aghnann ahar evaitena vājayanti
indre agnā namo bṛhad iti bārhatam aindrāgnam
ugragādham iva vā etad yacchandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya stomaḥ
adhvaryo adribhiḥ sutam iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
abhi somāsa āyava ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥ
dhartā divaḥ pavate kṛtvyo rasa ity adhṛta iva vā eṣas tryaho yad dharteti dhṛtyā eva
jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubho loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
vairūpaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai vairūpaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai virūpaḥ saṃvatsaro virūpam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai
āśu bhārgavaṃ bhavati
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā āśunābhyadhinvaṃs tad āśor āśutvam
mārgīyavaṃ bhavati
devaṃ vā etaṃ mṛgayur iti vadanty etena vai sa ubhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam āśnutobhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam aśnute mārgīyaveṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
saumitraṃ bhavati
yad eva saumitrasya brāhmaṇam
aiṭataṃ bhavati
iḍhan vā etena kāvyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
sākamaśvaṃ bhavati yad eva sākamaśvasya brāhmaṇam
tad u dhurāṃ sāmety āhuḥ prāṇā vai dhuraḥ prāṇānām avaruddhyai
vilambasauparṇaṃ bhavati
ātmā vā eṣa sauparṇānāṃ yad aṣṭame 'hani pakṣāv etāv abhito bhavato ye saptamanavamayor vīva vā antarātmā pakṣau lambate yadantarātmā pakṣau vilambate tasmād vilambasauparṇam
svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai sauparṇaṃ kriyate
dvihiṃkāraṃ vāmadevyaṃ bhavatyannādyasyāvaruddhyai
dvitīyaṃ hy etad rūpaṃ yac chandomāḥ
paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn saṃdadhāti
gāyatrapārśvaṃ bhavati
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā gāyatrapārśvena samatanvaṃs tasmād gāyatrapārśvam
trirātro yad vyaśīryata tam etaiḥ sāmabhir abhiṣajyan gāyatrapārśvenopāyacchan santaninā samatanvan saṃkṛtinā samaskurvan pratiṣṭhitau pūrvau trirātrāv apratiṣṭhita eṣa yad etāny eva sāmāni kriyanta etasyaiva pratiṣṭhityai
pauruhanmanaṃ bhavati
puruhanmā vā etena vaikhānaso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
abhyāghātyaṃ bhavaty abhyāghātyasāmāno hi chandomāḥ
dvaigataṃ bhavati
dvigad vā etena bhārgavo dviḥ svargaṃ lokam agacchad āgatya punar agacchat dvayoḥ kāmayor avaruddhyai dvaigataṃ kriyate
hārāyaṇaṃ bhavati
indras tejaskāmo haraskāmas tapo 'tapyata sa etaddhārāyaṇam apaśyat tena tejo haro 'vārunddha tejasvī harasvī bhavati hārāyaṇena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
achidraṃ bhavati
yad vā etasyāhnaś chidram āsīt tad devā acchidreṇāpyauhaṃs tad acchidrasyācchidratvam
bārhadukthaṃ bhavati
bṛhaduktho vā etena vāmneyo 'nnasya purodhām agacchad annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhānnādyasyāvaruddhyai
udvad bhārgavaṃ bhavati
pravatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyann udvatodāyan
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
ka īṃ veda sute saceti satobṛhatyaḥ
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yas saptame 'hani satobṛhatyo bhavanti nāṣṭame tasmād aṣṭame kāryā anapabhraṃśāya
tadāhuḥ śithilam iva vā etacchando yat satobṛhatītyeṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā bṛhatī yā punaḥpadā yad indra prāg apāg udag iti diśāṃ vimarśaḥ pratiṣṭhityai
tāsu naipātithaṃ brahmasāma
sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāllokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ubhayaṃ śṛṇavacca neti
yacca pṛṣṭhāni yāni caitānyahāni teṣām ubhayeṣāṃ santatyai
tāsu vaiyaśvam
vyaśvo vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyā etat pṛṣṭhānām antataḥ kriyate stomaḥ
pavasva deva āyuṣag indraṃ gacchatu te mada iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
abhi dyumnaṃ bṛhad yaśa ityamīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saharūpam upaityubhau hi varṇāvetadahaḥ
prāṇā śiśur mahīnām iti prāṇavatyo bhavanti prāṇān eva tad yajamāne dadhāti
abhī no vājasātamam ityabhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
pavasva soma mahān samudra ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtir atho etaddhyevaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ kriyante brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāśchandāṃsyāpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā ity etacchandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt
hinvanti sūram usraya iti gāyatryaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmājjagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
svāśirām arko bhavati
annaṃ vā arko 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai prāṇā vai svāśiraḥ prāṇānām avaruddhyai
surūpaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai surūpaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai
bhāsaṃ bhavati bhāti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
padanidhanaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
svarbhānur vā āsura ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat sa na vyarocata tasyātrir bhāsena tamo 'pāhan sa vyarocata yad vai tadbhā abhavat tad bhāsasya bhāsatvam
tama iva vā etāny ahāni yacchandomās tebhya etena sāmnā vivāsayati
kākṣīvataṃ bhavati
kakṣīvān vā etenauśijaḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati kākṣīvatena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
āsitaṃ bhavati
asito vā etena daivalas trayāṇāṃ lokānāṃ dṛṣṭim apaśyat trayāṇāṃ kāmānām avaruddhyā āsitaṃ kriyate
aiṣiraṃ bhavati prajātirvā aiṣirāṇi prajāyate bahurbhavatyaiṣireṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
traitaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
padanidhanaṃ rāthantaraṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
nāthavindu sāma vindate nāthaṃ nāthavindūny etānyahāni yat chandomā nātham evaitair vindate
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
kautsaṃ bhavati
etena vai kutso 'ndhaso vipānam apaśyat sa ha sma vai surādṛtinopavasathaṃ dhāvayaty ubhayasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai kautsaṃ kriyate
śuddhāśuddhīyaṃ bhavati
indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat so 'śuddho 'manyata sa etacchuddhāśuddhīyam apaśyat tenāśudhyacchudhyati śuddhāśuddhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
krauñcaṃ bhavati yad eva krauñcasya brāhmaṇaṃ yat dvitīye 'hani
rayiṣṭhaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai rayiṣṭhaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai
audalaṃ bhavati
udalo vā etena vaiśvāmitraḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavatyaudalena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā iti puruṣachandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadāś chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
viśoviśīyaṃ bhavati
agnir akāmayata viśo viśo 'tithis syāṃ viśo viśa ātithyam aśnuvīyeti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad viśoviśīyam apaśyat tena viśo viśo 'tithir abhavat viśo viśa ātithyam āśnuta viśo viśo 'tithir bhavati viśo viśa ātithyam aśnute viśoviśīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
iḍāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍā paśavaśchandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
preṣṭhaṃ vo atithim ityātithyasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
aindra no gadhi priya itīndriyasya vīryasyāvaruddhyai
purāṃ bhindur yuvā kavir amitaujā ajāyatendro viśvasya karmaṇo dhartā vajrī puruṣṭuta iti dhṛtyā eva
auśanaṃ bhavati
uśanā vai kāvyo 'kāmayata yāvān itareṣāṃ kāvyānāṃ lokas tāvantaṃ spṛṇuyām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad auśanam apaśyat tena tāvantaṃ lokam aspṛṇod yāvān itareṣāṃ kāvyānām āsīt tad vāva sa tarhyakāmayata kāmasani sāmauśanaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarunddhe
sāṃvartaṃ bhavati
devānāṃ vai yajñaṃ rakṣāṃsyajighāṃsaṃs tānyetena indraḥ saṃvartam apāvapad yat saṃvartam apāvapat tasmāt sāṃvartaṃ pāpmā vāva sa tān asacata taṃ sāṃvartenāpāghnatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate sāṃvartena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
mārutaṃ bhavati
māsā vai raśmayo maruto raśmayo maruto vai devānāṃ bhūyiṣṭhā bhūyiṣṭhā asāmeti vai sattram āsate bhūyiṣṭhā eva bhavantyṛtumanti pūrvāṇyahāny anṛtavaḥ chandomā yad etat sāma bhavati tenaitāny ahāny ṛtumanti bhavanti
catuścatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavatyojasyeva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ triṣṭup
akrān samudraḥ parame vidharmann iti navamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
paramaṃ vā etad ahar vidharma vidharma vā etad anyair aharbhir ahar yan navamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ hi variṣṭham
matsi vāyum iṣṭaye rādhase na iti vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇati tad eva tad avayajati
stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avaruddhyai
daśarco bhavati daśākṣarā virāṭ vairājam annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai
saprabhṛtayo bhavantīndriyasya vīryasya rasasyānaticārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
aṣṭarco bhavati
aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśas tat paśūn āpnoti aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarunddhe
ṣaḍṛcā bhavanty ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyai
catvāraḥ ṣaḍṛcā bhavanti caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati
savān uttamaḥ ṣaḍṛco bhavaty ubhayasya parokṣapratyakṣasyāvaruddhyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
aṣṭācatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
aganma mahā namasā yaviṣṭham ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
gacchantīva vā ete ye navamam ahar gacchanti
yo dīdāya samiddha sve duroṇa iti dīdāyeva hy eṣa yo navabhir aharbhis tuṣṭuvānaḥ svāhutam iti svāhuto hy eṣa yo navabhir aharbhir āhuto viśvataḥ pratyañcam iti viśvato hy eṣa pratyaṅ
tvaṃ varuṇa uta mitro agna iti vāruṇyeṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇati tad eva tad avayajati
mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣam iti rāthantaraṃ maitrāvaruṇam
ugragādham iva vā etad yacchandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya
mahāṃ indro ya ojasetyaindram aṣṭamena vai devā ahnendram avājayan navamena pāpmānam aghnann ahar evaitena mahayanti
tā huve yayor idam iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
ugragādham iva vā etad yacchandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya stomaḥ
pavamānasya jighnato hareś candrā asṛkṣateti harivatyo gāyatryo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
pavamānasya jighnata iti vai bṛhato rūpaṃ hareś candrā asṛkṣateti jagatyā ubhayoḥ saharūpam upaiti sāmnaś ca chandasaś ca
parīto ṣiñcatā sutam iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai navamam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
asāvi somo aruṣo vṛṣā harir iti jagatyas satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
bharadvājasyādārasṛd bhavati
divodāsaṃ vai bharadvājapurohitaṃ nānājanāḥ paryayatanta sa upāsīdad ṛṣe gātuṃ me vindeti tasmā etena sāmnā gātum avindad gātuvid vā etatsāmānena dāre nāsṛnmeti tad adārasṛto 'dārasṛttvaṃ vindate gātuṃ na dāre dhāvaty adārasṛtā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
surūpaṃ bhavati yad eva surūpasya brāhmaṇam
hariśrīnidhanaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai hariśriyaḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai śriyaṃ ca haraś copaiti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati yad eva saindhukṣitasya brāhmaṇam
gatanidhanaṃ bābhravaṃ bhavati gatyai
babhrur vā etena kaumbhyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
iḍānāṃ saṃkṣāro bhavati
paśavo vā iḍā paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti
ṛṣabhaḥ pāvamāno bhavati
paśavo vai chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati
pṛṣṭhaṃ vā etad ahnāṃ yan navamaṃ pṛṣṭha eva tat pṛṣṭhena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
kaulmalabarhiṣaṃ bhavati
kulmalabarhir vā etena svargaṃ lokam apaśyat prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati kaulmalabarhiṣeṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
arkapuṣpaṃ bhavati
annaṃ vai devā arka iti vadanti rasam asya puṣpam iti sarasam evānnādyam avarunddhe 'rkapuṣpeṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
dairghyaśravasaṃ bhavati
dīrghaśravā vai rājanya ṛṣir jyog aparuddho 'śanāyaṃś caran sa etad dairghaśravasam apaśyat tena sarvābhyo digbhyo 'nnādyam avārunddha sarvābhyo digbhyo 'nnādyam avarunddhe dairghaśravasena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vaiyaśvaṃ bhavati yad eva vaiyaśvasya brāhmaṇam
ābhīśavaṃ yad ābhīśavasya
devasthānaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai saṃskṛti bhavati saṃskṛtyai
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā devasthāne tiṣṭhantaḥ saṃkṛtinā samaskurvaṃs tat saṃkṛteḥ saṃkṛtitvaṃ devasthānena vai devāḥ svarge loke pratyatiṣṭhan svarge loke pratiṣṭhām ety etat
varuṇāya devatā rājyāya nātiṣṭhanta sa etad devasthānam apaśyat tato vai tās tasmai rājyāyātiṣṭhanta tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya
kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
bhargo bhargeṇa tuṣṭuvāno bhavati yaśo yaśasā
vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati yad eva vāsiṣṭhasya brāhmaṇam
dīrghatamaso 'rko bhavaty annaṃ vā arko 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai
sāmarājaṃ bhavati sāmrājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati sāmarājñā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
tad u saṃvad ity āhuḥ saṃvatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyann udvatodāyan
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
śrāyanta iva sūryam iti sūryavatyo bhavanti
ādityadevatyaṃ hy etad ahar anto vai sūro 'nta etan navamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
yata indra bhayāmahe tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi maghavañchagdhi tava tan na ūtaye vidviṣo vimṛdho jahīti dviṣaścaiva mṛdhaśca navamenāhnā vihatya daśamenāhnottiṣṭhanti
śrīr vai śrāyantīyaṃ śrīr navamam ahaḥ śriyam eva tacchriyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
samantaṃ bhavati
samantena paśukāmaḥ stuvīta purodhākāmaḥ samantena stuvīta
āgneyī pṛthivyāgneyo brāhmaṇa aindrī dyaur aindro rājanyo 'ntarikṣeṇa dyāvāpṛthivī samante antarikṣeṇaivainaṃ samantaṃ karoti vindate paśūn pra purodhām āpnoti ya evaṃ vidvān samantena stuvate stomaḥ
tvaṃ somāsi dhārayur iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
tvaṃ hyaṅga daivyeti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
pavasva devavītaya iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
parityaṃ haryataṃ harim iti parivatyo bhavantyanto vai navamam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
pavasva soma mahe dakṣāyetyakṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtir atho etaddhyevaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmāḥ kriyante brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃchandasaś chandomā ity etacchandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt
upoṣu jātam apturam iti gāyatryas satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāt jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
āśvasūktaṃ bhavati
agniṃ vai pūrvair aharbhir ājuhoty athaitad ādityadevatyam ahaḥ śukra āhuta ity asau vā ādityaḥ śukras tam evaitenājuhoti
śāmmadaṃ bhavati
śammad vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
dāvasunidhanaṃ bhavati
āśiṣam evāsmā etenāśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ
dāvasur vā etad āṅgirasaḥ paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjat yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai
pratīcīneḍaṃ kāśītaṃ bhavati
parācībhir vā anyābhir iḍābhī reto dadhadety athaitat pratīcīneḍaṃ kāśītaṃ prajātyai tasmāt parāñco garbhāḥ sambhavanti pratyañcaḥ prajāyante tasmād u te 'vācīnabilebhyo nāvapadyanta etena hy eva te dhṛtāḥ
hāviṣkṛtaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai kṛtānuvāda eva saḥ
sauparṇaṃ bhavati yad eva sauparṇasya brāhmaṇam
vaiśvamanasaṃ bhavati
viśvamanasaṃ vā ṛṣim adhyāyam udvrajitaṃ rakṣo 'gṛhṇāt tam indro 'cāyad ṛṣiṃ vai rakṣo 'grahīd iti tam abhyavadad ṛṣe kas tvaiṣa iti sthāṇur iti brūhīti rakṣo 'bravīt sa sthāṇur ity abravīt tasmai vā etena praharety asmā iṣīkāṃ vajraṃ prayacchann abravīt tenāsya sīmānam abhinat saiṣendreṇateṣīkā pāpmā vāva sa tam agṛhṇāt taṃ vaiśvamanasenāpāhatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate vaiśvamanasena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
nihavo bhavaty annādyasyāvaruddhyai
hīti vā annaṃ pradīyata ītyagnir annam atti
ṛṣayo vā indraṃ pratyakṣaṃ nāpaśyan sa vasiṣṭho 'kāmayata katham indraṃ pratyakṣaṃ paśyeyam iti sa etaṃ nihavam apaśyat tato vai sa indraṃ pratyakṣam apaśyat sa enam abravīd brāhmaṇaṃ te vakṣyāmi yathā tvatpurohitā bharatāḥ prajaniṣyante 'tha mānyebhya ṛṣibhyo mā pravoca iti tasmā etān stomabhāgān abravīt tato vai vasiṣṭhapurohitā bharatāḥ prājāyanta sendraṃ vā etat sāma yad etat sāma bhavati sendratvāya
yadvāhiṣṭhīyaṃ bhavati
brahmayaśasaṃ vā etāni sāmāny ṛcā śrotrīyāṇi brahmayaśasī bhavati yadvāhiṣṭhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
āsitaṃ bhavati yad evāsitasya brāhmaṇam
sādhraṃ bhavati siddhyai
ākūpāraṃ bhavati
akūpāro vā etena kaśyapo jemānaṃ mahimānam agacchajjemānaṃ mahimānaṃ gacchaty ākūpāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vidharma bhavati dharmasya vidhṛtyai
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsyāpyante kiṃchandasaśchandomā iti puruṣacchandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadā chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
śrudhyaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai śrudhyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai
prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān etena sāmnā śrūdhiyā ehiyety anvahvayat ta enam upāvartanta yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnām upāvṛttyai
upainaṃ paśava āvartante ya evaṃ veda
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyantīḍāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍā paśavaśchandomāḥ paśuṣveva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
āgneyīṣu pūrveṣām ahnām ukthāni praṇayantyathaitasyāhna āgneyyaindryāṃ praṇayantyubhayor eva rūpayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati
aidhmavāhaṃ bhavati
āgneyyaindrīṣu stuvanti brahma caiva tat kṣatraṃ ca sayujīkaroti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhāti brāhmaṇe kṣatraṃ ca viśaṃ cānuge karoti
traikakubhaṃ bhavati
ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ traikakubham
udvaṃśīyaṃ bhavati yad evodvaṃśīyasya brāhmaṇam
aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
gāyatraṃ vai saptamam ahas traiṣṭubham aṣṭamaṃ jāgataṃ navamam athaitad ānuṣṭubham ahar yad daśamam
tad āhur yad anuṣṭubhaṃ stomyāṃ pratyakṣam upeyuḥ parāṃ parāvataṃ yajamāno gacchen na pratitiṣṭhed iti yā vai caturviṃśatir gāyatryas tā aṣṭādaśānuṣṭubho 'nuṣṭubham eva tat stomyāṃ parokṣam upayanti pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
prajāpatiṃ vā etenāhnā pariveviṣati tanna vyavavadyaṃ yad vai śreṣṭhe pariviṣyamāṇo vadaty annādyasya so 'vagrahas tasmān na vyavavadyam annādyasyānavagrāhāya
tad u vyavavadyaṃ yathā śreṣṭhāya baliṃ hriyamāṇaṃ panthānaṃ paryanuvedayati gatyai tathā tat
yāvaty anuṣṭup tāvatīṃ vācaṃ sampādya vibrūyus tad v anatiriktaṃ svasyo caiva yajñasyāriṣṭyai
abhi vā ete devān ārohantīty āhur ye daśabhir aharbhiḥ stuvata iti pañcānām ahnām anurūpaiḥ pratyavayanti yathābhyāruhya pratyavarohet tathā tan navarco bhavati yā evāmūḥ prayacchan yā avadadhāti tā etā udasyati
vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajaty ādityaiṣā bhavatīyaṃ vā aditir asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
suṣamiddho na āvahety āpriya ājyāni bhavanti
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno 'manyata sa etāny āpriya ājyāny apaśyat tair ātmānam āprīṇāt dugdha iva vā eṣa riricāno yo daśabhir aharbhis tuṣṭuvāno yad etāny āpriya ājyāni bhavanty ātmānam evaitair āprīṇāti
yad adya sūra udita iti sūravan maitrāvaruṇam anto vai sūro 'nta etad daśamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyā ut tvā madantu somā ity udvad aindram utthānasya rūpam
indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti stomaḥ
uccā te jātam andhasa ity udvatyo gāyatryo bhavanty utthānasya rūpam
punānas soma dhārayeti panthānam eva tat paryavayanti
ā jāgṛvir vipra ṛtaṃ matīnām iti yad āpte pravatīḥ kuryur atipadyeran yad āvatyo bhavanty anatipādāya
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kﾱptiś cānnādyaṃ ca kﾱptiṃ caivaitenānnādyaṃ cābhyuttiṣṭhanti
ājigaṃ bhavaty ājijityāyai
ājir vā eṣa pratato yat dvādaśāhas tasyaitad ujjityai
ābhīkaṃ bhavaty abhikrāntyai
aṅgirasas tapas tepānāḥ śucam aśocaṃs ta etat sāmāpaśyaṃs tān abhīke 'bhyavarṣat tena śucam aśamayanta yad abhīke 'bhyavarṣat tasmād ābhīkaṃ yām eva pūrvair aharbhiḥ śucaṃ śocanti tām etenātra śamayitvottiṣṭhanti
utsedho bhavati
utsedhena vai devāḥ paśūn udasedhan niṣedhena paryagṛhṇan
antarotsedhaniṣedhau yajñāyajñīyam
paśavo 'nnādyaṃ yajñāyajñīyaṃ paśūn eva tad annādyam utsedhaniṣedhābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāti
mādhyandine vai pavamāne devā yajñāyajñīyena yajñaṃ saṃsthāpya svargaṃ lokam ārohaṃs tad ya evaṃ veda mādhyandina evaitat pavamāne yajñāyajñīyena yajñaṃ saṃsthāpya svargaṃ lokam ārohati
atho parokṣam anuṣṭubhaṃ sampadyate 'har eṣā vai pratyakṣam anuṣṭup yad yajñāyajñīyaṃ tad yat tṛtīyasavane kuryuḥ pratyakṣam anuṣṭubham ṛccheyus tasmān mādhyandine kurvanti tena parokṣam anuṣṭubham upayanti
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
etad vai yajñasya śvastanaṃ yad gaurīvitam etadāyatano yajamāno yan madhyandino yad gaurīvitaṃ madhyandine bhavati śvastanam eva tad yajamāna ātman dhatte stomaḥ
